saṅkṣayam aham ca airāvatam nāgam āruhya anuvraje vrajam marut gaṇaiḥ mahā vegaiḥ nanda goṣṭha jighāṃsayā śrī śukaḥ uvāca ittham maghavatā ājñaptāḥ meghāḥ nirmukta bandhanāḥ nanda gokulam āsāraiḥ pīḍayām āsuḥ ojasā tīvraiḥ marut gaṇaiḥ nunnāḥ vavṛṣuḥ jala śarkarāḥ sthūṇā sthūlāḥ varṣa dhārāḥ muñcatsu abhreṣu abhīkṣṇaśas jala oghaiḥ plāvyamānā bhūḥ na adṛśyata nata unnatam ati āsāra ati vātena paśavaḥ jāta vepanāḥ gopāḥ gopyaḥ ca śīta ārtāḥ govindam śaraṇam yayuḥ śiraḥ sutān ca kāyena pracchādya āsāra pīḍitāḥ vepamānāḥ bhagavataḥ pāda mūlam upāyayuḥ kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa mahā bhāga tvad nātham gokulam prabho śilā varṣā ati vātena hanyamānam acetanam nirīkṣya bhagavant mene kupita indra kṛtam hariḥ apartu ati ulbaṇam varṣam ati vātam śilā mayam sva yāge vihate asmābhiḥ indraḥ nāśāya varṣati lokeśa māninām mauḍhyāt dhaniṣye śrī madam tamaḥ na hi sat bhāva yuktānām surāṇām īśa vismayaḥ mattaḥ asatām māna bhaṅgaḥ praśamāya upakalpate tasmāt mad śaraṇam goṣṭham mad nātham mad parigraham dadhāra līlayā viṣṇuḥ chatrākam iva bālakaḥ yathopajoṣam viśata giri gartam sa go dhanāḥ na trāsaḥ iha vaḥ kāryaḥ mad hasta adri nipātanāt vāta varṣa bhayena alam tat trāṇam vihitam hi vaḥ tathā nirviviśuḥ gartam kṛṣṇā āśvāsita mānasaḥ yathāvakāśam sa dhanāḥ sa vrajāḥ sa upajīvinaḥ kṣudh tṛṣ vyathām sukha apekṣām hitvā taiḥ vraja vāsibhiḥ vīkṣyamāṇaḥ dadhāra adrim sapta aham na acalat padāt kṛṣṇa yoga anubhāvam tam niśamya indraḥ ati vismitaḥ kham vyabhram udita ādityam vāta varṣam ca dāruṇam niryāta tyajata trāsam gopāḥ sa strī dhana arbhakāḥ upāratam vāta varṣam vyuda prāyāḥ ca nimnagāḥ śakaṭa ūḍhā upakaraṇam strī bāla sthavirāḥ śanais bhagavān api tam śailam sva sthāne pūrva vat prabhuḥ paśyatām sarva bhūtānām sthāpayām āsa līlayā yathā samīyuḥ parirambhaṇa ādibhiḥ dadhi akṣata adbhiḥ yuyujuḥ sat āśiṣaḥ yaśodā rohiṇī nandaḥ rāmaḥ ca balinām varaḥ kṛṣṇam āliṅgya yuyujuḥ āśiṣaḥ sneha kātarāḥ divi deva gaṇāḥ siddhāḥ sādhyāḥ gandharva cāraṇāḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ mumucuḥ tuṣṭāḥ puṣpa varṣāṇi pārthiva tathāvidhāni asya kṛtāni gopikāḥ gāyantyaḥ īyuḥ muditāḥ hṛdi spṛśaḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca evaṃvidhāni karmāṇi gopāḥ kṛṣṇasya vīkṣya te yaḥ sapta hāyanaḥ bālaḥ kareṇa ekena līlayā katham bibhrat giri varam puṣkaram gaja rāj iva tokena āmīlita akṣeṇa pūtanāyāḥ mahā ojasaḥ pītaḥ stanaḥ saha prāṇaiḥ kālena iva vayaḥ tanvaḥ hinvataḥ adhas śayānasya māsyasya caraṇau udak eka hāyanaḥ āsīnaḥ hriyamāṇaḥ vihāyasā vane sañcārayan vatsān sa rāmaḥ bālakaiḥ vṛtaḥ hantu kāmam bakam dorbhyām mukhataḥ arim apāṭayat vatseṣu vatsa rūpeṇa praviśantam jighāṃsayā hatvā rāsabha daiteyam tad bandhūn ca bala anvitaḥ pralambam ghātayitvā ugram balena bala śālinā amocayat vraja paśūn gopān ca araṇya vahneḥ damitvā vimadam hradāt dustyajaḥ ca anurāgaḥ asmin sarveṣām naḥ vrajaukasām kva sapta hāyanaḥ bālaḥ kva mahā adri vidhāraṇam tatas naḥ jāyate śaṅkā vraja nātha tava ātmaje śrī nandaḥ uvāca śrūyatām mama vacaḥ gopāḥ vyetu śaṅkā ca vaḥ arbhake varṇāḥ trayaḥ kila asya āsan gṛhṇataḥ anu yugam tanūḥ śuklaḥ raktaḥ tathā pītaḥ idānīm kṛṣṇa tām gataḥ vāsudevaḥ iti śrīmān abhijñāḥ sampracakṣate bahūni santi nāmāni rūpāṇi ca sutasya te guṇa karma anurūpāṇi tāni aham veda naḥ janāḥ eṣa vaḥ śreyaḥ ādhāsyat gopa gokula nandanaḥ purā anena vraja pate sādhavaḥ dasyu pīḍitāḥ arājake rakṣyamāṇāḥ jigyuḥ dasyūn samedhitāḥ ye etasmin mahā bhāge prītim kurvanti mānavāḥ na arayaḥ abhibhavanti etān viṣṇu pakṣān iva asurāḥ tasmāt nanda kumāraḥ ayam nārāyaṇa samaḥ guṇaiḥ śriyā kīrtyā anubhāvena tad karmasu na vismayaḥ iti addhā mām samādiśya garge ca sva gṛham gate manye nārāyaṇasya aṃśam kṛṣṇam akliṣṭa kāriṇam iti nanda vacaḥ śrutvā garga gītam tam vraja okasaḥ muditāḥ nandam ānarcuḥ kṛṣṇam ca gata vismayāḥ deve varṣati yajña viplava ruṣā vajra asma varṣa anilaiḥ sīdat pāla paśu striyam ātma śaraṇam dṛṣṭvā anukampī utsmayan utpāṭya eka kareṇa śailam abalaḥ līlā ucchilīndhram yathā śrī śukaḥ uvāca govardhane dhṛte śaile āsārāt rakṣite vraje go lokāt āvrajat kṛṣṇam surabhiḥ śakraḥ eva ca viviktaḥ upasaṅgamya vrīḍītaḥ kṛta helanaḥ pasparśa pādayoḥ enam kirīṭena arka varcasā dṛṣṭa śruta anubhāvaḥ asya kṛṣṇasya amita tejasaḥ naṣṭa tri loka īśa madaḥ idam āha kṛtāñjaliḥ māyā mayaḥ ayam guṇa sampravāhaḥ na vidyate te grahaṇa anubandhaḥ kutas nu tad hetavaḥ īśa tad kṛtāḥ lobha ādayaḥ ye abudha linga bhāvāḥ pitā guruḥ tvam jagatām adhīśaḥ duratyayaḥ kālaḥ upātta daṇḍaḥ hitāya ca icchā tanubhiḥ samīhase mānam vidhunvan jagat īśa māninām ye mad vidha ājñāḥ jagat īśa māninaḥ tvām vīkṣya kāle abhayam āśu tad madam hitvā ārya mārgam prabhajanti apasmayāḥ īhā khalānām api te anuśāsanam kṣantum prabho atha arhasi mūḍha cetasaḥ mā evam punar bhūt matiḥ īśa me asatī tava avatāraḥ ayam adhokṣaja iha bhuvaḥ bharāṇām uru bhāra janmanām camū patīnām abhavāya deva bhavāya yuṣmad caraṇa anuvartinām vāsudevāya kṛṣṇāya sātvatām pataye namaḥ mayā idam bhagavan goṣṭha nāśāya asāra vāyubhiḥ ceṣṭitam vihate yajñe māninā tīvra manyunā īśvaram gurum ātmānam tvām aham śaraṇam gataḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca evam saṅkīrtitaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ maghonā bhagavān amum śrī bhagavān uvāca mayā te akāri maghavan makha bhaṅgaḥ anugṛhṇatā mām aiśvarya śrī mada andhaḥ daṇḍa pāṇim na paśyati gamyatām śakra bhadram vaḥ kriyatām mama anuśāsanam sthīyatām sva adhikāreṣu yuktaiḥ vaḥ stambha varjitaiḥ atha āha surabhiḥ kṛṣṇam abhivandya manasvinī sva santānaiḥ upāmantrya gopa rūpiṇam īśvaram kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa mahā yogin viśvātman viśva sambhava bhavāya bhava go vipra devānām ye ca sādhavaḥ indram naḥ tvā abhiṣekṣyāmaḥ brahmaṇā coditāḥ vayam avatīrṇaḥ asi viśvātman bhūmeḥ bhāra apanuttaye śṛī śukaḥ uvāca evam kṛṣṇam upāmantrya surabhiḥ payasā ātmanaḥ jalaiḥ ākāśa gaṅgāyāḥ airāvata kara uddhṛtaiḥ indraḥ sura ṛṣibhiḥ sākam coditaḥ deva mātṛbhiḥ abhyasiñcata dāśārham govindaḥ iti ca abhyadhāt tatra āgatāḥ tumburu nārada ādayaḥ gandharva vidyādhara siddha cāraṇāḥ jaguḥ yaśaḥ loka mala apaham hareḥ sura aṅganāḥ sannanṛtuḥ mudā anvitāḥ tam tuṣṭuvuḥ deva nikāya ketavaḥ hi avākiran ca adbhuta puṣpa vṛṣṭibhiḥ lokāḥ parām nirvṛtim āpnuvan trayaḥ gāvaḥ tadā gām anayan payaḥ drutām nānā rasa oghāḥ saritaḥ vṛkṣāḥ āsan madhu sravāḥ a kṛṣṭa pacya oṣadhayaḥ girayaḥ abibhran ud maṇīn kṛṣṇe abhiṣikte etāni sarvāṇi kuru nandana nirvairāṇi abhavan tāta krūrāṇi api nisargataḥ śrī bādarāyaṇiḥ uvāca ekādaśyām nirāhāraḥ samabhyarcya janārdanam snātum nandaḥ tu kālindyām dvādaśyām jalam āviśat tam gṛhītvā anayat bhṛtyaḥ varuṇasya asuraḥ antikam avajñāya āsurīm velām praviṣṭam udakam niśi cukruśuḥ tam a paśyantaḥ kṛṣṇa rāma iti gopakāḥ bhagavān tat upaśrutya pitaram varuṇa āhṛtam prāptam vīkṣya hṛṣīkeśam loka pālaḥ saparyayā śrī varuṇaḥ uvāca na yatra śrūyate māyā loka sṛṣṭi vikalpanā a jānatā māmakena mūḍhena akārya vedinā ānītaḥ ayam tava pitā tat bhavān kṣantum arhati mama api anugraham kṛṣṇa kartum arhasi aśeṣa dṛś śrī śukaḥ uvāca evam prasāditaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ bhagavān īśvara īśvaraḥ ādāya āgāt sva pitaram bandhūnām ca avahat mudam nandaḥ tu atīndriyam dṛṣṭvā loka pāla mahodayam kṛṣṇe ca sannatim teṣām jñātibhyaḥ vismitaḥ abravīt api naḥ sva gatim sūkṣmām upādhāsyat adhīśvaraḥ iti svānām sa bhagavān vijñāya akhila dṛś svayam uccāvacāsu gatiṣu na veda svām gatim bhraman iti sañcintya bhagavant mahā kāruṇikaḥ hariḥ darśayām āsa lokam svam gopānām tamasaḥ param yat hi paśyanti munayaḥ guṇa apāye samāhitāḥ te tu brahma hradam nītāḥ magnāḥ kṛṣṇena ca uddhṛtāḥ dadṛśuḥ brahmaṇaḥ lokam yatra akrūraḥ adhyagāt purā nanda ādayaḥ tu tam dṛṣṭvā parama ānanda nivṛtāḥ kṛṣṇam ca tatra chandobhiḥ stūyamānam su vismitāḥ śrī bādarāyaṇiḥ uvāca bhagavān api tāḥ rātṛīḥ śārada utphulla mallikāḥ vīkṣya rantum manaḥ cakre yoga māyām upāśritaḥ tadā uḍurājaḥ kakubhaḥ karaiḥ mukham prācyā vilimpan aruṇena śantamaiḥ sa carṣaṇīnām udagāt śucaḥ mṛjan priyaḥ priyāyāḥ iva dīrgha darśanaḥ dṛṣṭvā kumudvantam akhaṇḍa maṇḍalam rama ānana ābham nava kuṅkuma aruṇam jagau kalam vāma dṛśām manoharam niśamya gītām tat anaṅga vardhanam vraja striyaḥ kṛṣṇa gṛhīta mānasāḥ ājagmuḥ anyonyam alakṣita udyamāḥ sa yatra kāntaḥ java lola kuṇḍalāḥ duhatyaḥ abhiyayuḥ kāścid doham hitvā samutsukāḥ payaḥ adhiśritya saṃyāvam an udvāsya aparāḥ yayuḥ pariveṣayantyaḥ tat hitvā pāyayantyaḥ śiśūn payaḥ śuśrūṣantyaḥ patīn kāścid aśnantyaḥ apāsya bhojanam limpantyaḥ pramṛjantyaḥ anyāḥ añjantyaḥ kāḥ ca locane vyatyasta vastra ābharaṇāḥ kāścid kṛṣṇa antikam yayuḥ tāḥ vāryamāṇāḥ patibhiḥ pitṛbhiḥ bhrātṛ bandhubhiḥ govinda apahṛta ātmānaḥ na nyavartanta mohitāḥ antar gṛha gatāḥ kāścid gopyaḥ alabdha vinirgamāḥ kṛṣṇam tad bhāvanā yuktāḥ dadhyuḥ mīlita locanāḥ duḥsaha preṣṭha viraha tīvra tāpa dhuta aśubhāḥ dhyāna prāpta acyuta āśleṣa nirvṛtyā kṣīṇa maṅgalāḥ tam eva paramātmānam jāra buddhyā api saṅgatāḥ jahuḥ guṇa mayam deham sadyas prakṣīṇa bandhanāḥ śrī parīkṣit uvāca kṛṣṇam viduḥ param kāntam na tu brahma tayā mune guṇa pravāha uparamaḥ tāsām guṇa dhiyām katham śrī śukaḥ uvāca dviṣan api hṛṣīkeśam kim uta adhokṣaja priyāḥ nṛṇām niḥśreyasa arthāya vyaktiḥ bhagavantaḥ nṛpa tāḥ dṛṣṭvā antikam āyātāḥ bhagavān vraja yoṣitaḥ avadat vadatām śreṣṭhaḥ vācaḥ peśaiḥ vimohayan śrī bhagavān uvāca svāgatam vaḥ mahā bhāgāḥ priyam kim karavāṇi vaḥ vrajasya anāmayam kaccit brūta āgamana kāraṇam rajanī eṣā ghora rūpā ghora sattva niṣevitā pratiyāta vrajam na iha stheyam strībhiḥ su madhyamāḥ mātaraḥ pitaraḥ putrāḥ bhrātaraḥ patayaḥ ca vaḥ dṛṣṭam vanam kusumitam rākeśa kara rañjitam tat yāta mā ciram goṣṭham śuśrūṣadhvam patīn satīḥ krandanti vatsāḥ bālāḥ ca tān pāyayata duhyata atha vā mad abhisnehāt bhavatyaḥ yantrita āśayāḥ āgatāḥ hi upapannam vaḥ prīyante mayi jantavaḥ bhartuḥ śuśrūṣaṇam strīṇām paraḥ dharmaḥ hi amāyayā tad bandhūnām ca kalyāṇaḥ prajānām ca an upoṣaṇam duḥśīlaḥ durbhagaḥ vṛddhaḥ jaḍaḥ rogī adhanaḥ api vā śravaṇāt darśanāt dhyānāt mayi bhāvaḥ anukīrtanāt na tathā sannikarṣeṇa pratiyāta tatas gṛhān śrī śukaḥ uvāca viṣaṇṇāḥ bhagna saṅkalpāḥ cintām āpuḥ duratyayām kṛtvā mukhāni ava śucaḥ śvasanena śuṣyat bimba adharāṇi caraṇena bhuvaḥ likhantyaḥ tasthuḥ mṛjantyaḥ uru duḥkha bharāḥ sma tūṣṇīm preṣṭham priyetaram iva pratibhāṣamāṇam kṛṣṇam tad artha vinivartita sarva kāmāḥ śrī gopyaḥ ūcuḥ mā evam vibho arhati bhavān gaditum nṛ śaṃsam preṣṭhaḥ bhavān tanu bhṛtām kila bandhuḥ ātmā āśām dhṛtām tvayi cirāt aravinda netra cittam sukhena bhavatā apahṛtam gṛheṣu pādau padam na calataḥ tava pāda mūlāt yāmaḥ katham vrajam atho karavāma kim vā siñca aṅga naḥ tvad adhara amṛta pūrakeṇa hāsa avaloka kala gīta ja hṛd śaya agnim dhyānena yāma padayoḥ padavīm sakhe te yarhi ambuja akṣa tava pāda talam ramāyā asprākṣma tad prabhṛti na anya samakṣam añjas sthātum tvayā abhiramitāḥ bata pārayāmaḥ labdhvā api vakṣasi padam kila bhṛtya juṣṭam yasyāḥ sva vīkṣaṇe uta anya sura prayāsaḥ tat naḥ prasīda vṛjina ardana te anghri mūlam prāptāḥ visṛjya vasatīḥ tvad upāsana āśāḥ tapta ātmanām puruṣa bhūṣaṇa dehi dāsyam vīkṣya alaka āvṛta mukham tava kuṇdala śrī vakṣaḥ śriyā eka ramaṇam ca bhavāma dāsyaḥ kā strī aṅga te kala pada āyata veṇu gīta tapta staneṣu ca śiraḥsu ca kiṅkarīṇām śrī śukaḥ uvāca iti viklavitam tāsām śrutvā yogeśvara īśvaraḥ prahasya sa dayam gopīḥ ātma ārāmaḥ api arīramat tābhiḥ sametābhiḥ udāra ceṣṭitaḥ priya īkṣaṇa utphulla mukhībhiḥ acyutaḥ udāra hāsa dvija kunda dīdhatiḥ vyarocata eṇa aṅkaḥ iva uḍubhiḥ vṛtaḥ upagīyamānaḥ udgāyan vanitā śata yūthapaḥ mālām bibhrat vaijayantīm vyacarat maṇḍayan vanam nadyāḥ pulinam āviśya gopībhiḥ hima vālukam juṣṭam tat tarala ānandi kumuda āmoda vāyunā evam bhagavataḥ kṛṣṇāt labdha mānāḥ mahātmanaḥ ātmānam menire strīṇām māninyaḥ hi adhikam bhuvi tāsām tad saubhaga madam vīkṣya mānam ca keśavaḥ praśamāya prasādāya tatra eva antaradhīyata śrī śukaḥ uvāca atapyan tam a cakṣāṇāḥ kariṇyaḥ iva yūthapam ākṣipta cittāḥ pramadāḥ ramā pateḥ tāḥ tāḥ viceṣṭāḥ jagṛhuḥ tad ātmakāḥ gati smita prekṣaṇa bhāṣaṇa ādiṣu priyāḥ priyasya pratirūḍha mūrtayaḥ asau aham tu iti abalāḥ tad ātmakāḥ nyavediṣuḥ kṛṣṇa vihāra vibhramāḥ papracchuḥ ākāśa vat antaram bahis bhūteṣu santam puruṣam vanaspatīn dṛṣṭaḥ vaḥ kaccit aśvattha plakṣa nyagrodha naḥ manaḥ nanda sūnuḥ gataḥ hṛtvā prema hāsa avalokanaiḥ kaccit kurabaka aśoka nāga punnāga campakāḥ rāma anujaḥ māninīnām itas darpa hara smitaḥ prītim vaḥ janayan yātaḥ kara sparśena mādhavaḥ ye anye para artha bhavakāḥ yamunā upakūlāḥ śaṃsantu kṛṣṇa padavīm rahita ātmanām naḥ kim te kṛtam kṣiti tapaḥ bata keśava aṅghri āho varāha vapuṣaḥ parirambhaṇena tanvan dṛśām sakhi su nirvṛtim acyutaḥ vaḥ kānta aṅga saṅga kuca kuṅkuma rañjitāyāḥ bāhum priya aṃsaḥ upadhāya gṛhīta padmaḥ anvīyamānaḥ iha vaḥ taravaḥ praṇāmam pṛcchata imāḥ latāḥ bāhūn api āśliṣṭāḥ vanaspateḥ nūnam tad karaja spṛṣṭāḥ bibhrati utpulakāni aho iti unmatta vacaḥ gopyaḥ kṛṣṇa anveṣaṇa kātarāḥ līlāḥ bhagavataḥ tāḥ tāḥ hi anucakruḥ tad ātmikāḥ kasyācid pūtanāyantyāḥ kṛṣṇāyantī apibat stanam tokayitvā rudatī anyā padā ahan śakaṭāyatīm riṅgayām āsa kā api aṅghrī karṣantī ghoṣa niḥsvanaiḥ kṛṣṇa rāmāyite dve tu gopāyantyaḥ ca kāścana vatsāyatīm hanti ca anyā tatra ekā tu bakāyatīm āhūya dūra gāḥ yadvat kṛṣṇaḥ tam anuvartatīm veṇum kvaṇantīm krīḍantīm anyāḥ śaṃsanti sādhu iti kṛṣṇaḥ aham paśyata gatim lalitām iti tad manāḥ mā bhaiṣṭa vāta varṣābhyām tat trāṇam vihitam maya āruhya ekā padā ākramya śirasi āha aparām nṛpa duṣṭa ahe gaccha jātaḥ aham khalānām nanu daṇḍa kṛt tatra ekā uvāca he gopāḥ dāva agnim paśyata ulbaṇam cakṣūṃṣi āśu apidadhvam vaḥ vidhāsye kṣemam añjasā baddhā anyayā srajā kācid tanvī tatra ulūkhale badhnāmi bhāṇḍa bhettāram haiyaṅgava muṣam tu iti bhītā su dṛś pidhāya āsyam bheje bhīti viḍambanam evam kṛṣṇam pṛcchamānāḥ vrṇdāvana latāḥ tarūn lakṣyante hi dhvaja ambhoja vajra aṅkuśa yava ādibhiḥ vadhvāḥ padaiḥ su pṛktāni vilokya ārtāḥ samabruvan kasyāḥ padāni ca etāni yātāyāḥ nanda sūnunā aṃsa nyasta prakoṣṭhāyāḥ kareṇoḥ kariṇā yathā anayā ārādhitaḥ nūnam bhagavant hariḥ īśvaraḥ dhanyāḥ aho amī ālayaḥ govinda aṅghri abja reṇavaḥ tasyāḥ amūni naḥ kṣobham kurvanti uccais padāni yat na lakṣyante padāni atra tasyāḥ nūnam tṛṇa aṅkuraiḥ khidyat sujāta aṅghri talām unninye preyasīm priyaḥ gopyaḥ paśyata kṛṣṇasya bhāra ākrāntasya kāminaḥ atra avaropitā kāntā puṣpa hetoḥ mahātmanā atra prasūna avacayaḥ priya arthe preyasā kṛtaḥ keśa prasādhanam tu atra kāminyāḥ kāminā kṛtam tāni cūḍayatā kāntām upaviṣṭam iha dhruvam reme tayā ca ātma rataḥ ātma ārāmaḥ api akhaṇḍitaḥ kāminām darśayan dainyam strīṇām ca eva durātmatām yām gopīm anayat kṛṣṇaḥ vihāya anyāḥ striyaḥ vane sā ca mene tadā ātmānam variṣṭham sarva yoṣitām hitvā gopīḥ kāma yānāḥ mām asau bhajate priyaḥ tatas gatvā vana uddeśam dṛptā keśavam abravīt na pāraye aham calitum naya mām yatra te manaḥ tatas ca antardadhe kṛṣṇaḥ sā vadhūḥ anvatapyata hā nātha ramaṇa preṣṭha kva asi kva asi mahā bhuja dāsyāḥ te kṛpaṇāyāḥ me sakhe darśaya sannidhim śrī śukaḥ uvāca dadṛśuḥ priya viśleṣāt mohitām duḥkhitām sakhīm tayā kathitam ākarṇya māna prāptim ca mādhavāt avamānam ca daurātmyāt vismayam paramam yayuḥ tamaḥ praviṣṭam ālakṣya tatas nivavṛtuḥ striyaḥ tad manaskāḥ tad alāpāḥ tad viceṣṭāḥ tad ātmikāḥ tad guṇān eva gāyantyaḥ na ātma gārāṇi sasmaruḥ punar pulinam āgatya kālindyāḥ kṛṣṇa bhāvanāḥ samavetāḥ jaguḥ kṛṣṇam tad āgamana kāṅkṣitāḥ gopyaḥ ūcuḥ dayita dṛśyatām dikṣu tāvakāḥ tvayi dhṛta asavaḥ tvām vicinvate śarad udāśaye sādhu jāta sat sarasija udara śrī muṣā dṛśā viṣa jala apyayāt vyāla rākṣasāt varṣa mārutāt vaidyuta analāt vṛṣa maya ātmajāt viśvatas bhayāt ṛṣabha te vayam rakṣitāḥ muhur viracita abhayam vṛṣṇi dhūrya te caraṇam īyuṣām saṃsṛteḥ bhayāt kara saroruham kānta kāma dam śirasi dhehi naḥ śrī kara graham praṇata dehinām pāpa karṣaṇam tṛṇa cara anugam śrī niketanam phaṇi phaṇa arpitam te pada ambujam kṛṇu kuceṣu naḥ kṛndhi hṛd śayam madhurayā girā valgu vākyayā budha manojñayā puṣkarekṣaṇa vidhi karīḥ imāḥ vīra muhyatīḥ adhara sīdhunā āpyāyayasva naḥ tava kathā amṛtam tapta jīvanam kavibhiḥ īḍitam kalmaṣa apaham śravaṇa maṅgalam śrīmat ātatam bhuvi gṛṇanti ye bhūri dāḥ janāḥ prahasitam priya prema vīkṣaṇam viharaṇam ca te dhyāna maṅgalam rahasi saṃvidaḥ yāḥ hṛdi spṛśaḥ kuhaka naḥ manaḥ kṣobhayanti hi śila tṛṇa aṅkuraiḥ sīdati iti naḥ kalila tām manaḥ kānta gacchati praṇata kāma dam padmaja arcitam dharaṇī maṇḍanam dhyeyam āpadi caraṇa paṅkajam śantamam ca te ramaṇa naḥ staneṣu arpaya adhi han surata vardhanam śoka nāśanam svarita veṇunā suṣṭhu cumbitam itara rāga vismāraṇam nṛṇām vitara vīra naḥ te adhara amṛtam aṭati yat bhavān ahni kānanam truṭi yugāyate tvām apaśyatām kuṭila kuntalam śrī mukham ca te jaḍaḥ udīkṣatām pakṣma kṛt dṛśām pati suta anvaya bhrātṛ bāndhavān ati vilaṅghya te anti acyuta āgatāḥ rahasi saṃvidam hṛd śaya udayam prahasita ānanam prema vīkṣaṇam bṛhat uraḥ śriyaḥ vīkṣya dhāma te muhur ati spṛhā muhyate manaḥ tyaja manāk ca naḥ tvad spṛhā ātmanām sva jana hṛd rujām yat niṣūdanam yat te sujāta caraṇa amburuham staneṣu bhītāḥ śanais priya dadhīmahi karkaśeṣu kūrpa ādibhiḥ bhramati dhīḥ bhavat āyuṣām naḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca ruruduḥ su svaram rājan kṛṣṇa darśana lālasāḥ tāsām āvirabhūt śauriḥ smayamāna mukha ambujaḥ pīta ambara dharaḥ sragvī sākṣāt manmatha manmathaḥ tam vilokya āgatam preṣṭham prīti utphulla dṛśaḥ abalāḥ kācid kara ambujam śaureḥ jagṛhe añjalinā mudā kācid dadhāra tad bāhum aṃse candana bhūṣitam kācid añjalinā agṛhṇāt tanvī tāmbūla carvitam ghnantī iva aikṣat kaṭa ākṣepaiḥ sandaṣṭa daśana chadā aparā animiṣat dṛgbhyām juṣāṇā tad mukha ambujam āpītam api na atṛpyat santaḥ tad caraṇam yathā tam kācid netra randhreṇa hṛdi kṛtvā nimīlya ca pulaka aṅgā upaguhya āste yogī iva ānanda samplutā sarvāḥ tāḥ keśava āloka parama utsava nirvṛtāḥ jahuḥ viraha jam tāpam prājñam prāpya yathā janāḥ tābhiḥ vidhūta śokābhiḥ bhagavant acyutaḥ vṛtaḥ vyarocata adhikam tāta puruṣaḥ śaktibhiḥ yathā tāḥ samādāya kālindyāḥ nirviśya pulinam vibhuḥ śarad candra aṃśu sandoha dhvasta doṣa tamaḥ śivam kṛṣṇāyāḥ hasta taralā cita komala vālukam tad darśana āhlāda vidhūta hṛd rujaḥ manoratha antam śrutayaḥ yathā yayuḥ svaiḥ uttarīyaiḥ kuca kuṅkuma aṅkitaiḥ acīkḷpan āsanam ātma bandhave tatra upaviṣṭaḥ bhagavān saḥ īśvaraḥ yogeśvara antar hṛdi kalpita āsanaḥ sabhājayitvā tam anaṅga dīpanam sa hāsa līlā īkṣaṇa vibhrama bhruvā saṃsparśanena aṅka kṛta aṅghri hastayoḥ saṃstutya īṣat kupitāḥ babhāṣire śrī gopyaḥ ūcuḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca na tatra sauhṛdam dharmaḥ svārtha artham tat hi na anyathā ātma ārāmāḥ hi āpta kāmāḥ akṛta jñāḥ guru druhaḥ na aham tu sakhyaḥ bhajataḥ api jantūn bhajāmi amīṣām anuvṛtti vṛttaye mayā aparokṣam bhajatā tirohitam mā asūyitum mā arhatha tat priyam priyāḥ na pāraye aham niravadya saṃyujām sva sādhu kṛtyam vibudha āyuṣā api vaḥ yāḥ mā ābhajan durjara geha śṛṅkhalāḥ saṃvṛścya tat vaḥ pratiyātu sādhunā śrī śukaḥ uvāca ittham bhagavataḥ gopyaḥ śrutvā vācaḥ su peśalāḥ jahuḥ viraha jam tāpam tad aṅga upacita āśiṣaḥ tatra ārabhata govindaḥ rāsa krīḍām anuvrataiḥ rāsa utsavaḥ sampravṛttaḥ gopī maṇḍala maṇḍitaḥ yogeśvareṇa kṛṣṇena tāsām madhye dvayoḥ dvayoḥ praviṣṭena gṛhītānām kaṇṭhe sva nikaṭam striyaḥ divaukasām sa dārāṇām autsukya apahṛta ātmanām tatas dundubhayaḥ neduḥ nipetuḥ puṣpa vṛṣṭayaḥ valayānām nūpurāṇām kiṅkiṇīnām ca yoṣitām sa priyāṇām abhūt śabdaḥ tumulaḥ rāsa maṇḍale tatra atiśuśubhe tābhiḥ bhagavān devakī sutaḥ madhye maṇīnām haimānām mahā marakataḥ yathā bhajyan madhyaiḥ cala kuca paṭaiḥ kuṇḍalaiḥ gaṇḍa lolaiḥ uccais jaguḥ nṛtyamānāḥ rakta kaṇṭhyaḥ rati priyāḥ kṛṣṇa abhimarśa muditāḥ yad gītena idam āvṛtam kācid samam mukundena svara jātīḥ a miśritāḥ unninye pūjitā tena prīyatā sādhu sādhu iti kācid rāsa pariśrāntā pārśva sthasya gadā bhṛtaḥ tatra eka aṃsa gatam bāhum kṛṣṇasya utpala saurabham candana āliptam āghrāya hṛṣṭa romā cucumba ha kasyāścid nāṭya vikṣipta kuṇḍala tviṣa maṇḍitam gaṇḍam gaṇḍe sandadhatyāḥ prādāt tāmbūla carvitam nṛtyatī gāyatī kācid kūjat nūpura mekhalā pārśva stha acyuta hasta abjam śrāntā adhāt stanayoḥ śivam gṛhīta kaṇṭhyaḥ tad dorbhyām gāyantyaḥ tam vijahrire gopyaḥ samam bhagavatā nanṛtuḥ sva keśa evam pariṣvaṅga kara abhimarśa snigdha īkṣaṇa uddāma vilāsa hāsaiḥ tad aṅga saṅga pramudā ākula indriyāḥ keśān dukūlam kuca paṭṭikām vā na añjas prativyoḍhum alam vraja striyaḥ visrasta mālā ābharaṇāḥ kuru udvaha kṛṣṇa vikrīḍitam vīkṣya mumuhuḥ khecara striyaḥ kāma arditāḥ śaśāṅkaḥ ca sa gaṇaḥ vismitaḥ abhavat kṛtvā tāvantam ātmānam yāvatīḥ gopa yoṣitaḥ reme sa bhagavant tābhiḥ ātma ārāmaḥ api līlayā tāsām rati vihāreṇa śrāntānām vadanāni saḥ prāmṛjat karuṇaḥ premṇā śantamena aṅga pāṇinā gaṇḍa śriyā sudhita hāsa nirīkṣaṇena mānam dadhatyaḥ ṛṣabhasya jaguḥ kṛtāni puṇyāni tad kara ruha sparśa pramodāḥ ghṛṣṭa srajaḥ sa kuca kuṅkuma rañjitāyāḥ śrāntaḥ gajībhiḥ ibha rāj iva bhinna setuḥ tatas ca kṛṣṇa upavane prasūna gandha anila juṣṭa diś taṭe cacāra bhṛṅga pramadā gaṇa āvṛtaḥ yathā mada cyut dviradaḥ kareṇubhiḥ evam śaśāṅka aṃśu virājitāḥ niśāḥ sa satya kāmaḥ anurata abalā gaṇaḥ siṣeva ātmani avaruddha saurataḥ sarvāḥ śarad kāvya kathā rasa āśrayāḥ śrī parīkṣit uvāca avatīrṇaḥ hi bhagavān aṃśena jagat īśvaraḥ sa katham dharma setūnām vaktā kartā abhirakṣitā śrī śukaḥ uvāca dharma vyatikramaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ īśvarāṇām ca sāhasam tejīyasām na doṣāya vahneḥ sarva bhujaḥ yathā na etat samācaret jātu manasā api hi anīśvaraḥ vinaśyati ācaran mauḍhyāt yathā arudraḥ abdhi jam viṣam īśvarāṇām vacaḥ satyam tathā eva ācaritam kvacid teṣām yat sva vacaḥ yuktam buddhimān tat samācaret viparyayeṇa vā anarthaḥ nirahaṅkāriṇām prabho īśituḥ ca īśitavyānām kuśala akuśala anvayaḥ yad pāda paṅkaja parāga niṣeva tṛptā gopīnām tad patīnām ca sarveṣām eva dehinām anugrahāya bhaktānām mānuṣam deham āsthitaḥ bhajate tādṛśīḥ krīḍa yāḥ śrutvā tad paraḥ bhavet na asūyan khalu kṛṣṇāya mohitāḥ tasya māyayā manyamānāḥ sva pārśva sthān svān svān dārān vrajaukasaḥ brahma rātre upāvṛtte vāsudeva anumoditāḥ vikrīḍitam vraja vadhūbhiḥ idam ca viṣṇoḥ śraddhā anvitaḥ anuśṛṇuyāt atha varṇayet yaḥ hṛd rogam āśu apahinoti acireṇa dhīraḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca ekadā deva yātrāyām gopālāḥ jāta kautukāḥ tatra snātvā sarasvatyām devam paśu patim vibhum ānarcuḥ arhaṇaiḥ bhaktyā devīm ca nṛpate ambikām gāvaḥ hiraṇyam vāsāṃsi madhu madhu annam ādṛtāḥ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ daduḥ sarve devaḥ naḥ prīyatām iti ūṣuḥ sarasvatī tīre jalam prāśya yata vratāḥ rajanīm tām mahā bhāgāḥ nanda sunandaka ādayaḥ yadṛcchayā āgataḥ nandam śayānam ura gaḥ agrasīt sa cukrośa ahinā grastaḥ kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa mahān ayam tasya ca ākranditam śrutvā gopālāḥ sahasā utthitāḥ grastam ca dṛṣṭvā vibhrāntāḥ sarpam vivyadhuḥ ulmukaiḥ alātaiḥ dahyamānaḥ api na amuñcat tam uraṅgamaḥ tam aspṛśat padā abhyetya bhagavān sātvatām patiḥ sa vai bhagavataḥ śrīmat pāda sparśa hata aśubhaḥ tam apṛcchat dhṛṣīkeśaḥ praṇatam samavasthitam dīpyamānena vapuṣā puruṣam hema mālinam katham jugupsitām etām gatim vā prāpitaḥ avaśaḥ aham vidyādharaḥ kaścid sudarśanaḥ iti śrutaḥ śriyā sva rūpa sampattyā vimānena ācaran diśaḥ ṛṣīn virūpa aṅgirasaḥ prāhasam rūpa darpitaḥ taiḥ imām prāpitaḥ yonim pralabdhaiḥ svena pāpmanā śāpaḥ me anugrahāya eva kṛtaḥ taiḥ karuṇa ātmabhiḥ yat aham loka guruṇā padā spṛṣṭaḥ hata aśubhaḥ tam tvā aham bhava bhītānām prapannānām bhaya apaham āpṛcche śāpa nirmuktaḥ pāda sparśāt amīva han anujānīhi mām deva sarva loka īśvara īśvara yad nāma gṛhṇan akhilān śrotṝn ātmānam eva ca sadyas punāti kim bhūyas tasya spṛṣṭaḥ padā hi te iti anujñāpya dāśārham parikramya abhivandya ca sudarśanaḥ divam yātaḥ kṛcchrāt nandaḥ ca mocitaḥ niśāmya kṛṣṇasya tat ātma vaibhavam nṛpāyayuḥ tat kathayantaḥ ādṛtāḥ niśā mukham mānayantau udita uḍupa tārakam jagatuḥ sarva bhūtānām manaḥ śravaṇa maṅgalam gopyaḥ tad gītam ākarṇya mūrcchitāḥ na avidat nṛpa sraṃsat dukūlam ātmānam srasta keśa srajam tatas evam vikrīḍatoḥ svairam gāyatoḥ sampramatta vat śaṅkhacūḍaḥ iti khyātaḥ dhanada anucaraḥ abhyagāt tayoḥ nirīkṣatoḥ rājan tad nātham pramadā janam krośantam kālayām āsa diśi udīcyām aśaṅkitaḥ krośantam kṛṣṇa rāma iti vilokya sva parigraham yathā gāḥ dasyunā grastāḥ bhrātarau anvadhāvatām mā bhaiṣṭa iti abhaya ārāvau śāla hastau tarasvinau sa vīkṣya tau anuprāptau kāla mṛtyū iva udvijan viṣṛjya strī janam mūḍhaḥ prādravat jīvita icchayā jahāra muṣṭinā eva aṅga saha cūḍa maṇim vibhuḥ śaṅkhacūḍam nihatya evam maṇim ādāya bhāsvaram agrajāyā adadāt prītyā paśyantīnām ca yoṣitām śrī śukaḥ uvāca gopyaḥ kṛṣṇe vanam yāte tam anudruta cetasaḥ kṛṣṇa līlāḥ pragāyantyaḥ ninyuḥ duḥkhena vāsarān śrī gopyaḥ ūcuḥ komala aṅgulibhiḥ āśrita mārgam gopyaḥ īrayati yatra mukundaḥ kāma mārgaṇa samarpita cittāḥ kaśmalam yayuḥ apasmṛta nīvyaḥ hanta citram abalāḥ śṛṇuta idam hāra hāse urasi sthira vidyut nanda sūnuḥ ayam ārta janānām narma daḥ yarhi kūjita veṇuḥ vṛndaśas vraja vṛṣāḥ mṛga gāvaḥ veṇu vādya hṛta cetasaḥ ārāt danta daṣṭa kavalāḥ dhṛta karṇāḥ nidritāḥ likhita citram iva āsan spṛhayatīḥ vayam iva abahu puṇyāḥ prema vepita bhujāḥ stimita apaḥ anucaraiḥ samanuvarṇita vīryaḥ ādi pūruṣaḥ iva acala bhūtiḥ vana caraḥ giri taṭeṣu carantīḥ veṇunā āhvayati gāḥ sa yadā hi vana latāḥ taravaḥ ātmani viṣṇum vyañjayantyaḥ iva puṣpa phala āḍhyāḥ praṇata bhāra viṭapāḥ madhu dhārāḥ prema hṛṣṭa tanavaḥ vavṛṣuḥ sma ali kulaiḥ alaghu gītām abhīṣṭam ādriyan yarhi sandhita veṇuḥ sarasi sārasa haṃsa vihaṅgāḥ cāru gītā hṛta cetasaḥ etya harim upāsata te yata cittāḥ hanta mīlita dṛśaḥ dhṛta maunāḥ saha balaḥ sraj avataṃsa vilāsaḥ sānuṣu kṣiti bhṛtaḥ vraja devyaḥ vividha gopa caraṇeṣu vidagdhaḥ veṇu vādyaḥ urudhā nija śikṣāḥ savanaśas tat upadhārya sura īśāḥ śakra śarva parameṣṭhi purogāḥ kavayaḥ ānata kandhara cittāḥ kaśmalam yayuḥ aniścita tattvāḥ vrajati tena vayam sa vilāsa vīkṣaṇa arpita manobhava vegāḥ kuja gatim gamitāḥ na vidāmaḥ kaśmalena kavaram vasanam vā maṇi dharaḥ kvacid āgaṇayan gāḥ mālayā dayita gandha tulasyāḥ kvaṇita veṇu rava vañcita cittāḥ kṛṣṇam anvasata kṛṣṇa gṛhiṇyaḥ guṇa gaṇa arṇam anugatya hariṇyaḥ gopikāḥ iva vimukta gṛha āśāḥ utsavam śrama rucā api dṛśīnām unnayan khura rajaḥ churita sraj ditsayā eti suhṛd āsiṣaḥ eṣa devakī jaṭhara bhūḥ uḍu rājaḥ mada vighūrṇita locanaḥ īṣat māna daḥ sva suhṛdām vana mālī badara pāṇḍu vadanaḥ mṛdu gaṇḍam maṇḍayan kanaka kuṇḍala lakṣmyā śrī śukaḥ uvāca evam vraja striyaḥ rājan kṛṣṇa līlā anugāyatīḥ śrī bādarāyaṇiḥ uvāca atha tarhi āgataḥ goṣṭham ariṣṭaḥ vṛṣabha asuraḥ mahīm mahā kakud kāyaḥ kampayan khura vikṣatām rambhamāṇaḥ kharataram padā ca vilikhan mahīm udyamya puccham vaprāṇi viṣāṇa agreṇa ca uddharan yasya nirhrāditena aṅga niṣṭhureṇa gavām nṛṇām tam tīkṣṇa śṛṅgam udvīkṣya gopyaḥ gopāḥ ca tatrasuḥ kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa iti te sarve govindam śaraṇam yayuḥ mā bhaiṣṭa iti girā āśvāsya vṛṣa asuram upāhvayat mayi śāstari duṣṭānām tvad vidhānām durātmanām iti āsphotya acyutaḥ ariṣṭam tala śabdena kopayan saḥ api evam kopitaḥ ariṣṭaḥ khureṇa avanim ullikhan agra nyasta viṣāṇa agraḥ stabdha asṛj locanaḥ acyutam kaṭākṣipya adravat tūrṇam indra muktaḥ aśaniḥ yathā gṛhītvā śṛṅgayoḥ tam vai aṣṭādaśa padāni saḥ āpatat svinna sarva aṅgaḥ niḥśvasan krodha mūrcchitaḥ tam āpatantam sa nigṛhya śṛṅgayoḥ padā samākramya nipātya bhū tale niṣpīḍayām āsa yathā ārdram ambaram kṛtvā viṣāṇena jaghāna saḥ apatat asṛj vaman mūtra śakṛt samutsṛjan kṣipan ca pādān anavasthita īkṣaṇaḥ jagāma kṛcchram nirṛteḥ atha kṣayam puṣpaiḥ kirantaḥ harim īḍire surāḥ evam kukudminam hatvā stūyamānaḥ dvijātibhiḥ viveśa goṣṭham sa balaḥ gopīnām nayana utsavaḥ ariṣṭe nihate daitye kṛṣṇena adbhuta karmaṇā kaṃsāya atha āha bhagavān nāradaḥ deva darśanaḥ yaśodāyāḥ sutām kanyām devakyāḥ kṛṣṇam eva ca rāmam ca rohiṇī putram vasudevena bibhyatā nyastau sva mitre nande vai yābhyām te puruṣāḥ hatāḥ niśātam asim ādatta vasudeva jighāṃsayā jñātvā loha mayaiḥ pāśaiḥ babandha saha bhāryayā pratiyāte tu deva ṛṣau kaṃse ābhāṣya keśinam preṣayām āsa hanyetām bhavatā rāma keśavau tatas muṣṭika cāṇūra śala tośalaka ādikān amātyān hastipān ca eva samāhūya āha bhoja rāj bho bho niśamyatām etat vīra cāṇūra muṣṭikau rāma kṛṣṇau tatas mahyam mṛtyuḥ kila nidarśitaḥ mañcāḥ kriyantām vividhāḥ malla raṅga pariśritāḥ mahāmātra tvayā bhadra raṅga dvāri upanīyatām ārabhyatām dhanuḥ yāgaḥ caturdaśyām yathāvidhi viśasantu paśūn medhyān bhūta rājāya mīḍhuṣe iti ājñāpya artha tantra jñaḥ āhūya yadu puṅgavam gṛhītvā pāṇinā pāṇim tatas akrūram uvāca ha bho bho dāna pate mahyam kriyatām maitram ādṛtaḥ āsāte tau iha anena rathena ānaya mā ciram nisṛṣṭaḥ kila me mṛtyuḥ devaiḥ vaikuṇṭha saṃśrayaiḥ tau ānaya samam gopaiḥ nanda ādyaiḥ sa abhyupāyanaiḥ ghātayiṣye iha ānītau kāla kalpena hastinā tad bandhūn nihaniṣyāmi vṛṣṇi bhoja daśārhakān ugrasenam ca pitaram sthaviram rājya kāmukam tatas ca eṣā mahī mitra bhavitrī naṣṭa kaṇṭakā śambaraḥ narakaḥ bāṇaḥ mayi eva kṛta sauhṛdāḥ taiḥ aham sura pakṣīyān hatvā bhokṣye mahīm nṛpān etat jñātvā ānaya kṣipram rāma kṛṣṇau iha arbhakau dhanuḥ makha nirīkṣā artham draṣṭum yadu pura śriyam śrī akrūraḥ uvāca yujyate harṣa śokābhyām tathā api ājñām karomi te śrī śukaḥ uvāca evam ādiśya ca akrūram mantriṇaḥ ca viṣṛjya saḥ praviveśa gṛham kaṃsaḥ tathā akrūraḥ svam ālayam śrī śukaḥ uvāca keśī tu kaṃsa prahitaḥ khuraiḥ mahīm saṭā avadhūta abhra vimāna saṅkulam kurvan nabhaḥ heṣita bhīṣita akhilaḥ tam trāsayantam bhagavān sva gokulam tad ha iṣitaiḥ vāla vighūrṇita ambudam ātmānam ājau mṛgayantam agra nīḥ sa tam niśāmya abhimukhaḥ makhena kham durāsadaḥ caṇḍa javaḥ duratyayaḥ tat vañcayitvā tam adhokṣajaḥ ruṣā pragṛhya dorbhyām parividhya pādayoḥ sa avajñam utsṛjya dhanuḥ śata antare yathā uragam tārkṣya sutaḥ vyavasthitaḥ saḥ labdha saṃjñaḥ punar utthitaḥ ruṣā vyādāya keśī tarasā apatat harim yathā āmayaḥ saṃvavṛdhe upekṣitaḥ samedhamānena sa kṛṣṇa bāhunā niruddha vāyuḥ caraṇān ca vikṣipan prasvinna gātraḥ parivṛtta locanaḥ papāta laṇḍam visṛjan kṣitau vyasuḥ tad dehāt karkaṭikā phala upamāt vyasoḥ apākṛṣya bhujam mahā bhujaḥ avismitaḥ ayatna hata arikaḥ suraiḥ prasūna varṣaiḥ varṣadbhiḥ īḍitaḥ kṛṣṇam akliṣṭa karmāṇam rahasi etat abhāṣata kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa aprameya ātman yogeśa jagat īśvara vāsudeva akhila āvāsa sātvatām pravara prabho tvam ātmā sarva bhūtānām ekaḥ jyotiḥ iva edhasām gūḍhaḥ guhā śayaḥ sākṣī mahā puruṣaḥ īśvaraḥ ātmanā ātma āśrayaḥ pūrvam māyayā sasṛje guṇān taiḥ idam satya saṅkalpaḥ sṛjasi atsi avasi īśvaraḥ sa tvam bhūdhara bhūtānām daitya pramatha rakṣasām avatīrṇaḥ vināśāya sādhunām rakṣaṇāya ca diṣṭyā te nihataḥ daityaḥ līlayā ayam haya ākṛtiḥ cāṇūram muṣṭikam ca eva mallān anyān ca hastinam tasya anu śaṅkha yavana murāṇām narakasya ca udvāham vīra kanyānām vīrya śulka ādi lakṣaṇam nṛgasya mokṣaṇam śāpāt dvārakāyām jagat pate syamantakasya ca maṇeḥ ādānam saha bhāryayā mṛta putra pradānam ca brāhmaṇasya sva dhāmataḥ pauṇḍrakasya vadham paścāt kāśi puryāḥ ca dīpanam yāni ca anyāni vīryāṇi dvārakām āvasan bhavān atha te kāla rūpasya kṣapayiṣṇoḥ amuṣya vai akṣauhiṇīnām nidhanam drakṣyāmi arjuna sāratheḥ viśuddha vijñāna ghanam sva saṃsthayā sva tejasā nitya nivṛtta māyā tvām īśvaram svāśrayam ātma māyayā vinirmita aśeṣa viśeṣa kalpanam krīḍā artham adya ātta manuṣya vigraham nataḥ asmi dhuryam yadu vṛṣṇi sātvantām śrī śukaḥ uvāca evam yadu patim kṛṣṇam bhāgavata pravaraḥ muniḥ paśūn apālayat pālaiḥ prītaiḥ vraja sukha āvahaḥ ekadā te paśūn pālāḥ cārayantaḥ adri sānuṣu cakruḥ nilāyana krīḍāḥ cora pāla apadeśāt tatra āsan katicid corāḥ pālāḥ ca katicid nṛpa meṣāyitāḥ ca tatra eke vijahruḥ akutobhayāḥ meṣāyitān apovāha prāyas corāyitaḥ bahūn giri daryām vinikṣipya nītam nītam mahā asuraḥ śilayā pidadhe dvāram catur pañca avaśeṣitāḥ tasya tat karma vijñāya kṛṣṇaḥ śaraṇa daḥ satām gopān nayantam jagrāha vṛkam hariḥ iva ojasā sa nijam rūpam āsthāya giri indra sadṛśam balī icchan vimoktum ātmānam na aśaknot grahaṇa āturaḥ tam nigṛhya acyutaḥ dorbhyām pātayitvā mahī tale paśyatām divi devānām paśu māram amārayat guhā pidhānam nirbhidya gopān niḥsārya kṛcchrataḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca akrūraḥ api ca tām rātrim madhu puryām mahā matiḥ kim mayā ācaritam bhadram kim taptam paramam tapaḥ kim vā atha api arhate dattam yat drakṣyāmi adya keśavam viṣaya ātmanaḥ yathā brahma kīrtanam śūdra janmanaḥ mā evam mama adhamasya api syāt eva acyuta darśanam mama adya amaṅgalam naṣṭam phalavān ca eva me bhavaḥ kaṃsaḥ bata adya akṛta me ati anugraham drakṣye aṅghri padmam prahitaḥ amunā hareḥ kṛta avatārasya duratyayam tamaḥ pūrve ataran yad nakha maṇḍala tviṣā śriyā ca devyā munibhiḥ sa sātvataiḥ go cāraṇāya anucaraiḥ carat vane yat gopikānām kuca kuṅkuma aṅkitam drakṣyāmi nūnam su kapola nāsikam smita avaloka aruṇa kañja locanam mukham mukundasya guḍālaka āvṛtam pradakṣiṇam me pracaranti vai mṛgāḥ api adya viṣṇoḥ manuja tvam īyuṣaḥ bhāra avatārāya bhuvaḥ nija icchayā lāvaṇya dhāmnaḥ bhavitā upalambhanam mahyam na na syāt phalam añjasā dṛśaḥ yaḥ īkṣita aham rahitaḥ api asat satoḥ sva tejasā apāsta tamaḥ bhidā bhramaḥ sva māyayā ātman racitaiḥ tad īkṣayā prāṇa akṣa dhībhiḥ sadaneṣu abhīyate yasya akhila amīva habhiḥ su maṅgalaiḥ vācaḥ vimiśrāḥ guṇa karma janmabhiḥ prāṇanti śumbhanti punanti vai jagat yāḥ tad viraktāḥ śava śobhanāḥ matāḥ sa ca avatīrṇaḥ kila satvata anvaye sva setu pāla amara varya śarma kṛt yaśaḥ vitanvan vraje āste īśvaraḥ gāyanti devāḥ yat aśeṣa maṅgalam tam tu adya nūnam mahatām gatim gurum rūpam dadhānam śriyaḥ īpsita āspadam drakṣye mama āsan uṣasaḥ su darśanāḥ atha avarūḍhaḥ sapadīśayoḥ rathāt pradhāna puṃsoḥ caraṇam sva labdhaye dhiyā dhṛtam yogibhiḥ api aham dhruvam namasyaḥ ābhyām ca sakhīn vanaukasaḥ datta abhayam kāla bhujāṅga raṃhasā prodvejitānām śaraṇa eṣiṇām ṇṛnām kaṃsasya dūtaḥ prahitaḥ api viśva dṛś kṣetra jñaḥ īkṣati amalena cakṣuṣā api aṅghri mūle avahitam kṛtāñjalim mām īkṣitā sa smitam ārdrayā dṛśā voḍhā mudam vīta viśaṅkaḥ ūrjitām suhṛttamam jñātim ananya daivatam dorbhyām bṛhadbhyām parirapsyate atha mām labdhvā aṅga saṅgam praṇatam kṛtāñjalim mām vakṣyate akrūra tata iti uruśravāḥ tadā vayam janma bhṛtaḥ mahīyasā kim ca agrajaḥ mā avanatam yadu uttamaḥ smayan pariṣvajya gṛhītam añjalau gṛham praveṣya āpta samasta satkṛtam samprakṣyate kaṃsa kṛtam sva bandhuṣu śrī śukaḥ uvāca rathena gokulam prāptaḥ sūryaḥ ca asta girim nṛpa padāni tasya akhila loka pāla kirīṭa juṣṭa amala pāda reṇoḥ dadarśa goṣṭhe kṣiti kautukāni vilakṣitāni abja yavāṅkuśa ādyaiḥ tad darśana āhlāda vivṛddha sambhramaḥ premṇā ūrdhva roma aśru kalā ākula īkṣaṇaḥ dehaṃbhṛtām iyān arthaḥ hitvā dambham bhiyam śucam sandeśāt yaḥ hareḥ liṅga darśana śravaṇa ādibhiḥ dadarśa kṛṣṇam rāmam ca vraje go dohanam gatau pīta nīla ambara dharau śarad amburaha īkṣaṇau kiśorau śyāmala śvetau śrī niketau bṛhat bhujau śobhayantau mahātmānau sa anukrośa smita īkṣaṇau pradhāna puruṣau ādyau jagat hetū jagat patī avatīrṇau jagatī arthe sva aṃśena bala keśavau diśaḥ vitimirāḥ rājan kurvāṇau prabhayā svayā yathā mārakataḥ śailaḥ raupyaḥ ca kanaka ācitau papāta caraṇa upānte daṇḍa vat rāma kṛṣṇayoḥ bhagavat darśana āhlāda bāṣpa paryākula īkṣaṇaḥ pulaka cita aṅgaḥ autkaṇṭhyāt su ākhyāne na aśakat nṛpa bhagavān tam abhipretya rathāṅga aṅkita pāṇinā parirebhe abhyupākṛṣya prītaḥ praṇata vatsalaḥ saṅkarṣaṇaḥ ca praṇatam upaguhya mahā manāḥ gṛhītvā pāṇinā pāṇī anayat sa anujaḥ gṛham pṛṣṭvā atha su āgatam tasmai nivedya ca varāsanam nivedya gām ca atithaye saṃvāhya śrāntam āḍṛtaḥ annam bahu guṇam medhyam śraddhayā upāharat vibhuḥ makha vāsaiḥ gandha mālyaiḥ parām prītim vyadhāt punar kaṃse jīvati dāśārha sauna pālāḥ iva avayaḥ kim nu svid tat prajānām vaḥ kuśalam vimṛśāmahe ittham sūnṛtayā vācā nandena su sabhājitaḥ akrūraḥ paripṛṣṭena jahau adhva pariśramam śrī śukaḥ uvāca sukha upaviṣṭaḥ paryaṅke rama kṛṣṇa ūru mānitaḥ tathā api tad pare rājan na hi vāñchanti kiñcana sāyantanāśanam kṛtvā bhagavān devakī sutaḥ suhṛtsu vṛttam kaṃsasya papraccha anyat cikīrṣitam śrī bhagavān uvāca api sva jñāti bandhūnām anamīvam anāmayam kim nu naḥ kuśalam pṛcche edhamāne kula āmaye kaṃse mātula nāmnā aṅga svānām naḥ tad prajāsu ca diṣṭyā adya darśanam svānām mahyam vaḥ saumya kāṅkṣitam sañjātam varṇyatām tāta tava āgamana kāraṇam śrī śukaḥ uvāca pṛṣṭaḥ bhagavatā sarvam varṇayām āsa mādhavaḥ yad sandeśaḥ yad artham vā dūtaḥ sampreṣitaḥ svayam śrutvā akrūra vacaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ balaḥ ca para vīra hā prahasya nandam pitaram rājñā diṣṭam vijajñatuḥ gopān samādiśat saḥ api gṛhyatām sarva go rasaḥ upāyanāni gṛhṇīdhvam yujyantām śakaṭāni ca yāsyāmaḥ śvas madhu purīm dāsyāmaḥ nṛpate rasān drakṣyāmaḥ su mahat parva yānti jānapadāḥ kila rāma kṛṣṇau purīm netum akrūram vrajam āgatam kāścid tad kṛta hṛd tāpa śvāsa mlāna mukha śriyaḥ anyāḥ ca tad anudhyāna nivṛtta aśeṣa vṛttayaḥ na abhyajānan imam lokam ātma lokam gatāḥ iva smarantyaḥ ca aparāḥ śaureḥ anurāga smita īritāḥ hṛdi spṛśaḥ citra padāḥ giraḥ sammumuhuḥ striyaḥ gatim su lalitām ceṣṭām snigdha hāsa avalokanam śoka apahāni narmāṇi proddāma caritāni ca sametāḥ saṅghaśas procuḥ aśru mukhyaḥ acyuta āśayāḥ śrī gopyaḥ ūcuḥ tān ca akṛtārthān viyunaṅkṣi apārthakam vikrīḍitam te arbhaka ceṣṭitam yathā yaḥ tvam pradarśya asita kuntala āvṛtam karoṣi pārokṣyam asādhu te kṛtam krūraḥ tvam akrūra samākhyayā sma naś tvadīyam adrākṣma vayam madhu dviṣaḥ na nanda sūnuḥ kṣaṇa bhaṅga sauhṛdaḥ samīkṣate naḥ sva kṛta āturā bata vihāya gehān sva janān sutān patīn sukham prabhātāḥ rajanīyam āśiṣaḥ satyāḥ babhūvuḥ pura yoṣitām dhruvam yāḥ saṃpraviṣṭasya mukham vrajas pateḥ pāsyanti apāṅga utkalita smita āsavam tāsām mukundaḥ madhu mañju bhāṣitaiḥ adya dhruvam tatra dṛśaḥ bhaviṣyate dāśārha bhoja andhaka vṛṣṇi sātvatām mahā utsavaḥ śrī ramaṇam guṇa āspadam drakṣyanti ye ca adhvani devakī sutam mā etad vidhasya akaruṇasya nāma bhūt akrūraḥ iti etat atīva dāruṇaḥ yaḥ asau an āśvāsya su duḥkhitam janam priyāt priyam neṣyati pāram adhvanaḥ nivārayāmaḥ samupetya mādhavam kim naḥ akariṣyan kula vṛddha bāndhavāḥ līlāvaloka parirambhaṇa rāsa goṣṭhām nītāḥ sma naḥ kṣaṇam iva kṣaṇadā vinā tam veṇum kvaṇan smita kata akṣa nirīkṣaṇena śrī śukaḥ uvāca evam bruvāṇāḥ viraha āturāḥ bhṛśam vraja striyaḥ kṛṣṇa viṣakta mānasāḥ strīṇām evam rudantīnām udite savitari atha akrūraḥ codayām āsa kṛta maitra ādikaḥ ratham gopāḥ tam anvasajjanta nanda ādyāḥ śakaṭaiḥ tatas ādāya upāyanam bhūri kumbhān go rasa sambhṛtān gopyaḥ ca dayitam kṛṣṇam anuvrajya anurañjitāḥ pratyādeśam bhagavataḥ kāṅkṣantyaḥ ca avatasthire tāḥ tathā tapyatīḥ vīkṣya sva prasthāṇe yadu uttamaḥ yāvat ālakṣyate ketuḥ yāvat reṇuḥ rathasya ca anuprasthāpita ātmānaḥ lekhyāni iva upalakṣitāḥ viśokāḥ ahanī ninyuḥ gāyantyaḥ priya ceṣṭitam bhagavān api samprāptaḥ rāma akrūra yutaḥ nṛpa rathena vāyu vegena kālindīm agha nāśinīm tatra upaspṛśya pānīyam pītvā mṛṣṭam maṇi prabham vṛkṣa ṣaṇḍam upavrajya sa rāmaḥ ratham āviśat kālindyāḥ hradam āgatya snānam vidhi vat ācarat tau eva dadṛśe akrūraḥ rāma kṛṣṇau samanvitau tatra api ca yathā pūrvam āsīnau punar eva saḥ nyamajjat darśanam yat me mṛṣā kim salile tayoḥ bhūyas tatra api saḥ adrākṣīt stūyamānam ahīśvaram nīla ambaram śṛṅgaiḥ śvetam iva sthitam tasya utsaṅge ghana syāmam pīta kauśeya vāsasam puruṣam catur bhujam śāntam padma pattra aruṇa īkṣaṇam cāru prasanna vadanam cāru hāsa nirīkṣaṇam su bhrū unnasam caru karṇam su kapola aruṇa adharam pralamba pīvara bhujam tuṅga aṃsa uraḥ sthala śriyam cāru jānu yugam cāru jaṅghā yugala saṃyutam nava aṅguli aṅguṣṭha dalaiḥ vilasat pāda paṅkajam su mahārha maṇi vrāta kirīṭa kaṭaka aṅgadaiḥ kaṭi sūtra brahma sūtra hāra nūpura kuṇḍalaiḥ bhrājamānam padma karam śaṅkha cakra gadā dharam śrīvatsa vakṣasam bhrājat kaustubham vana mālinam stūyamānam pṛthak bhāvaiḥ vacobhiḥ amala ātmabhiḥ śriyā puṣṭyā girā kāntyā kīrtyā tuṣṭyā ilayoḥ ūrjayā vidyayā avidyayā śaktyā māyayā ca niṣevitam vilokya su bhṛśam prītaḥ bhaktyā paramayā yutaḥ hṛṣyat tanūruhaḥ bhāva pariklinna ātma locanaḥ girā gadgadayā astauṣīt sattvam ālambya sātvataḥ praṇamya mūrdhnā avahitaḥ kṛta añjali puṭaḥ śanais śrī akrūraḥ uvāca nataḥ asmi aham tvā akhila hetu hetum nārāyaṇam pūruṣam ādyam avyayam yad nābhi jātāt aravinda koṣāt brahmā avirāsīt yatas eṣa lokaḥ bhūḥ toyam agniḥ pavanam kham ādiḥ mahān aja ādiḥ manaḥ indriyāṇi na ete sva rūpam viduḥ ātmanaḥ te hi aja ādayaḥ anātma tayā gṛhītaḥ ajaḥ anubaddhaḥ sa guṇaiḥ ajāyāḥ guṇāt param veda na te svarūpam tvām yoginaḥ yajanti addhā mahā puruṣam īśvaram sa adhyātmam sa adhibhūtam ca sa adhidaivam ca sādhavaḥ trayyā ca vidyayā kecid tvām vai vaitānikāḥ dvijāḥ yajante vitataiḥ yajñaiḥ nānā rūpa amara ākhyayā eke tvā akhila karmāṇi sannyasya upaśamam gatāḥ jñāninaḥ jñāna yajñena yajanti jñāna vigraham tvām eva anye śiva uktena mārgeṇa śiva rūpiṇam yathā adri prabhavāḥ nadyaḥ parjanya āpūritāḥ prabho sattvam rajaḥ tamaḥ iti bhavataḥ prakṛteḥ guṇāḥ teṣu hi prākṛtāḥ protāḥ ā brahma sthāvara ādayaḥ tubhyam namaḥ te tu aviṣakta dṛṣṭaye sarva ātmane sarva dhiyām ca sākṣiṇe guṇa pravāhaḥ ayam avidyayā kṛtaḥ agniḥ mukham te avaniḥ aṅghriḥ īkṣaṇam sūryaḥ nabhaḥ nābhiḥ atho diśaḥ śrutiḥ dyauḥ kam sura indrāḥ tava bāhavaḥ arṇavāḥ romāṇi vṛkṣa oṣadhayaḥ śiroruhā meghāḥ parasya asthi nakhāni te adrayaḥ nimeṣaṇam rātri ahanī prajāpatiḥ meḍhraḥ tu vṛṣṭiḥ tava vīryam iṣyate tvayi avyaya ātman puruṣe prakalpitāḥ lokāḥ sa pālāḥ bahu jīva saṅkulāḥ yāni yāni iha rūpāṇi krīḍana artham bibharṣi hi taiḥ āmṛṣṭa śucaḥ lokāḥ mudā gāyanti te yaśaḥ namaḥ kāraṇa matsyāya pralaya abdhi carāya ca haya śīrṣṇe namaḥ tubhyam madhu kaiṭabha mṛtyave akūpārāya bṛhate namaḥ mandara dhāriṇe kṣiti uddhāra vihārāya namaḥ śūkara mūrtaye namaḥ bhṛguṇām pataye dṛpta kṣatra vana chide namaḥ te vāsudevāya namaḥ saṅkarṣaṇāya ca namaḥ aham ca ātma ātmaja āgāra dāra artha sva jana ādiṣu dvandva ārāmaḥ tamaḥ viṣṭaḥ na jāne tvā ātmanaḥ priyam abhyeti mṛga tṛṣṇām vai tadvat tvā aham parāc mukhaḥ na utsahe aham kṛpaṇa dhīḥ kāma karma hatam manaḥ roddhum pramāthibhiḥ ca akṣaiḥ hriyamāṇam itas tatas saḥ aham tava aṅghri upagataḥ asmi asatām durāpam puruṣa īśa pradhānāya brahmaṇe ananta śaktaye hṛṣīkeśa namaḥ tubhyam prapannam pāhi mām prabho śrī śukaḥ uvāca bhūyas samāharat kṛṣṇaḥ naṭaḥ nāṭyam iva ātmanaḥ kṛtvā ca āvaśyakam sarvam vismitaḥ ratham āgamat tam apṛcchat dhṛṣīkeśaḥ kim te dṛṣṭam iva adbhutam bhūmau viyati toye vā tathā tvām lakṣayāmahe śrī akrūraḥ uvāca tvayi viśvātmake tāni kim me adṛṣṭam vipaśyataḥ yatra adbhutāni sarvāṇi bhūmau viyati vā jale tam tvā anupaśyataḥ brahman kim me dṛṣṭam iha adbhutam iti uktvā codayām āsa syandanam gāndinī sutaḥ mathurām anayat rāmam kṛṣṇam ca eva dina atyaye mārge grāma janāḥ rājan tatra tatra upasaṅgatāḥ vasudeva sutau vīkṣya prītāḥ dṛṣṭim na ca ādaduḥ tān sametya āha bhagavant akrūram jagat īśvaraḥ gṛhītvā pāṇinā pāṇim praśritam prahasan iva bhavān praviśatām agre saha yānaḥ purīm gṛham vayam tu iha avamucya atha tatas drakṣyāmahe purīm śrī akrūraḥ uvāca na aham bhavadbhyām rahitaḥ pravekṣye mathurām prabho āgaccha yāma gehān naḥ sa nāthān kuru adhokṣaja saha agrajaḥ sa gopālaiḥ suhṛdbhiḥ ca suhṛttama punīhi pāda rajasā gṛhān naḥ gṛha medhinām yat śaucena anutṛpyanti pitaraḥ sa agnayaḥ surāḥ avanijya aṅghri yugalam āsīt ślokyaḥ baliḥ mahān aiśvaryam atulam lebhe gatim ca ekāntinām tu yā śirasā ādhatta yāḥ śarvaḥ svar yātāḥ sagara ātmajāḥ nārāyaṇa namaḥ astu te śrī bhagavant uvāca śrī śukaḥ uvāca purīm praviṣṭaḥ kaṃsāya karma āvedya gṛham yayau atha aparāhne bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ saṅkarṣaṇa anvitaḥ mathurām prāviśat gopaiḥ didṛkṣuḥ parivāritaḥ dadarśa tām sphāṭika tuṇga gopura dvārām bṛhat hema kapāṭa toraṇām tāmrāri koṣṭhām parikhā durāsadām udyāna ramya upavana upaśobhitām sauvarṇa śṛṅgāṭaka harmya niṣkuṭaiḥ śreṇī sabhābhiḥ bhavanaiḥ upaskṛtām juṣṭeṣu jālāmukha randhra kuṭṭimeṣu āviṣṭa pārāvata barhi nāditām saṃsikta rathyā āpaṇa mārga catvarām prakīrṇa mālya aṅkura lāja taṇḍulām āpūrṇa kumbhaiḥ dadhi candana ukṣitaiḥ prasūna dīpa āvalibhiḥ sa pallavaiḥ sa vṛnda rambhā kramukaiḥ sa ketubhiḥ su alaṅkṛta dvāra gṛhām sa paṭṭikaiḥ draṣṭum samīyuḥ tvaritāḥ pura striyaḥ harmyāṇi ca eva āruruhuḥ nṛpa utsukāḥ kāścid viparyak dhṛta vastra bhūṣaṇā vismṛtya ca ekam yugaleṣu atha aparāḥ na aṅktvā dvitīyam tu aparāḥ ca locanam aśnantyaḥ ekāḥ tat apāsya sa utsavāḥ abhyajyamānāḥ a kṛta upamajjanāḥ manāṃsi tāsām aravinda locanaḥ pragalbha līlā hasita avalokaiḥ dṛṣṭvā muhur śrutam anudruta cetasaḥ tam tad prekṣaṇa utsmita sudhā ukṣaṇa labdha mānāḥ ānanda mūrtim upaguhya dṛśā ātma labdham prāsāda śikhara ārūḍhāḥ prīti utphulla mukha ambujāḥ tau ānarcuḥ pramuditāḥ tatra tatra dvijātayaḥ rajakam kañcid āyāntam raṅga kāram gadāgrajaḥ dṛṣṭvā ayācata vāsāṃsi dhautāni ati uttamāni ca dehi āvayoḥ samucitāni aṅga vāsāṃsi ca arhatoḥ bhaviṣyati param śreyaḥ dātuḥ te na atra saṃśayaḥ sa ākṣepam ruṣitaḥ prāha bhṛtyaḥ rājñaḥ su durmadaḥ īdṛśāni eva vāsāṃsī nityam giri vane caraḥ yāta āśu bāliśāḥ mā evam prārthyam yadi jijīvīṣā rajakasya kara agreṇa śiraḥ kāyāt apātayat tasya anujīvinaḥ sarve vāsaḥ kośān visṛjya vai dudruvuḥ sarvatas mārgam vāsāṃsi jagṛhe acyutaḥ vasitvā ātma priye vastre kṛṣṇaḥ saṅkarṣaṇaḥ tathā śeṣāṇi ādatta gopebhyaḥ visṛjya bhuvi kānicid nānā lakṣaṇa veṣābhyām kṛṣṇa rāmau virejatuḥ tasya prasannaḥ bhagavān prādāt sārūpyam ātmanaḥ śriyam ca paramām loke bala aiśvarya smṛti indriyam tatas sudāmnaḥ bhavanam mālā kārasya jagmatuḥ tau dṛṣṭvā sa samutthāya nanāma śirasā bhuvi tayoḥ āsanam ānīya pādyam ca arghya arhaṇa ādibhiḥ pūjām sa anugayoḥ cakre sraj tāmbūla anulepanaiḥ prāha naḥ sārthakam janma pāvitam ca kulam prabho pitṛ deva ṛṣayaḥ mahyam tuṣṭāḥ hi āgamanena vām avatīrṇau iha aṃśena kṣemāya ca bhavāya ca na hi vām viṣamā dṛṣṭiḥ suhṛdoḥ jagat ātmanoḥ tau ajñāpayatam bhṛtyam kim aham karavāṇi vām iti abhipretya rāja indra sudāmā prīta mānasaḥ tābhiḥ su alaṅkṛtau prītau kṛṣṇa rāmau saha anugau tad bhakteṣu ca sauhārdam bhūteṣu ca dayām parām balam āyuḥ yaśaḥ kāntim nirjagāma saha agrajaḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca atha vrajan rāja pathena mādhavaḥ striyam gṛhīta aṅga vilepa bhājanām vilokya kubjām yuvatīm varānanām papraccha yāntam prahasan rasa pradaḥ kā tvam vara ūro etat u ha anulepanam kasya aṅgane vā kathayasva sādhu naḥ rūpa peśala mādhurya hasita ālāpa vīkṣitaiḥ tatas tau aṅga rāgeṇa sva varṇa itara śobhinā samprāpta para bhāgena śuśubhāte anurañjitau prasannaḥ bhagavān kubjām tri vakrām rucira ānanām ṛjvīm kartum manaḥ cakre darśayan darśane phalam padbhyām ākramya prapade dri aṅguli uttāna pāṇinā sā tad arju samāna aṅgā bṛhat śroṇi payodharā tatas rūpa guṇa audārya sampannā prāha keśavam uttarīya antam a kṛṣya smayantī jāta hṛd śayā ehi vīra gṛham yāmaḥ na tvām tyaktum iha utsahe tvayā unmathita cittāyāḥ prasīda puruṣa ṛṣabha evam striyā yācyamānaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ rāmasya paśyataḥ mukham vīkṣya anu gopānām prahasan tām uvāca ha eṣyāmi te gṛham su bhru puṃsām ādhi vikarśanam sādhita arthaḥ agṛhāṇām naḥ pānthānām tvam parāyaṇam visṛjya mādhvyā vāṇyā tām vrajan mārge vaṇij pathaiḥ nānā upāyana tāmbūla sraj gandhaiḥ sa agrajaḥ arcitaḥ tad darśana smara kṣobhāt ātmānam na avidan striyaḥ tatas paurān pṛcchamānaḥ dhanuṣaḥ sthānam acyutaḥ vāryamāṇaḥ nṛbhiḥ kṛṣṇaḥ prasahya dhanuḥ ādade kareṇa vāmena sa līlam uddhṛtam sajyam ca kṛtvā nimiṣeṇa paśyatām nṛṇām vikṛṣya prababhañja madhyatas yathā ikṣu daṇḍam mada karī urukramaḥ dhanuṣaḥ bhajyamānasya śabdaḥ kham rodasī diśaḥ pūrayām āsa yam śrutvā kaṃsaḥ trāsam upāgamat tad rakṣiṇaḥ sa anucaram kupitāḥ ātatāyinaḥ gṛhītu kāmāḥ āvavruḥ gṛhyatām vadhyatām iti kruddhau dhanvanaḥ ādāya śakale tān ca jaghnatuḥ balam ca kaṃsa prahitam hatvā śālā mukhāt tatas niṣkramya ceratuḥ hṛṣṭau nirīkṣya pura sampadaḥ tayoḥ tat adbhutam vīryam niśāmya pura vāsinaḥ kṛṣṇa rāmau vṛtau gopaiḥ purāt śakaṭam īyatuḥ gopyaḥ mukunda vigame viraha āturāḥ yāḥ āśāsata āśiṣaḥ ṛtāḥ madhu puri abhūvan sampaśyatām puruṣa bhūṣaṇa gātra lakṣmīm hitvā itarān nu bhajataḥ cakame ayanam śrīḥ ūṣatuḥ tām sukham rātrim jñātvā kaṃsa cikīrṣitam kaṃsaḥ tu dhanuṣaḥ bhaṅgam rakṣiṇām sva balasya ca vadham niśamya govinda rāma vikrīḍitam param bahūni acaṣṭa ubhayathā mṛtyoḥ dautya karāṇi ca asati api dvitīye ca dvairūpyam jyotiṣām tathā chidra pratītiḥ chāyāyām prāṇa ghoṣa an upaśrutiḥ svarṇa pratītiḥ vṛkṣeṣu sva padānām adarśanam svapne preta pariṣvaṅgaḥ khara yānam viṣādanam anyāni ca itthaṃbhūtāni svapna jāgaritāni ca vyuṣṭāyām niśi kauravya sūrye ca adbhyaḥ samutthite kārayām āsa vai kaṃsaḥ malla krīḍā mahā utsavam ānarcuḥ puruṣāḥ raṅgam tūrya bheryaḥ ca jaghnire mañcāḥ ca alaṅkṛtāḥ sragbhiḥ patākā caila toraṇaiḥ teṣu paurāḥ jānapadāḥ brahma kṣatra purogamāḥ yathopajoṣam viviśuḥ rājānaḥ ca kṛta āsanāḥ kaṃsaḥ parivṛtaḥ amātyaiḥ rāja mañce upāviśat maṇḍaleśvara madhya sthaḥ hṛdayena vidūyatā vādyamānesu tūryeṣu malla tālottareṣu ca mallāḥ su alaṅkṛtāḥ dṛptāḥ sa upādhyāyāḥ samāsata cāṇūraḥ muṣṭikaḥ kūtaḥ śalaḥ tośalaḥ eva ca te āseduḥ upasthānam valgu vādya praharṣitāḥ nanda gopa ādayaḥ gopāḥ bhoja rāja samāhutāḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca atha kṛṣṇaḥ ca rāmaḥ ca kṛta śaucau parantapa malla dundubhi nirghoṣam śrutvā draṣṭum upeyatuḥ apaśyat kuvalayāpīḍam kṛṣṇaḥ ambaṣṭha pracoditam baddhvā parikaram śauriḥ samuhya kuṭila alakān uvāca hastipam vācā megha nāda gabhīrayā ambaṣṭha ambaṣṭha mārgam nau dehi apakrama mā ciram codayām āsa kṛṣṇāya kāla antaka yama upamam karāt vigalitaḥ saḥ amum nihatya aṅghriṣu alīyata saṅkruddhaḥ tam acakṣāṇaḥ ghrāṇa dṛṣṭiḥ sa keśavam parāmṛśat puṣkareṇa sa prasahya vinirgataḥ pucche pragṛhya ati balam dhanuṣaḥ pañca viṃśatim vicakarṣa yathā nāgam suparṇaḥ iva līlayā babhrāma bhrāmyamāṇena go vatsena iva bālakaḥ prādravan pātayām āsa spṛśyamānaḥ pade pade sa dhāvan kṛīdayā bhūmau patitvā sahasā utthitaḥ codyamānaḥ mahāmātraiḥ kṛṣṇam abhyadravat ruṣā tam āpatantam āsādya bhagavant madhusūdanaḥ nigṛhya pāṇinā hastam pātayām āsa bhū tale dantam utpāṭya tena ibham hastipān ca ahanat hariḥ mṛtakam dvipam utsṛjya danta pāṇiḥ samāviśat aṃsa nyasta viṣāṇaḥ asṛj mada bindubhiḥ aṅkitaḥ raṅgam viviśatuḥ rājan gaja danta vara āyudhau mallānām aśaniḥ nṛṇām nara varaḥ strīṇām smaraḥ mūrtimān gopānām sva janaḥ asatām kṣiti bhujām śāstā sva pitroḥ śiśuḥ mṛtyuḥ bhoja pateḥ virāj aviduṣām tattvam param yoginām vṛṣṇīnām para devatā iti viditaḥ raṅgam gataḥ sāgrajaḥ hatam kuvalayāpīḍam dṛṣṭvā tau api durjayau yathā naṭau uttama veṣa dhāriṇau manaḥ kṣipantau prabhayā nirīkṣatām nirīkṣya tau uttama pūruṣau janāḥ mañca sthitāḥ nāgara rāṣṭrakāḥ nṛpa praharṣa vega utkalita īkṣaṇa ānanāḥ papuḥ na tṛptāḥ nayanaiḥ tad ānanam jighrantaḥ iva nāsābhyām śliṣyantaḥ iva bāhubhiḥ ūcuḥ parasparam te vai yathā dṛṣṭam yathā śrutam tad rūpa guṇa mādhurya prāgalbhya smāritāḥ iva etau bhagavataḥ sākṣāt hareḥ nārāyaṇasya hi avatīrṇau iha aṃśena vasudevasya veśmani eṣa vai kila devakyām jātaḥ nītaḥ ca gokulam kālam etam vasan gūḍhaḥ vavṛdhe nanda veśmani pūtanā anena nīta antam cakravātaḥ ca dānavaḥ gāvaḥ sa pālāḥ etena dāva agneḥ parimocitāḥ kāliyaḥ damitaḥ sarpaḥ indraḥ ca vimadaḥ kṛtaḥ varṣa vāta aśanibhyaḥ ca paritrātam ca gokulam paśyantyaḥ vividhān tāpān taranti sma āśramam mudā vadanti anena vaṃśaḥ ayam yadoḥ su bahu viśrutaḥ śriyam yaśaḥ mahatvam ca lapsyate parirakṣitaḥ ayam ca asya agrajaḥ śrīmān rāmaḥ kamala locanaḥ janeṣu evam bruvāṇeṣu tūryeṣu ninadatsu ca kṛṣṇa rāmau samābhāṣya cāṇūraḥ vākyam abravīt niyuddha kuśalau śrutvā rājñā āhūtau didṛkṣuṇā priyam rājñaḥ prakurvatyaḥ śreyaḥ vindanti vai prajāḥ manasā karmaṇā vācā viparītam atas anyathā nityam pramuditāḥ gopāḥ vatsa pālāḥ yathā sphuṭam vaneṣu malla yuddhena krīḍantaḥ cārayanti gāḥ tasmāt rājñaḥ priyam yūyam vayam ca karavāma he bhūtāni naḥ prasīdanti sarva bhūta mayaḥ nṛpaḥ tat niśamya abravīt kṛṣṇaḥ deśa kāla ucitam vacaḥ bālāḥ vayam tulya balaiḥ krīḍiṣyāmaḥ yathocitam bhavet niyuddham mā adharmaḥ spṛśet malla sabhā sadaḥ cāṇūraḥ uvāca na bālaḥ na kiśoraḥ tvam balaḥ ca balinām varaḥ mayi vikrama vārṣṇeya balena saha muṣṭikaḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca āsasāda atha caṇūram muṣṭtikam rohiṇī sutaḥ hastābhyām hastayoḥ baddhvā padbhyām eva ca pādayoḥ aratnī dve aratnibhyām jānubhyām ca eva jānunī śiraḥ śīrṣṇā urasā uraḥ tau anyonyam abhijaghnatuḥ paribhrāmaṇa vikṣepa parirambha avapātanaiḥ utsarpaṇa apasarpaṇaiḥ ca anyonyam pratyarundhatām parasparam jigīṣantau apacakratuḥ ātmanaḥ tat balābalavat yuddham sametāḥ sarva yoṣitaḥ ūcuḥ parasparam rājan sa anukampāḥ varūthaśas mahān ayam bata adharmaḥ eṣām rāja sabhā sadām kva ca ati sukumāra aṅgau kiśorau na āpta yauvanau na sabhām praviśet prājñaḥ sabhya doṣān anusmaran valgataḥ śatrum abhitas kṛṣṇasya vadana ambujam vīkṣyatām śrama vāri uptam padma kośam iva ambuṣu muṣṭikam prati sa amarṣam hāsa saṃrambha śobhitam puṇyāḥ bata vraja bhuvaḥ yat ayam nṛ liṅga gūḍhaḥ purāṇa puruṣaḥ vana citra mālyaḥ gāḥ pālayan saha balaḥ kvaṇayan ca veṇum vikrīdayā añcati ekānta dhāma yaśasaḥ śrīya aiśvarasya prātar vrajāt vrajataḥ āviśataḥ ca sāyam nirgamya tūrṇam abalāḥ pathini bhūri puṇyāḥ evam prabhāṣamāṇāsu strīṣu yogeśvaraḥ hariḥ sa bhayāḥ strī giraḥ śrutvā putra sneha śucā āturau bhagavat gātra niṣpātaiḥ vajra nīṣpeṣa niṣṭhuraiḥ cāṇūraḥ bhajyamāna aṅgaḥ muhur glānim avāpa ha sa śyena vegaḥ utpatya muṣṭī kṛtya karau ubhau na acalat tad prahāreṇa mālā hataḥ iva dvipaḥ bāhvoḥ nigṛhya cāṇūram bahuśas bhrāmayan hariḥ bhū pṛṣṭhe pothayām āsa tarasā kṣīṇa jīvitam tathā eva muṣṭikaḥ pūrvam sva muṣṭyā abhihatena vai vyasuḥ papāta urvī upasthe vāta āhataḥ iva aṅghripaḥ tatas kūṭam anuprāptam rāmaḥ praharatām varaḥ avadhīt līlayā rājan sa avajñam vāma muṣṭinā tarhi eva hi śalaḥ kṛṣṇa prapada āhata śīrṣakaḥ dvidhā vidīrṇaḥ tośalakaḥ ubhau api nipetatuḥ cāṇūre muṣṭike kūṭe śale tośalake hate śeṣāḥ pradudruvuḥ mallāḥ sarve prāṇa parīpsavaḥ gopān vayasyān ākṛṣya taiḥ saṃsṛjya vijahratuḥ vādyamāneṣu tūryeṣu valgantau ruta nūpurau janāḥ prajahṛṣuḥ sarve karmaṇā rāma kṛṣṇayoḥ ṛte kaṃsam vipra mukhyāḥ sādhavaḥ sādhu sādhu iti nyavārayat sva tūryāṇi vākyam ca idam uvāca ha ugrasenaḥ pitā ca api sa anugaḥ para pakṣa gaḥ tam āviśantam ālokya mṛtyum ātmanaḥ āsanāt tam khaḍga pāṇim vicarantam āśu śyenam yathā dakṣiṇa savyam ambare pragṛhya keśeṣu calat kirītam nipātya raṅga upari tuṅga mañcāt tasya upariṣṭāt svayam abja nābhaḥ papāta viśvāśrayaḥ ātma tantraḥ hā hā iti śabdaḥ su mahān tadā abhūt udīritaḥ sarva janaiḥ narendra tasya anujāḥ bhrātaraḥ aṣṭau kaṅka nyagrodhaka ādayaḥ abhyadhāvan ati kruddhāḥ bhrātuḥ nirveśa kāriṇaḥ tathā ati rabhasān tān tu saṃyattān rohiṇī sutaḥ puṣpaiḥ kirantaḥ tam prītāḥ śaśaṃsuḥ nanṛtuḥ striyaḥ teṣām striyaḥ mahā rāja suhṛd maraṇa duḥkhitāḥ tatra abhīyuḥ vinighnantyaḥ śīrṣāṇi aśru vilocanāḥ śayānān vīra śayāyām patīn āliṅgya śocatīḥ vilepuḥ su svaram nāryaḥ visṛjantyaḥ muhur śucaḥ hā nātha priya dharma jña karuṇā nātha vatsala tvayā hatena nihatāḥ vayam te sa gṛha prajāḥ tvayā virahitā patyā purī iyam puruṣa ṛṣabha anāgasām tvam bhūtānām kṛtavān droham ulbaṇam tena imām bho daśām nītaḥ kaḥ labheta śam sarveṣām iha bhūtānām eṣa hi prabhava apyayaḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca rāja yoṣitaḥ āśvāsya bhagavān loka bhāvanaḥ yām āhuḥ laukikīm saṃsthām hatānām samakārayat kṛṣṇa rāmau vavandāte śirasā spṛśya pādayoḥ devakī vasudevaḥ ca vijñāya jagat īśvarau śrī śukaḥ uvāca mā bhūt iti nijām māyām tatāna jana mohinīm uvāca pitarā etya sa agrajaḥ sātvana ṛṣabhaḥ praśraya avanataḥ prīṇan amba tāta iti sādaram bālya paugaṇḍa kaiśorāḥ putrābhyām abhavan kvacid yām bālāḥ pitṛ geha sthāḥ vindante lālitāḥ mudam na tayoḥ yāti nirveśam pitroḥ martyaḥ śata āyuṣā vṛttim na dadyāt tam pretya sva māṃsam khādayanti hi mātaram pitaram vṛddham bhāryām sādhvīm sutam śiśum a kurvatoḥ vām śuśrūṣām kliṣṭayoḥ durhṛdā bhṛśam śrī śukaḥ uvāca iti māyā manuṣyasya hareḥ viśvātmanaḥ girā siñcantau aśru dhārābhiḥ sneha pāśena ca āvṛtau na kiñcid ūcatuḥ rājan bāṣpa kaṇṭhau vimohitau evam āśvāsya pitarā bhagavān devakī sutaḥ mātāmaham tu ugrasenam yadūnām akarot ṇṛpam āha ca asmān mahā rāja prajāḥ ca ājñaptum arhasi yayāti śāpāt yadubhiḥ na āsitavyam nṛpa āsane balim haranti avanatāḥ kim uta anye narādhipāḥ sarvān svān jñati sambandhān digbhyaḥ kaṃsa bhaya ākulān yadu vṛṣṇi andhaka madhu dāśārha kukura ādikān sabhājitān samāśvāsya videśa āvāsa karśitān kṛṣṇa saṅkarṣaṇa bhujaiḥ guptāḥ labdha manorathāḥ gṛheṣu remire siddhāḥ kṛṣṇa rāma gata jvarāḥ vīkṣantaḥ ahar ahar prītāḥ mukunda vadana ambujam nityam pramuditam śrīmat sa daya smita vīkṣaṇam saṅkarṣaṇaḥ ca rāja indra pariṣvajya idam ūcatuḥ pitar yuvābhyām snigdhābhyām poṣitau lālitau bhṛśam sa pitā sā ca jananī yau puṣṇītām sva putra vat śiśūn bandhubhiḥ utsṛṣṭān akalpaiḥ poṣa rakṣaṇe yāta yūyam vrajan tāta vayam ca sneha duḥkhitān jñātīn vaḥ draṣṭum eṣyāmaḥ vidhāya suhṛdām sukham vāsaḥ alaṅkāra kupya ādyaiḥ arhayām āsa sādaram purodhasā brāhmaṇaiḥ ca yathāvat dvija saṃskṛtim tebhyaḥ adāt dakṣiṇāḥ gāvaḥ rukma mālāḥ su alaṅkṛtāḥ su alaṅkṛtebhyaḥ sampūjya sa vatsāḥ kṣauma mālinīḥ yāḥ kṛṣṇa rāma janma ṛkṣe manaḥ dattā mahā matiḥ tāḥ ca adadāt anusmṛtya kaṃsena adharmataḥ hṛtāḥ gargāt yadu kula ācāryāt gāyatram vratam āsthitau na anya siddha amalam jñānam gūhamānau nara īhitaiḥ kāśyam sāndīpanim nāma hi avanti pura vāsinam tayoḥ dvija varaḥ tuṣṭaḥ śuddha bhāva anuvṛttibhiḥ provāca vedān akhilān saṅga upaniṣadaḥ guruḥ sa rahasyam dhanuḥ vedam dharmān nyāya pathān tathā tathā ca ānvīkṣikīm vidyām rāja nītim ca ṣaḍvidhām sakṛt nigada mātreṇa tau sañjagṛhatuḥ nṛpa ahar rātraiḥ catuḥṣaṣṭyā saṃyattau tāvatīḥ kalāḥ guru dakṣiṇayā ācāryam chandayām āsatuḥ nṛpa saṃlokṣya rājan ati mānusīm matim sammantrya patnyā sa mahā arṇave mṛtam bālam prabhāse babhūva ha velām upavrajya niṣīdatuḥ kṣanam tam āha bhagavān āśu guru putraḥ pradīyatām śrī samudraḥ uvāca na ca ahārṣam aham deva daityaḥ pañcajanaḥ mahān antar jala caraḥ kṛṣṇa śaṅkha rūpa dharaḥ asuraḥ āste tena āhṛtaḥ nūnam tat śrutvā sa tvaram prabhuḥ jalam āviśya tam hatvā na apaśyat udare arbhakam tad aṅga prabhavam śaṅkham ādāya ratham āgamat tatas saṃyamanīm nāma yamasya dayitām purīm gatvā janārdanaḥ śaṅkham pradadhmau sa halāyudhaḥ śaṅkha nirhrādam ākarṇya prajā saṃyamanaḥ yamaḥ tayoḥ saparyām mahatīm cakre bhakti upabṛṃhitām uvāca avanataḥ kṛṣṇam sarva bhūta āśaya ālayam līlā manuṣyayoḥ viṣṇo yuvayoḥ karavāma kim śrī bhagavān uvāca ānayasva mahā rāja mad śāsana puraskṛtaḥ dattvā sva gurave bhūyas vṛṇīṣva iti tam ūcatuḥ śrī guruḥ uvāca kaḥ nu yuṣmad vidha guroḥ kāmānām avaśiṣyate gacchatam sva gṛham vīrau kīrtiḥ vām astu pāvanī guruṇā evam anujñātau rathena anila raṃhasā samanandan prajāḥ sarvāḥ dṛṣṭvā rāma janārdanau śrī śukaḥ uvāca vṛṣṇīnām pravaraḥ mantrī kṛṣṇasya dayitaḥ sakhā śiṣyaḥ bṛhaspateḥ sākṣāt uddhavaḥ buddhi sattamaḥ tam āha bhagavān preṣṭham bhaktam ekāntinam kvacid gṛhītvā pāṇinā pāṇim prapanna ārti haraḥ hariḥ gopīnām mad viyoga ādhim mad sandeśaiḥ vimocaya tāḥ mad manaskāḥ tṛṣṭ prāṇāḥ mad arthe tyakta daihikāḥ mām eva dayitam preṣṭham ātmānam manasā gatāḥ mayi tāḥ preyasām preṣṭhe dūra sthe gokula striyaḥ dhārayanti ati kṛcchreṇa prāyas prāṇān kathañcana śrī śukaḥ uvāca iti uktaḥ uddhavaḥ rājan saṃdeśam bhartuḥ ādṛtaḥ channa yānaḥ praviśatām paśūnām khura reṇubhiḥ vāśitā arthe abhiyudhyadbhiḥ nāditam śuśmibhiḥ vṛṣaiḥ dhāvantībhiḥ ca vāsrābhiḥ udhas bhāraiḥ sva vatsakān go doha śabda abhiravam veṇūnām niḥsvanena ca gāyantībhiḥ ca karmāṇi śubhāni bala kṛṣṇayoḥ dhūpa dīpaiḥ ca mālyaiḥ ca gopa āvāsaiḥ manaḥ ramam haṃsa kāraṇḍava ākīrṇaiḥ padma ṣaṇḍaiḥ ca maṇḍitam tam āgatam samāgamya kṛṣṇasya anucaram priyam bhojitam parama annena saṃviṣṭam kaśipau sukham gata śramam paryapṛcchat pāda saṃvāhana ādibhiḥ kaccit aṅga mahā bhāga sakhā naḥ śūra nandanaḥ diṣṭyā kaṃsaḥ hataḥ pāpaḥ sa anugaḥ svena pāpmanā sādhūnām dharma śīlānām yadūnām dveṣṭi yaḥ sadā api smarati naḥ kṛṣṇaḥ mātaram suhṛdaḥ sakhīn gopān vrajam ca ātma nātham gāvaḥ vṛndāvanam girim api āyāsyati govindaḥ sva janān sakṛt īkṣitum dāva agneḥ vāta varṣāt ca vṛṣa sarpāt ca rakṣitāḥ duratyayebhyaḥ mṛtyubhyaḥ kṛṣṇena su mahātmanā smaratām kṛṣṇa vīryāṇi līlā apāṅga nirīkṣitam hasitam bhāṣitam ca aṅga sarvāḥ naḥ śithilāḥ kriyāḥ ākrīḍān īkṣyamāṇānām manaḥ yāti tad ātma tām manye kṛṣṇam ca rāmam ca prāptau iha sura uttamau surāṇām mahā arthāya gargasya vacanam yathā kaṃsam nāga ayuta prāṇam mallau gaja patim yathā avadhiṣṭām līlayā eva paśūn iva mṛgādhipaḥ tāla trayam mahā sāram dhanuḥ yaṣṭim iva ibha rāj pralambaḥ dhenukaḥ ariṣṭaḥ tṛṇāvartaḥ baka ādayaḥ daityāḥ sura asura jitaḥ hatāḥ yena iha līlayā śrī śukaḥ uvāca iti saṃsmṛtya saṃsmṛtya nandaḥ kṛṣṇa anurakta dhīḥ ati utkaṇṭhaḥ abhavat tūṣṇīm prema prasara vihvalaḥ yaśodā varṇyamānāni putrasya caritāni ca śṛṇvantī aśrūṇi avāsrākṣīt sneha snuta payodharā tayoḥ ittham bhagavati kṛṣṇe nanda yaśodayoḥ vīkṣya anurāgam paramam nandam āha uddhavaḥ mudā śrī uddhavaḥ uvāca yuvām ślāghyatamau nūnam dehinām iha māna da nārāyaṇe akhila gurau yat kṛtā matiḥ īdṛśī etau hi viśvasya ca bīja yonī rāmaḥ mukundaḥ puruṣaḥ pradhānam anvīya bhūteṣu vilakṣaṇasya jñānasya ca īśātaḥ imau purāṇau yasmin janaḥ prāṇa viyoga kāle kṣanam samāveśya manaḥ aviśuddham nirhṛtya karma āśayam āśu yāti parām gatim brahma mayaḥ arka varṇaḥ bhāvam vidhattām nitarām mahātman kim vā avaśiṣṭam yuvayoḥ su kṛtyam āgamiṣyati adīrgheṇa kālena vrajam acyutaḥ priyam vidhāsyate pitroḥ bhagavān sātvatām patiḥ hatvā kaṃsam raṅga madhye pratīpam sarva sātvatām yat āha vaḥ samāgatya kṛṣṇaḥ satyam karoti tat mā khidyatam mahā bhāgau drakṣyathaḥ kṛṣṇam antike na hi asya asti priyaḥ kaścid na apriyaḥ vā asti amāninaḥ na mātā na pitā tasya na bhāryā na suta ādayaḥ krīḍā artham saḥ api sādhūnām paritrāṇāya kalpate krīḍan atītaḥ api guṇaiḥ sṛjati avan hanti ajaḥ yathā bhramarikā dṛṣṭyā bhrāmyati iva mahīyate citte kartari tatra ātmā kartā iva aham dhiyā smṛtaḥ sarveṣām ātmajaḥ hi ātmā pitā mātā saḥ īśvaraḥ dṛṣṭam śrutam bhūta bhavat bhaviṣyat sthāsnuḥ cariṣṇuḥ mahat alpakam ca vinā acyutāt vastu tarām na vācyam saḥ eva sarvam paramātma bhūtaḥ evam niśā sā bruvatoḥ vyatītā nandasya kṛṣṇa anucarasya rājan tāḥ dīpa dīptaiḥ maṇibhiḥ virejuḥ rajjūḥ vikarṣat bhuja kaṅkaṇa srajaḥ calat nitamba stana hāra kuṇḍala tviṣat kapola aruṇa kuṅkuma ānanāḥ udgāyatīnām aravinda locanam vraja aṅganānām divam aspṛśat dhvaniḥ dṛṣṭvā ratham śātakaumbham kasya ayam iti ca bruvan akrūraḥ āgataḥ kim vā yaḥ kaṃsasya artha sādhakaḥ yena nītaḥ madhu purīm kṛṣṇaḥ kamala locanaḥ kim sādhayiṣyati asmābhiḥ bhartuḥ prītasya niṣkṛtim tatas strīṇām vadantīnām uddhavaḥ agāt kṛta āhnikaḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca tam vīkṣya kṛṣā anucaram vraja striyaḥ pīta ambaram puṣkara mālinam mukha aravindam parimṛṣṭa kuṇḍalam su vismitāḥ kaḥ ayam apīvya darśanaḥ kutas ca kasya acyuta veṣa bhūṣaṇaḥ tam uttamaḥ śloka pada ambuja āśrayam tam praśrayeṇa avanatāḥ su sat kṛtam sa vrīḍa hāsa īkṣaṇa sūnṛta ādibhiḥ rahasi apṛcchan upaviṣṭam āsane vijñāya saṃdeśa haram ramā pateḥ jānīmaḥ tvām yadu pateḥ pārṣadam samupāgatam pumbhiḥ strīṣu kṛtā yadvat sumanaḥsu iva ṣaṭpadaiḥ niḥsvam tyajanti gaṇikāḥ akalpam nṛpatim prajāḥ adhīta vidyāḥ ācāryam ṛtvijaḥ datta dakṣiṇam khagāḥ vīta phalam vṛkṣam bhuktvā ca atithayaḥ gṛham dagdham mṛgāḥ tathā araṇyam jārāḥ bhuktvā ratām striyam kṛṣṇa dūte samāyāte uddhave tyakta laukikāḥ gāyantyaḥ prīya karmāṇi rudantyaḥ ca gata hriyaḥ tasya saṃsmṛtya saṃsmṛtya yāni kaiśora bālyayoḥ kācid madhukaram dṛṣṭvā dhyāyantī kṛṣṇa saṅgamam madhupa kitava bandho mā spṛśa aṅghrim sapatnyāḥ kuca vilulita mālā kuṅkuma śmaśrubhiḥ naḥ vahatu madhu patiḥ tad māninīnām prasādam sakṛt adhara sudhām svām mohinīm pāyayitvā kim iha bahu ṣaṣ aṅghre gāyasi tvam yadūnām adhipatim a gṛhāṇām agratas naḥ purāṇam vijaya sakha sakhīnām gīyatām tad prasaṅgaḥ kṣapita kuca rujaḥ te kalpayanti iṣṭam iṣṭāḥ divi bhuvi ca rasāyām kāḥ striyaḥ tad durāpāḥ kapaṭa rucira hāsa bhrū vijṛmbhasya yāḥ syuḥ api ca kṛpaṇa pakṣe hi uttamaḥ śloka śabdaḥ visṛja śirasi pādam vedmi aham cātu kāraiḥ sva kṛte iha viṣṛṣṭā apatya pati anya lokā striyam akṛta virūpām strī jitaḥ kāma yānām balim api balim attvā veṣṭayat dhvāṅkṣa vat yaḥ yad anucarita līlā karṇa pīyūṣa vipruṣ sakṛt adana vidhūta dvandva dharmāḥ vinaṣṭāḥ sapadi gṛha kuṭumbam dīnam utsṛjya dīnā vayam ṛtam iva jihma vyāhṛtam śraddadhānāḥ kulika rutam iva ājñāḥ kṛṣṇa vadhvaḥ hariṇyaḥ priya sakha punar āgāḥ preyasā preṣitaḥ kim satatam urasi saumya śrīḥ vadhūḥ sākam āste smarati sa pitṛ gehān saumya bandhūn ca gopān kvacid api sa kathā naḥ kiṅkarīṇām gṛṇīte śrī śukaḥ uvāca atha uddhavaḥ niśamya evam kṛṣṇa darśana lālasāḥ śrī uddhavaḥ uvāca aho yūyam sma pūrṇa arthāḥ bhavatyaḥ loka pūjitāḥ śreyobhiḥ vividhaiḥ ca anyaiḥ kṛṣṇe bhaktiḥ hi sādhyate bhaktiḥ pravartitā diṣṭyā munīnām api durlabhā diṣṭyā putrān patīn dehān sva janān bhavanāni ca yūyam yat kṛṣṇa ākhyam puruṣam param sarva ātma bhāvaḥ adhikṛtaḥ bhavatīnām adhokṣaje viraheṇa mahā bhāgā mahān me anugrahaḥ kṛtaḥ śrūyatām priya sandeśaḥ bhavatīnām sukha āvahaḥ yam ādāya āgataḥ bhadrā aham bhartuḥ rahaḥ karaḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca yathā bhūtāni bhūteṣu kham vāyu agniḥ jalam mahī tathā aham ca manaḥ prāṇa bhūta indriya guṇa āśrayaḥ ātmani eva ātmanā ātmānam sṛje hanmi anupālaye ātma māyā anubhāvena bhūta indriya guṇa ātmanā ātmā jñāna mayaḥ śuddhaḥ vyatiriktaḥ aguṇa anvayaḥ yena indriya arthān dhyāyeta mṛṣā svapna vat utthitaḥ etad antaḥ samāmnāyaḥ yogaḥ sāṅkhyam manīṣiṇām tyāgaḥ tapaḥ damaḥ satyam samudra antāḥ iva āpagāḥ yat tu aham bhavatīnām vai dūre varte priyaḥ dṛśām manasaḥ sannikarṣa artham mad anudhyāna kāmyayā yathā dūra care preṣṭhe manaḥ āviśya vartate strīṇām ca na tathā cetaḥ sannikṛṣṭe akṣi gocare mayi āveśya manaḥ kṛtsnam vimukta aśeṣa vṛtti yat yāḥ mayā krīḍatā rātryām vane asmin vraje āsthitāḥ alabdha rāsāḥ kalyāṇyaḥ mā āpuḥ mad vīrya cintayā śrī śukaḥ uvāca evam priyatama ādiṣṭam ākarṇya vraja yoṣitaḥ tāḥ ūcuḥ uddhavam prītāḥ tad saṃdeśa āgata smṛtīḥ gopyaḥ ūcuḥ diṣṭyā āhitaḥ hataḥ kaṃsaḥ yadūnām sa anugaḥ agha kṛt diṣṭi āptaiḥ labdha sarva arthaiḥ kuśalī āste acyutaḥ adhunā prītim naḥ snigdha sa vrīḍa hāsa udāra īkṣaṇa arcitaḥ katham rati viśeṣa jñaḥ priyaḥ ca pura yoṣitām goṣṭhi madhye pura strīṇām grāmyāḥ svaira kathā antare tāḥ kim niśāḥ smarati yāsu tadā priyābhiḥ vṛndāvane kumuda kunda śaśāṅka ramye reme kvaṇat caraṇa nūpura rāsa goṣṭhyām asmābhiḥ īḍita manojña kathaḥ kadācid api eṣyati iha dāśārhaḥ taptāḥ sva kṛtayā śucā kasmāt kṛṣṇaḥ iha āyāti prāpta rājyaḥ hata ahitaḥ narendra kanyāḥ udvāhya prītaḥ sarva suhṛd vṛtaḥ śrī pateḥ āpta kāmasya kriyeta arthaḥ kṛtātmanaḥ param saukhyam hi nairāśyam svairiṇī api āha piṅgalā tat jānatīnām naḥ kṛṣṇe tathā api āśā duratyayā saṅkarṣaṇa sahāyena kṛṣṇena ācaritāḥ prabho gatyā lalitayā udāra hāsa līlā avalokanaiḥ mādhvyā girā hṛta dhiyaḥ katham tam vismarāma he he nātha he ramā nātha vraja nātha ārti nāśana śrī śukaḥ uvāca tatas tāḥ kṛṣṇa sandeśaiḥ vyapeta viraha jvarāḥ uddhavam jñātvā ātmānam adhokṣajam uvāsa katicid māsān gopīnām vinudan śucaḥ kṛṣṇa līlā kathām gāyan ramayām āsa gokulam vrajaukasām kṣaṇa prāyāṇi āsan kṛṣṇasya vārtayā sarit vana giri droṇīḥ vīkṣan kusumitān drumān kṛṣṇam saṃsmārayan reme hari dāsaḥ vrajaukasām dṛṣṭvā evam ādi gopīnām kṛṣṇa āveśa ātma viklavam govinde eva nikhila ātmani rūḍha bhāvāḥ kva imāḥ striyaḥ vana carīḥ vyabhicāra duṣṭāḥ kṛṣṇe kva ca eṣa paramātmani rūḍha bhāvaḥ nanu īśvaraḥ anubhajataḥ aviduṣaḥ api sākṣāt na ayam śriyaḥ aṅge nitānta rateḥ prasādaḥ svar yoṣitām nalina gandha rucām kutas anyāḥ rāsa utsave asya bhuja daṇḍa gṛhīta kaṇṭha labdha āśiṣām yaḥ udagāt vraja vallabhīnām āsām aho caraṇa reṇu juṣām aham syām vṛndāvane kim api gulma latā oṣadhīnām yāḥ vai śriyā arcitam aja ādibhiḥ āpta kāmaiḥ yoga īśvaraiḥ api yat ātmani rāsa goṣṭhyām kṛṣṇasya tat bhagavataḥ caraṇa aravindam vande nanda vraja strīṇām pāda reṇum abhīkṣṇaśas yāsām hari kathā udgītam punāti bhuvana trayam śrī śukaḥ uvāca atha gopīḥ anujñāpya yaśodām nandam eva ca gopān āmantrya dāśārhaḥ yāsyan āruruhe ratham tam nirgatam samāsādya nānā upāyana pāṇayaḥ nanda ādayaḥ anurāgeṇa prāvocan aśru locanāḥ manasaḥ vṛttayaḥ naḥ syuḥ kṛṣṇa pāda ambuja āśrayāḥ vācaḥ abhidhāyinīḥ nāmnām kāyaḥ tad prahvaṇa ādiṣu karmabhiḥ bhrāmyamāṇānām yatra kvāpi īśvara icchayā maṅgala ācaritaiḥ dānaiḥ ratiḥ naḥ kṛṣṇe īśvare evam sabhājitaḥ gopaiḥ kṛṣṇa bhaktyā narādhipa uddhavaḥ punar āgacchat mathurām kṛṣṇa pālitām kṛṣṇāya bhakti udrekam vrajaukasām vasudevāya rāmāya rājñe ca upāyanāni adāt śrī śukaḥ uvāca atha vijñāya bhagavān sarva ātmā sarva darśanaḥ sairandhryāḥ kāma taptāyāḥ priyam icchan gṛham yayau mahārha upaskaraiḥ āḍhyam kāma upāya upabṛṃhitam muktā dāma patākābhiḥ vitāna śayana āsanaiḥ gṛham tam āyāntam avekṣya sā āsanāt sadyas samutthāya hi jāta sambhramā yathā upasaṅgamya sakhībhiḥ acyutam sabhājayām āsa sat āsana ādibhiḥ tathā uddhavaḥ sādhu tayā abhipūjitaḥ nyaṣīdat urvyām abhimṛśya ca āsanam kṛṣṇaḥ api tūrṇam śayanam mahā dhanam viveśa loka ācaritāni anuvrataḥ sā majjana ālepa dukūla bhūṣaṇa sraj gandha tāmbūla sudhā āsava ādibhiḥ prasādhita ātmā upasasāra mādhavam sa vrīḍa līlā utsmita vibhrama īkṣitaiḥ āhūya kāntām nava saṅgama hriyā viśaṅkitām kaṅkaṇa bhūṣite kare pragṛhya śayyām adhiveśya rāmayā reme anulepa arpaṇa puṇya leśayā ānanda mūrtim ajahāt ati dīrgha tāpam sā evam kaivalya nātham tam prāpya duṣprāpyam īśvaram aṅga rāga arpaṇena aho durbhagā idam ayācata saha uṣyatām iha preṣṭha dināni katicid mayā tasyai kāma varam dattvā mānayitvā ca māna daḥ durārdhyam samārādhya viṣṇum sarva īśvara īśvaram yaḥ vṛṇīte manaḥ grāhyam asattvāt kumanīṣī asau akrūra bhavanam kṛṣṇaḥ saha rāma uddhavaḥ prabhuḥ kiñcid cikīrṣayan prāgāt akrūra prīya kāmyayā sa tān nara vara śreṣṭhān ārāt vīkṣya sva bāndhavān nanāma kṛṣṇam rāmam ca sa taiḥ api abhivāditaḥ pūjayām āsa vidhi vat kṛta āsana parigrahān pāda avanejanīḥ āpaḥ dhārayan śirasā nṛpa arcitvā śirasā ānamya pādau aṅka gatau mṛjan praśraya avanataḥ akrūraḥ kṛṣṇa rāmau abhāṣata diṣṭyā pāpaḥ hataḥ kaṃsaḥ sa anugaḥ vām idam kulam ātma sṛṣṭam idam viśvam anvāviśya sva śaktibhiḥ yathā hi bhūteṣu carācareṣu mahī ādayaḥ yoniṣu bhānti nānā evam bhavān kevalaḥ ātma yoniṣu ātmā ātma tantraḥ bahudhā vibhāti deha ādi upādheḥ anirūpita tvāt bhavaḥ na sākṣāt na bhidā ātmanaḥ syāt tvayā uditaḥ ayam jagataḥ hitāya yadā yadā veda pathaḥ purāṇaḥ bādhyeta pāṣaṇḍa pathaiḥ asadbhiḥ tadā bhavān sattva guṇam bibharti sva aṃśena bhāram apanetum iha asi bhūmeḥ akṣauhiṇī śata vadhena suretara aṃśa rājñām amuṣya ca kulasya yaśaḥ vitanvan adya īśa naḥ vasatayaḥ khalu bhūri bhāgā yaḥ sarva deva pitṛ bhūta nṛ deva mūrtiḥ sa tvam jagat guruḥ adhokṣaja yāḥ praviṣṭaḥ kaḥ paṇḍitaḥ tvat aparam śaraṇam samīyāt bhakta priyāt ṛta giraḥ suhṛdaḥ kṛta jñāt sarvān dadāti suhṛdaḥ bhajataḥ abhikāmān diṣṭyā janārdana bhavān iha naḥ pratīto yoga īśvaraiḥ api durāpa gatiḥ sura īśaiḥ deha ādi moha raśanām bhavadīya māyām śrī bhagavān uvāca tvam naḥ guruḥ pitṛvyaḥ ca ślāghyaḥ bandhuḥ ca nityadā vayam tu rakṣyāḥ poṣyāḥ ca anukampyāḥ prajāḥ hi vaḥ bhavad-vidhāḥ mahābhāgāḥ niṣevyāḥ arha sattamāḥ śreyaḥ kāmaiḥ nṛbhiḥ nityam devāḥ sva arthāḥ na sādhavaḥ na hi am mayāni tīrthāni na devāḥ mṛd śilā mayāḥ sa bhavān suhṛdām vai naḥ śreyān śreyaḥ cikīrṣayā jijñāsā artham pāṇḍavānām gacchasva tvam gajāhvayam pitari uparate bālāḥ saha mātrā su duḥkhitāḥ ānītāḥ sva puram rājñā vasante iti śuśruma teṣu rājā ambikā putraḥ bhrātṛ putreṣu dīna dhīḥ gaccha jānīhi tad vṛttam adhunā sādhu asādhu vā vijñāya tat vidhāsyāmaḥ yathā śam suhṛdām bhavet iti akrūram samādiśya bhagavant hariḥ īśvaraḥ saṅkarṣaṇa uddhavābhyām vai tatas sva bhavanam yayau śrī śukaḥ uvāca dadarśa tatra ambikeyam sa bhīṣmam viduram pṛthām saha putram ca vāhlīkam bhāradvājam sa gautamam karnam suyodhanam drauṇim pāṇḍavān suhṛdaḥ aparān sampṛṣṭaḥ taiḥ suhṛd vārttām svayam ca apṛcchat avyayam uvāsa katicid māsān rājñaḥ vṛtta vivitsayā tejaḥ ojaḥ balam vīryam praśraya ādīn ca sat guṇān prajā anurāgam pārtheṣu na sahadbhiḥ cikīṛṣitam kṛtam ca dhārtarāṣṭraiḥ yat gara dāna ādi apeśalam pṛthā tu bhrātaram prāptam akrūram upasṛtya tam uvāca janma nilayam smarantī aśru kala īkṣaṇā bhrātreyaḥ bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ śaraṇyaḥ bhakta vatsalaḥ smarati rāmaḥ ca amburuha īkṣaṇaḥ sapatna madhye śocantīm vṛkānām hariṇīm iva sāntvayiṣyati mām vākyaiḥ pitṛ hīnān ca bālakān kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa mahā yogin viśvātman viśva bhāvana prapannām pāhi govinda śiśubhiḥ ca avasīdatīm na anyat tava pada ambhojāt paśyāmi śaraṇam nṛṇām bibhyatām mṛtyu saṃsārāt īsvarasya āpavargikāt namaḥ kṛṣṇāya śuddhāya brahmaṇe paramātmane yogeśvarāya yogāya tvām aham śaraṇam gatā śrī śukaḥ uvāca iti anusmṛtya sva janam kṛṣṇam ca jagat īśvaram prārudat duḥkhitā rājan bhavatām prapitāmahī sama duḥkha sukhaḥ akrūraḥ viduraḥ ca mahā yaśāḥ sāntvayām āsatuḥ kuntīm tad putra utpatti hetubhiḥ yāsyan rājānam abhyetya viṣamam putra lālasam akrūraḥ uvāca bho bho vaicitravīrya tvam kurūṇām kīrti vardhana bhrātari uparate pāṇḍau adhunā āsanam āsthitaḥ dharmeṇa pālayan urvīm prajāḥ śīlena rañjayan vartamānaḥ samaḥ sveṣu śreyaḥ kīrtim avāpsyasi tasmāt samatve vartasva pāṇḍaveṣu ātmajeṣu ca rājan svena api dehena kim jāyā ātmaja ādibhiḥ sambhojanīya apadeśaiḥ jalāni iva jalaukasaḥ puṣṇāti yān adharmeṇa sva buddhyā tam apaṇḍitam te akṛtārtham prahiṇvanti prāṇāḥ rāyaḥ suta ādayaḥ vīkṣya āyamya ātmanā ātmānam samaḥ śāntaḥ bhava prabho dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca yathā vadati kalyāṇīm vācam dāna pate bhavān tathā anayā na tṛpyāmi martyaḥ prāpya yathā amṛtam tathā api sūnṛtā saumya hṛdi na sthīyate cale putra anurāga viṣame vidyut saudāmanī yathā bhūmeḥ bhāra avatārāya yaḥ avatīrṇaḥ yadoḥ kule sṛṣṭvā guṇān vibhajate tad anupraviṣṭaḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca suhṛdbhiḥ samanujñātaḥ punar yadu purīm agāt śaśaṃsa rāma kṛṣṇābhyām dhṛtarāṣṭra viceṣṭitam śrī śukaḥ uvāca mṛte bhartari duḥkha ārte īyatuḥ sma pituḥ gṛhān sa tat apriyam ākarṇya śoka amarṣa yutaḥ nṛpa ayādavīm mahīm kartum cakre paramam udyamam akṣauhiṇībhiḥ viṃśatyā tisṛbhiḥ ca api saṃvṛtaḥ yadu rājadhānīm mathurām nyarudhat sarvatas diśam nirīkṣya tad balam kṛṣṇaḥ udvelam iva sāgaram cintayām āsa bhagavant hariḥ kāraṇa mānuṣaḥ tad deśa kāla anuguṇam sva avatāra prayojanam haniṣyāmi balam hi etat bhuvi bhāram samāhitam māgadhena samānītam vaśyānām sarva bhūbhujām akṣauhiṇībhiḥ saṅkhyātam bhaṭa aśva ratha kuñjaraiḥ etad arthaḥ avatāraḥ ayam bhū bhāra haraṇāya me saṃrakṣaṇāya sādhūnām kṛtaḥ anyeṣām vadhāya ca evam dhyāyati govindaḥ ākāśāt sūrya varcasau āyudhāni ca divyāni purāṇāni yadṛcchayā dṛṣṭvā tāni hṛṣīkeśaḥ saṅkarṣaṇam atha abravīt paśya ārya vyasanam prāptam yadūnām tvāvatām prabho eṣa te rathaḥ āyātaḥ dayitāni āyudhāni ca etad artham hi nau janma sādhūnām īśa śarma kṛt trayoviṃśati anīka ākhyam bhūmeḥ bhāram apākuru evam sammantrya dāśārhau daṃśitau rathinau purāt nirjagmatuḥ sva āyudha āḍhyau balena alpīyasā vṛtau tatas abhūt para sainyānām hṛdi vitrāsa vepathuḥ tau āha māgadhaḥ vīkṣya he kṛṣṇa puruṣa adhama hitvā vā mat śaraiḥ chinnam deham svar yāhi mām jahi śrī bhagavān uvāca na gṛhṇīmaḥ vacaḥ rājan āturasya mumūrṣataḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca sa sainya yāna dhvaja vāji sārathī sūrya analau vāyuḥ iva abhra reṇubhiḥ striyaḥ pura aṭṭālaka harmya gopuram samāśritāḥ sammumuhuḥ śucā arditaḥ hariḥ para anīka payomucām muhur śilīmukha ati ulbaṇa varṣa pīḍitam gṛhṇan niśaṅgāt atha sandadhat śarān vikṛṣya muñcan śita bāṇa pūgān nirbhinna kumbhāḥ kariṇaḥ nipetuḥ anekaśas aśvāḥ śara vṛkṇa kandharāḥ rathāḥ hata aśva dhvaja sūta nāyakāḥ padāyataḥ chinna bhuja ūru kandharāḥ sañchidyamāna dvipada ibha vājinām aṅga prasūtāḥ śataśas asṛj āpagāḥ bhuja ahayaḥ pūruṣa śīrṣa kacchapāḥ hata dvipa dvīpa haya graha ākulāḥ kara ūru mīnāḥ nara keśa śaivalāḥ dhanuḥ taraṅga āyudha gulma saṅkulāḥ acchūrikā āvarta bhayānakāḥ mahā maṇi praveka ābharaṇa aśma śarkarāḥ pravartitāḥ bhīru bhaya āvahāḥ mṛdhe manasvinām harṣa karīḥ parasparam vinighnatā arīn musalena durmadān saṅkarṣaṇena aparīmeya tejasā kṣayam praṇītam vasudeva putrayoḥ vikrīḍitam tat jagat īśayoḥ param samīhite ananta guṇaḥ sva līlayā jagrāha viratham rāmaḥ jarāsandham mahā balam hata anīka avaśiṣṭa asum siṃhaḥ siṃham iva ojasā badhyamānam hata arātim pāśaiḥ vāruṇa mānuṣaiḥ vārayām āsa govindaḥ tena kārya cikīrṣayā sā muktaḥ loka nāthābhyām vrīḍitaḥ vīra sammataḥ tapase kṛta saṅkalpaḥ vāritaḥ pathi rājabhiḥ hateṣu sarva anīkeṣu nṛpaḥ bārhadrathaḥ tadā mukundaḥ api akṣata balaḥ nistīrṇa ari bala arṇavaḥ vikīryamāṇaḥ kusumaiḥ trīdaśaiḥ anumoditaḥ upagīyamāna vijayaḥ sūta māgadha vandibhiḥ śaṅkha dundubhayaḥ neduḥ bherī tūryāṇi anekaśas vīṇā veṇu mṛdaṅgāni puram praviśati prabhau sikta mārgām hṛṣṭa janām patākābhiḥ abhyalaṅkṛtām nirghuṣṭām brahma ghoṣeṇa kautuka ābaddha toraṇām nicīyamānaḥ nārībhiḥ mālya dadhi akṣata aṅkuraiḥ nirīkṣyamāṇaḥ sa sneham prīti utkalita locanaiḥ āyodhana gatam vittam anantam vīra bhūṣaṇam yadu rājāya tat sarvam āhṛtam prādiśat prabhuḥ evam saptadaśa kṛtvas tāvatī akṣauhiṇī balaḥ yuyudhe māgadhaḥ rājā yadubhiḥ kṛṣṇa pālitaiḥ akṣiṇvan tad balam sarvam vṛṣṇayaḥ kṛṣṇa tejasā hateṣu sveṣu anīkeṣu tyaktaḥ agāt aribhiḥ nṛpaḥ aṣṭādaśama saṅgrāma āgāmini tad antarā nārada preṣitaḥ vīraḥ yavanaḥ pratyadṛśyata nṛ loke ca apratidvandvaḥ vṛṣṇīn śrutvā ātma sammitān tam dṛṣṭvā acintayat kṛṣṇaḥ saṅkarṣaṇa sahāyavān aho yadūnām vṛjinam prāptam hi ubhayatas mahat māgadhaḥ api adya vā śvas vā paraśvas vā āgamiṣyati āvayoḥ yudhyatoḥ asya yadi āgantā jarā sutaḥ tatra jñātīn samādhāya yavanam ghātayāmahe dṛśyate yatra hi tvāṣṭram vijñānam śilpa naipuṇam hema śṛṅgaiḥ divi spṛgbhiḥ sphaṭika aṭṭāla gopuraiḥ rājata ārakuṭaiḥ koṣṭhaiḥ hema kumbhaiḥ alaṅkṛtaiḥ vāstoṣpatīnām ca gṛhaiḥ vallabhībhiḥ ca nirmitam cātur varṇya jana ākīrṇam yadu deva gṛha ullasat sudharmām pārijātam ca mahā indraḥ prāhiṇot hareḥ śyāma eka varṇān varuṇaḥ hayān śuklān manaḥ javān aṣṭau nidhi patiḥ kośān loka pālaḥ nija udayān prajā pālena rāmeṇa kṛṣṇaḥ samanumantritaḥ nirjagāma pura dvārāt padma mālī nirāyudhaḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca darśanīyatamam śyāmam pīta kauśeya vāsasam pṛthu dīrgha catur bāhum nava kañja aruṇa īkṣaṇam mukha aravindam bibhrāṇam sphurat makara kuṇḍalam vāsudevaḥ hi ayam iti pumān śrīvatsa lāñchanaḥ anvadhāvat jighṛkṣuḥ tam durāpam api yoginām hasta prāptam iva ātmānam harīṇā sa pade pade nītaḥ darśayatā dūram yavana īśaḥ adri kandaram iti kṣipan anugataḥ na enam prāpa ahata aśubhaḥ saḥ api praviṣṭaḥ tatra anyam śayānam dadṛśe naram nanu asau dūram ānīya śete mām iha sādhu vat iti matvā acyutam mūḍhaḥ tam padā samatāḍayat diśaḥ vilokayan pārśve tam adrākṣīt avasthitam sa tāvat tasya ruṣṭasya dṛṣṭi pātena bhārata śrī rājā uvāca kasmāt guhām gataḥ śiṣye kiṃtejaḥ yavana ardanaḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca saḥ ikṣvāku kule jātaḥ māndhātṛ tanayaḥ mahān sa yācitaḥ sura gaṇaiḥ indra ādyaiḥ ātma rakṣaṇe rājan viramatām kṛcchrāt bhavān naḥ paripālanāt asmān pālayataḥ vīra kāmāḥ te sarve ujjhitāḥ sutāḥ mahiṣyaḥ bhavataḥ jñātayaḥ amātya mantrinaḥ prajāḥ ca tulya kālīnāḥ na adhunā santi kālitāḥ kālaḥ balīyān balinām bhagavān īśvaraḥ avyayaḥ prajāḥ kālayate krīḍan paśu pālaḥ yathā paśūn varam vṛṇīṣva bhadram te ṛte kaivalyam adya naḥ evam uktaḥ sa vai devān abhivandya mahā yaśāḥ aśayiṣṭa guhā viṣṭaḥ nidrayā deva dattayā ātmānam darśayām āsa mucukundāya dhīmate tam ālokya ghana śyāmam pīta kauśeya vāsasam catur bhujam rocamānam vaijayantyā ca mālayā prekṣaṇīyam nṛ lokasya sa anurāga smita īkṣaṇam śaṅkitaḥ śanakais rājā durdharṣam iva tejasā śrī mucukundaḥ uvāca padbhyām padma palāśābhyām vicarasi uru kaṇṭake kim svid tejasvinām tejaḥ bhagavān vā vibhāvasuḥ manye tvām deva devānām trayāṇām puruṣa ṛṣabham yat bādhase guhā dhvāntam pradīpaḥ prabhayā yathā śuśrūṣatām avyalīkam asmākam nara puṅgava vayam tu puruṣa vyāghra aikṣvākāḥ kṣatra bandhavaḥ śaye asmin vijane kāmam kena api utthāpitaḥ adhunā saḥ api bhasmīkṛtaḥ nūnam ātmīyena eva pāpmanā anantaram bhavān śrīmān lakṣitaḥ amitra śāsanaḥ tejasā te aviṣahyeṇa bhūri draṣṭum na śaknumaḥ hata ojasā mahā bhāga mānanīyaḥ asi dehinām evam sambhāṣitaḥ rājñā bhagavān bhūta bhāvanaḥ pratyāha prahasan vāṇyā megha nāda gabhīrayā śrī bhagavān uvāca janma karma abhidhānāni santi me aṅga sahasraśas tathā api adyatanāni aṅga śṛnuṣva gadataḥ mama bhūmeḥ bhārāyamāṇānām asurāṇām kṣayāya ca kālanemiḥ hataḥ kaṃsaḥ pralamba ādyāḥ ca sat dviṣaḥ ayam ca yavanaḥ dagdhaḥ rājan te tigma cakṣuṣā saḥ aham tava anugraha artham guhām etām upāgataḥ prārthitaḥ pracuram pūrvam tvayā aham bhakta vatsalaḥ varān vṛṇīṣva rājarṣe sarvān kāmān dadāmi te śrī śukaḥ uvāca jñātvā nārāyaṇam devam garga vākyam anusmaran śrī mucukundaḥ uvāca vimohitaḥ ayam janaḥ īśa māyayā tvadīyayā tvām na bhajati anartha dṛś sukhāya duḥkha prabhaveṣu sajjate gṛheṣu yoṣit puruṣaḥ ca vañcitaḥ gṛha andha kūpe patitaḥ yathā paśuḥ martya ātma buddheḥ suta dāra kośa bhūṣu āsajjamānasya duranta cintayā vṛtaḥ ratha ibha aśva padāti anīkapaiḥ gām paryaṭan tu āgaṇayan su durmadaḥ mataṃgajaiḥ vā nara deva saṃjñitaḥ kalevaraḥ viṣ kṛmi bhasma saṃjñitaḥ gṛheṣu maithunya sukheṣu yoṣitām krīḍā mṛgaḥ pūruṣaḥ īśa nīyate punar ca bhūyāsam aham sva rāj iti pravṛddha tarṣaḥ na sukhāya kalpate manye mama anugrahaḥ īśa te kṛtaḥ rājya anubandha apagamaḥ yadṛcchayā yaḥ prārthyate sādhubhiḥ eka caryayā vanam vivikṣadbhiḥ akhaṇḍa bhūmi paiḥ ārādhya kaḥ tvām hi apavarga dam hare vṛṇīte āryaḥ varam ātma bandhanam tasmāt visṛjya āśiṣaḥ īśa sarvatas rajaḥ tamaḥ sattva guṇa anubandhanāḥ nirañjanam nirguṇam advayam param tvām jñāpti mātram puruṣam vrajāmi aham a vitṛṣa ṣaṣ amitraḥ alabdha śāntiḥ kathañcid abhayam ṛtam aśokam pāhi mā āpannam īśa śrī bhagavān uvāca na
