dhīḥ ekānta bhaktānām āśīrbhiḥ bhidyate kvacid yuñjānānām abhaktānām prāṇāyāma ādibhiḥ manaḥ akṣīṇa vāsanam rājan dṛśyate punar utthitam vicarasva mahīm kāmam mayi āveśita mānasaḥ kṣātra dharma sthitaḥ jantūn nyavadhīḥ mṛgayā ādibhiḥ samāhitaḥ tat tapasā jahi agham mad upāśritaḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca ittham saḥ nandanaḥ saṃvīkṣya kṣullakān martyān paśūn vīrudh vanaspatīn matvā kali yugam prāptam jagāma diśam uttarām tapaḥ śraddhā yutaḥ dhīraḥ niḥsaṅgaḥ mukta saṃśayaḥ samādhāya manaḥ kṛṣṇe prāviśat gandhamādanam badarī āśramam āsādya nara nārāyaṇa ālayam bhagavān punar āvrajya purīm yavana veṣṭitām hatvā mleccha balam ninye tadīyam dvārakām dhanam nīyamāne dhane gobhiḥ nṛbhiḥ ca acyuta coditaiḥ ājagāma jarāsandhaḥ trayoviṃśati anīka paḥ padbhyām palāśābhyām celatuḥ bahu yojanam palāyamānau tau dṛṣṭvā māgadhaḥ prahasan balī anvadhāvat ratha anīkaiḥ īśayoḥ apramāṇa vid pradrutya dūram saṃśrāntau tuṅgam āruhatām girim pravarṣaṇa ākhyam bhagavān nityadā yatra varṣati girau nilīnau ājñāya na adhigamya padam nṛpa alakṣyamāṇau ripuṇā sa anugena yadu uttamau sva puram punar āyātau samudra parikhām nṛpa saḥ api dagdhau iti mṛṣā manvānaḥ bala keśavau ānarta adhipatiḥ śrīmān raivataḥ raivatīm sutām brahmaṇā coditaḥ prādāt balāya iti purā uditam vaidarbhīm bhīṣmaka sutām śriyaḥ mātrām svayaṃvare pramathya tarasā rājñaḥ śālva ādīn caidya pakṣa gān paśyatām sarva lokānām tārkṣya putraḥ sudhām iva śrī rājā uvāca bhagavān bhīṣmaka sutām rukmiṇīm rucira ānanām bhagavan śrotum icchāmi kṛṣṇasya amita tejasaḥ yathā māgadha śālva ādīn jitvā kanyām upāharat brahman kṛṣṇa kathāḥ puṇyāḥ mādhvīḥ loka mala apahāḥ kaḥ nu tṛpyeta śṛṇvānaḥ śruta jñaḥ nitya nūtanāḥ śrī bādarāyaṇiḥ uvāca rājā āsīt bhīṣmakaḥ nāma vidarbha adhipatiḥ mahān tasya panca abhavan putrāḥ kanyā ekā ca varānanā rukma keśaḥ rukma mālī rukmiṇī eṣā svasā satī sā upaśrutya mukundasya rūpa vīrya guṇa śriyaḥ gṛha āgataiḥ gīyamānāḥ tam mene sadṛśam patim tām buddhi lakṣaṇa audārya rūpa śīla guṇa āśrayām kṛṣṇaḥ ca sadṛśīm bhāryām samudvoḍhum manaḥ dadhe bandhūnām icchatām dātum kṛṣṇāya bhaginīm nṛpa tatas nivārya kṛṣṇa dviṣ rukmī caidyam amanyata tat avetya asita apāṅgā vaidarbhī durmanāḥ bhṛśam vicintya āptam dvijam kañcid kṛṣṇāya prāhiṇot drutam dvārakām sa samabhyetya pratīhāraiḥ praveśitaḥ apaśyat ādyam puruṣam āsīnam kāñcana āsane dṛṣṭvā brahmaṇya devaḥ tam avaruhya nija āsanāt upaveśya arhayām cakre yathā ātmānam divaukasaḥ tam bhuktavantam viśrāntam upagamya satām gatiḥ pāṇinā abhimṛśan pādau avyagraḥ tam apṛcchata vartate na ati kṛcchreṇa santuṣṭa manasaḥ sadā a santuṣṭaḥ asakṛt lokān āpnoti api sureśvaraḥ akiñcanaḥ api santuṣṭaḥ śete sarva aṅga vijvaraḥ viprān sva lābha santuṣṭān sādhūn bhūta suhṛttamān nirahaṅkāriṇaḥ śāntān namasye śirasā asakṛt sukham vasanti viṣaye pālyamānāḥ sa me priyaḥ sarvam naḥ brūhi a guhyam ced kim kāryam karavāma te evam sampṛṣṭa sampraśnaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinā śrī rukmiṇī uvāca śrutvā guṇān bhuvana sundara śṛṇvatām te rūpam dṛśām dṛśimatām akhila artha lābham kā tvā mukunda mahatī kula śīla rūpa dhīrā patim kulavatī na vṛṇīta kanyā tat me bhavān khalu vṛtaḥ patiḥ aṅga jāyām mā vīra bhāgam abhimarśatu caidyaḥ ārāt ārādhitaḥ yadi gadāgrajaḥ etya pāṇim gṛhṇātu me na damaghoṣa suta ādayaḥ anye guptaḥ sametya pṛtanā patibhiḥ parītaḥ mām rākṣasena vidhinā udvaha vīrya śulkām yasya aṅghri paṅkaja rajaḥ snapanam jahyām asūn vrata kṛśān śata janmabhiḥ syāt brāhmaṇaḥ uvāca iti ete guhya sandeśāḥ yadu deva mayā āhṛtāḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca pragṛhya pāṇinā pāṇim prahasan idam abravīt śrī bhagavān uvāca veda aham rukmiṇā dveṣāt mama udvāhaḥ nivāritaḥ tām ānayiṣye unmathya rājanya apasadān mṛdhe mad parām anavadya aṅgīm edhasaḥ agni śikhām iva śrī śukaḥ uvāca udvāha ṛkṣam ca vijñāya rukmiṇyāḥ madhusūdanaḥ rathaḥ saṃyujyatām āśu dāruka iti āha sārathim sa ca aśvaiḥ śaibya sugrīva meghapuṣpa balāhakaiḥ āruhya syandanam śauriḥ dvijam āropya tūrṇa gaiḥ ānartāt eka rātreṇa vidarbhān agamat hayaiḥ rājā sa kuṇḍina patiḥ putra sneha vaśa anugaḥ śiśupālāya svām kanyām dāsyan karmāṇi akārayat puram sammṛṣṭa saṃsikta mārga rathyā catuṣpatham juṣṭam strī puruṣaiḥ śrīmat gṛhaiḥ aguru dhūpitaiḥ bhojayitvā yathā nyāyam vācayām āsa maṅgalam su snātām su datīm kanyām kṛta kautuka maṅgalām āhata aṃśuka yugmena bhūṣitām bhūṣaṇa uttamaiḥ cakruḥ sāma ṛc yajuḥ mantraiḥ vadhvaḥ rakṣām dvijottamāḥ vāsāṃsi tilān ca guḍa miśritān prādāt dhenūḥ ca viprebhyaḥ rājā vidhi vidām varaḥ evam cedi patiḥ rājā damaghoṣaḥ sutāya vai patti aśva saṅkulaiḥ sainyaiḥ parītaḥ kuṇdīnam yayau niveśayām āsa mudā kalpita anya niveśane ājagmuḥ caidya pakṣīyāḥ pauṇḍraka ādyāḥ sahasraśas kṛṣṇa rāma dviṣaḥ yattāḥ kanyām caidyāya sādhitum yadi āgatya haret kṛṣnaḥ rāma ādyaiḥ yadubhiḥ vṛtaḥ yotsyāmaḥ saṃhatāḥ tena iti niścita mānasāḥ ājagmuḥ bhū bhujaḥ sarve samagra bala vāhanāḥ kṛṣṇam ca ekam gatam hartum kanyām kalaha śaṅkitaḥ balena mahatā sārdham bhrātṛ sneha pariplutaḥ tvaritaḥ kuṇḍinam prāgāt gaja aśva ratha pattibhiḥ bhīṣma kanyā varārohā kāṅkṣantī āgamanam hareḥ na āgacchati aravinda akṣaḥ na aham vedmi atra kāraṇam api mayi anavadya ātmā dṛṣṭvā kiñcid jugupsitam mad pāṇi grahaṇe nūnam na āyāti hi kṛta udyamaḥ durbhagāyāḥ na me dhātā na anukūlaḥ maheśvaraḥ devī vā vimukhī gaurī rudrāṇī girijā satī evam cintayatī bālā govinda hṛta mānasā nyamīlayata kāla jñā netre ca aśru kalā ākule evam vadhvāḥ pratīkṣantyāḥ govinda āgamanam nṛpa vāmaḥ ūruḥ bhujaḥ netram asphuran priya bhāṣiṇaḥ atha kṛṣṇa vinirdiṣṭaḥ saḥ eva dvija sattamaḥ antaḥpura carīm devīm rāja putrīm dadarśa ha sā tam prahṛṣṭa vadanam avyagra ātma gatim satī ālakṣya lakṣaṇa abhijñā samapṛcchat śuci smitā tasyai āvedayat prāptam śaśaṃsa yadu nandanam tam āgatam samājñāya vaidarbhī hṛṣṭa mānasā na paśyantī brāhmaṇāya priyam anyat nanāma sā abhyayāt tūrya ghoṣeṇa rāma kṛṣṇau samarhaṇaiḥ madhu parkam upānīya vāsāṃsi virajāṃsi saḥ upāyanāni abhīṣṭāni vidhi vat samapūjayat tayoḥ niveśanam śrīmat upākalpya mahā matiḥ evam rājñām sametānām yathā vīryam yathā vayaḥ yathā balam yathā vittam sarvaiḥ kāmaiḥ samarhayat kṛṣṇam āgatam ākarṇya vidarbha pura vāsinaḥ asya eva bhāryā bhavitum rukmiṇī arhati na aparā asau api anavadya ātmā bhaiṣmyāḥ samucitaḥ patiḥ anugṛhṇātu gṛhṇātu vaidarbhyāḥ pāṇim acyutaḥ kanyā ca antaḥpurāt prāgāt bhaṭaiḥ guptā ambikālayam padbhyām viniryayau draṣṭum bhavānyāḥ pāda pallavam sā ca anudhyāyatī samyak mukunda caraṇa ambujam yata vāc mātṛbhiḥ sārdham sakhībhiḥ parivāritā guptāḥ rāja bhaṭaiḥ śūraiḥ sannaddhaiḥ udyata āyudhaiḥ mṛḍaṅga śaṅkha paṇavāḥ tūrya bheryaḥ ca jaghnire nānā upahāra balibhiḥ vāramukhyāḥ sahasraśas gāyantyaḥ ca stuvantaḥ ca gāyakāḥ vādya vādakāḥ parivārya vadhūm jagmuḥ sūta māgadha vandinaḥ āsādya devī sadanam dhauta pāda kara ambujā upaspṛśya śuciḥ śāntā praviveśa ambikā antikam tām vai pravayasaḥ bālām vidhi jñāḥ vipra yoṣitaḥ bhavānīm cakruḥ bhava patnīm bhava anvitām namasye tvā ambike abhīkṣṇam sva santāna yutām śivām bhūyāt patiḥ me bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ tat anumodatām adbhiḥ gandha akṣataiḥ dhūpaiḥ vāsaḥ sraj mālya bhūṣaṇaiḥ nānā upahāra balibhiḥ pradīpa āvalibhiḥ pṛthak lavaṇa apūpa tāmbūla kaṇṭha sūtra phala ikṣubhiḥ tasyai striyaḥ tāḥ pradaduḥ śeṣām yuyujuḥ āśiṣaḥ tābhyaḥ devyai namaḥ cakre śeṣām ca jagṛhe vadhūḥ muni vratam atha tyaktvā niścakrāma ambikā gṛhāt pragṛhya pāṇinā bhṛtyām ratna mudrā upaśobhinā tām deva māyām iva dhīra mohinīm su madhyamām kuṇḍala maṇḍita ānanām śyāmām nitamba arpita ratna mekhalām vyañjat stanīm kuntala śaṅkita īkṣaṇām śuci smitām bimba phala adhara dyuti śoṇāyamāna dvija kunda kuḍmalām padā calatīm kala haṃsa gāminīm siñjat kalā nūpura dhāma śobhinā vilokya vīrāḥ mumuhuḥ samāgatāḥ yaśasvinaḥ tad kṛta hṛd śaya arditāḥ yām vīkṣya te nṛpatayaḥ tat udāra hāsa vrīda avaloka hṛta cetasaḥ ujjhita astrāḥ petuḥ kṣitau gaja ratha aśva gatāḥ vimūḍhāḥ yātrā chalena haraye arpayatīm sva śobhām sā evam śanais calayatī cala padma kośau prāptim tadā bhagavataḥ prasamīkṣamāṇā utsārya vāma karajaiḥ alakān apaṅgaiḥ prāptān hriyā aikṣata nṛpān dadṛśe acyutam ca tām rāja kanyām ratham ārurakṣatīm jahāra kṛṣṇaḥ dviṣatām samīkṣatām ratham samāropya suparṇa lakṣaṇam rājanya cakram paribhūya mādhavaḥ tatas yayau rāma purogamaḥ śanais śṛgāla madhyāt iva bhāga hṛt hariḥ tam māninaḥ sva abhibhavam yaśaḥ kṣayam aho dhik asmān yaśaḥ ātta dhanvanām gopaiḥ hṛtam kesariṇām mṛgaiḥ iva śrī śukaḥ uvāca iti sarve su saṃrabdhāḥ vāhān āruhya daṃśitāḥ svaiḥ svaiḥ balaiḥ parikrāntāḥ anvīyuḥ dhṛta kārmukāḥ tān āpatataḥ ālokya yādava anīka yūthapāḥ mumucuḥ śara varṣāṇi meghāḥ adriṣu apaḥ yathā patyuḥ balam śara āsāraiḥ channam vīkṣya su madhyamā vinaṅkṣyati adhunā eva etat tāvakaiḥ śātravam balam teṣām tad vikramam vīrāḥ gada saṅkarṣana ādayaḥ amṛṣyamāṇāḥ nārācaiḥ jaghnuḥ haya gajān rathān petuḥ śirāṃsi rathinām aśvinām gajinām bhuvi sa kuṇḍala kirīṭāni sa uṣṇīṣāṇi ca koṭiśas hastāḥ sa asi gadeṣu āsāḥ karabhāḥ ūravaḥ aṅghrayaḥ aśva aśvatara nāga uṣṭra khara martya śirāṃsi ca hanyamāna bala anīkāḥ vṛṣṇibhiḥ jaya kāṅkṣibhiḥ rājānaḥ vimukhāḥ jagmuḥ jarāsandha puraḥsarāḥ śiśupālam samabhyetya hṛta dāram iva āturam naṣṭa tviṣam gata utsāham śuṣyat vadanam abruvan na priya apriyayoḥ rājan niṣṭhā dehiṣu dṛśyate yathā dāru mayī yoṣit nṛtyate kuhaka icchayā śaureḥ sapta daśa aham vai saṃyugāni parājitaḥ tathā api aham na śocāmi na prahṛṣyāmi karhicit adhunā api vayam sarve vīra yūthapa yūthapāḥ parājitāḥ phalgu tantraiḥ yadubhiḥ kṛṣṇa pālitaiḥ ripavaḥ jigyuḥ adhunā kāle ātma anusāriṇi tadā vayam vijeṣyāmaḥ yadā kālaḥ pradakṣiṇaḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca hata śeṣāḥ punar te api yayuḥ svam svam puram nṛpāḥ rukmī tu rākṣasa udvāham kṛṣṇa dviṣ asahān svasuḥ pṛṣṭhatas anvagamat kṛṣṇam akṣauhiṇyā vṛtaḥ balī rukmī amarṣī su saṃrabdhaḥ śṛṇvatām sarva bhūbhujām pratijajñe mahā bāhuḥ daṃśitaḥ sa śarāsanaḥ a hatvā samare kṛṣṇam a pratyūhya ca rukmiṇīm kuṇḍinam na pravekṣyāmi satyam etat bravīmi vaḥ codaya aśvān yatas kṛṣṇaḥ tasya me saṃyugam bhavet adya aham niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ gopālasya su durmateḥ neṣye vīrya madam yena svasā me prasabham hṛtā vikatthamānaḥ kumatiḥ īśvarasya apramāṇa vid dhanuḥ vikṛṣya su dṛḍham jaghne kṛṣṇam tribhiḥ śaraiḥ āha ca atra kṣaṇam tiṣṭha yadūnām kula pāṃsana yatra yāsi svasāram me muṣitvā dhvāṅkṣa vat haviḥ hariṣye adya madam manda māyinaḥ kūṭa yodhinaḥ yāvat na me hataḥ bāṇaiḥ śayīthāḥ muñca dārīkām smayan kṛṣṇaḥ dhanuḥ chittvā ṣaḍbhiḥ vivyādha rukmiṇam aṣṭabhiḥ caturaḥ vāhān dvābhyām sūtam dhvajam tribhiḥ sa ca anyat dhanuḥ ādhāya kṛṣṇam vivyādha pañcabhiḥ parigham paṭṭiśam śūlam carma āsī śakti tomarau tatas rathāt avaplutya khaḍga pāṇiḥ jighāṃsayā tasya ca āpatataḥ khaḍgam tilaśas carma ca iṣubhiḥ dṛṣṭvā bhrātṛ vadha udyogam rukmiṇī bhaya vihvalā patitvā pādayoḥ bhartuḥ uvāca karuṇam satī śrī rukmiṇī uvāca hantum na arhasi kalyāṇa bhrātaram me mahā bhuja śrī śukaḥ uvāca tayā paritrāsa vikampita aṅgayā śucā avaśuṣyat mukha ruddha kaṇṭhayā kātarya visraṃsita hema mālayā gṛhīta pādaḥ karuṇaḥ nyavartata cailena baddhvā tam asādhu kārīṇam sa śmaśru keśam pravapan vyarūpayat tāvat mamarduḥ para sainyam adbhutam yadu pravīrāḥ nalinīm yathā gajāḥ kṛṣṇa antikam upavrajya dadṛśuḥ tatra rukmiṇam tathā bhūtam hata prāyam dṛṣṭvā saṅkarṣaṇaḥ vibhuḥ vimucya baddham karuṇaḥ bhagavant kṛṣṇam abravīt asādhu idam tvayā kṛṣṇa kṛtam asmad jugupsitam vapanam śmaśru keśānām vairūpyam suhṛdaḥ vadhaḥ mā eva asmān sādho asūyethāḥ bhrātuḥ vairūpya cintayā tyājyaḥ svena eva doṣeṇa hataḥ kim hanyate punar kṣatriyāṇām ayam dharmaḥ prajāpati vinirmitaḥ māninaḥ anyasya vā hetoḥ śrī mada andhāḥ kṣipanti hi tava iyam viṣamā buddhiḥ sarva bhūteṣu durhṛdām ātma mohaḥ nṛṇām eva kalpate deva māyayā suhṛd durhṛd udāsīnaḥ iti deha ātma māninām nānā iva gṛhyate mūḍhaiḥ yathā jyotiḥ yathā nabhaḥ dehaḥ ādi antavān eṣa dravya prāṇa guṇa ātmakaḥ ātmani avidyayā kḷptaḥ saṃsārayati dehinam tad hetu tvāt tad prasiddheḥ dṛś rūpābhyām yathā raveḥ yathā śayānaḥ ātmānam viṣayān phalam eva ca tasmāt ajñāna jam śokam ātma śoṣa vimohanam śrī śukaḥ uvāca evam bhagavatā tanvī rāmeṇa pratibodhitā prāṇa avaśeṣaḥ utsṛṣṭaḥ dviḍbhiḥ hata bala prabhaḥ a hatvā durmatim kṛṣṇam a pratyūhya yavīyasīm kuṇḍinam na pravekṣyāmi iti uktvā tatra avasat ruṣā bhagavān bhīṣmaka sutām evam nirjitya bhūmipān tadā mahā utsavaḥ nṝṇām yadu puryām gṛhe gṛhe abhūt ananya bhāvānām kṛṣṇe yadu patau nṛpa narāḥ nāryaḥ ca muditāḥ pramṛṣṭa maṇi kuṇḍalāḥ āpūrṇa kumbha aguru dhūpa dīpakaiḥ sikta mārgāḥ mada cyudbhiḥ āhūta preṣṭha bhūbhujām gajaiḥ dvāḥsu parāmṛṣṭa rambhā pūga upaśobhitā rukmiṇyāḥ haraṇam śrutvā gīyamānam tatas tatas rājānaḥ rāja kanyāḥ ca babhūvuḥ bhṛśa vismitāḥ dvārakāyām abhūt rājan mahā modaḥ puraukasām rukmiṇyā ramayā upetam dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇam śriyaḥ patim śrī śukaḥ uvāca kāmaḥ tu vāsudeva aṃśaḥ dagdhaḥ prāk rudra manyunā saḥ eva jātaḥ vaidarbhyām kṛṣṇa vīrya samudbhavaḥ tam śambaraḥ kāma rūpī hṛtvā tokam anirdaśam sa viditvā ātmanaḥ śatrum prāsya udanvati agāt gṛham tam nirjagāra balavān mīnaḥ saḥ api aparaiḥ saha vṛtaḥ jālena mahatā gṛhītaḥ matsya jīvibhiḥ tam śambarāya kaivartāḥ upājahruḥ upāyanam sūdāḥ mahānasam nītvā vadyan sudhitinā adbhutam dṛṣṭvā tad udare bālam māyāvatyai nyavedayan nāradaḥ akathayat sarvam tasyāḥ śaṅkita cetasaḥ sā ca kāmasya vai patnī ratiḥ nāma yaśasvinī nirūpitā śambareṇa sā sūda odana sādhane kāmadevam śiśum buddhvā cakre sneham tadā arbhake na ati dīrgheṇa kālena sa kārṣṇi rūḍha yauvanaḥ janayām āsa nārīṇām vīkṣantīnām ca vibhramam tām aha bhagavān kārṣṇiḥ mātar te matiḥ anyathā mātṛ bhāvam atikramya vartase kāminī yathā bhavān nārāyaṇa sutaḥ śambareṇa hṛtaḥ gṛhāt aham te adhikṛtā patnī ratiḥ kāmaḥ bhavān prabho eṣa tvā anirdaśam sindhau akṣipat śambaraḥ asuraḥ tam imam jahi durdharṣam durjayam śatrum ātmanaḥ māyā śata vidam tam ca māyābhiḥ mohana ādibhiḥ parīśocati te mātā kurarī iva gata prajā putra sneha ākulā dīnā vivatsā gauḥ iva āturā prabhāṣya evam dadau vidyām pradyumnāya mahātmane māyāvatī mahā māyām sarva māyā vināśinīm niścakrāma gadā pāṇiḥ amarṣāt tāmra locanaḥ prakṣipya vyanadat nādam vajra niṣpeṣa niṣṭhuram tām āpatantīm bhagavān pradyumnaḥ gadayā gadām apāsya śatrave kruddhaḥ prāhiṇot sva gadām nṛpa sa ca māyām samāśritya daiteyīm maya darśitam mumuce astra mayam varṣam kārṣṇau vaihāyasaḥ asuraḥ bādhyamānaḥ astra varṣeṇa raukmiṇeyaḥ mahā rathaḥ sattva ātmakām mahā vidyām sarva māyā upamardinīm tatas gauhyaka gāndharva paiśāca uraga rākṣasīḥ prāyuṅkta śataśas daityaḥ kārṣṇiḥ vyadhamayat sa tāḥ niśātam asim udyamya sa kirīṭam sa kuṇḍalam śambarasya śiraḥ kāyāt tāmra śmaśru ojasā āharat ākīryamāṇaḥ divi jaiḥ stuvadbhiḥ kusuma utkaraiḥ bhāryayā ambara cārinyā puram nītaḥ vihāyasā antaḥpura varam rājan lalanā śata saṅkulam tam dṛṣṭvā jalada śyāmam pīta kauśeya vāsasam pralamba bāhum tāmra akṣam su smitam rucira ānanam su alaṅkṛta mukha ambhojam nīla vakra alaka ālibhiḥ kṛṣṇam matvā striyaḥ hrītāḥ nililyuḥ tatra tatra ha avadhārya śanais īṣat vailakṣaṇyena yoṣitaḥ upajagmuḥ pramuditāḥ sa strī ratnam su vismitāḥ atha tatra asitāpāṅgī vaidarbhī valgu bhāṣiṇī kaḥ nu ayam nara vaidūryaḥ kasya vā kamala īkṣaṇaḥ dhṛtaḥ kayā vā jaṭhare kā iyam labdhā tu anena vā mama ca api ātmajaḥ naṣṭaḥ nītaḥ yaḥ sūtikā gṛhāt katham tu anena samprāptam sārūpyam śārṅga dhanvanaḥ ākṛtyā avayavaiḥ gatyā svara hāsa avalokanaiḥ amuṣmin prītiḥ adhikā vāmaḥ sphurati me bhujaḥ evam mīmāṃsamaṇāyām vaidarbhyām devakī sutaḥ vijñāta arthaḥ api bhagavān tūṣṇīm āsa janārdanaḥ nāradaḥ akathayat sarvam śambara āharaṇa ādikam tat śrutvā mahat āścaryam kṛṣṇa antar pura yoṣitaḥ abhyanandan bahūn abdān naṣṭam mṛtam iva āgatam devakī vasudevaḥ ca kṛṣṇa rāmau tathā striyaḥ naṣṭam pradyumnam āyātam ākarṇya dvārakā okāḥ aho mṛtaḥ iva āyātaḥ bālaḥ diṣṭyā iti ha abruvan yam vai muhur pitṛ sarūpa nija īśa bhāvāḥ tad mātaraḥ yat abhajan raha rūḍha bhāvāḥ kāme smare akṣa viṣaye kim uta anya nāryaḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca satrājitaḥ sva tanayām kṛṣṇāya kṛta kilbiṣaḥ śrī rājā uvāca satrājitaḥ kim akarot brahman kṛṣṇasya kilbiṣaḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca āsīt satrājitaḥ sūryaḥ bhaktasya paramaḥ sakhā prītaḥ tasmai maṇim prādāt sa ca tuṣṭaḥ syamantakam sa tam bibhran maṇim kaṇṭhe bhrājamānaḥ yathā raviḥ praviṣṭaḥ dvārakām rājan tejasā na upalakṣitaḥ tam vilokya janāḥ dūrāt tejasā muṣṭa dṛṣṭayaḥ dīvyate akṣaiḥ bhagavate śaśaṃsuḥ sūrya śaṅkitāḥ nārāyaṇa namaḥ te astu śaṅkha cakra gadā dhara eṣaḥ āyāti savitā tvām didṛkṣuḥ jagat pate muṣṇan gabhasti cakreṇa nṛṇām cakṣūṃṣi tigma guḥ nanu anvicchanti te mārgam trī lokyām vibudha ṛṣabhāḥ jñātvā adya gūḍham yaduṣu draṣṭum tvām yāti ajaḥ prabho śrī śukaḥ uvāca prāha na asau raviḥ devaḥ satrājit maṇinā jvalan satrājit sva gṛham śrīmat kṛta kautuka maṅgalam dine dine svarṇa bhārān aṣṭau sa sṛjati prabho durbhikṣa mārī ariṣṭāni sarpa ādhi vyādhayaḥ aśubhāḥ sa yācitaḥ maṇim kvāpi yadu rājāya śauriṇā na eva artha kāmukaḥ prādāt yācñā bhaṅgam a tarkayan tam ekadā maṇim kaṇṭhe pratimucya mahā prabham prasenam sa hayam hatvā maṇim ācchidya keśarī girim viśan jāmbavatā nihataḥ maṇim icchatā saḥ api cakre kumārasya maṇim krīḍanakam bile prāyas kṛṣṇena nihataḥ maṇi grīvaḥ vanam gataḥ bhrātā mama iti tat śrutvā karṇe karṇe ajapan janāḥ mārṣṭum prasena padavīm anvapadyata nāgaraiḥ hatam prasenam aśvam ca vīkṣya keśariṇā vane tam ca adri pṛṣṭhe nihatam ṛkṣeṇa dadṛśuḥ janāḥ ṛkṣa rāja bilam bhīmam andhena tamasā āvṛtam ekaḥ viveśa bhagavān avasthāpya bahis prajāḥ tatra dṛṣṭvā maṇi preṣṭham bāla krīḍanakam kṛtam tam apūrvam naram dṛṣṭvā dhātrī cukrośa bhīta vat puruṣam prākṛtam matvā kupitaḥ na anubhāva vid āsīt tat aṣṭāvimśa aham itaretara muṣṭibhiḥ kṛṣṇa muṣṭi viniṣpāta niṣpiṣṭa aṅga ūru bandhanaḥ kṣīṇa sattvaḥ svinna gātraḥ tam āha atīva vismitaḥ jāne tvām saṛva bhūtānām prāṇaḥ ojaḥ sahaḥ balam viṣṇum purāṇa puruṣam prabhaviṣṇum adhīśvaram tvam hi viśva sṛjām sraṣṭā sṛṣṭānām api yat ca sat kālaḥ kalayatām īśaḥ paraḥ ātmā tathā ātmanām yasya īṣat utkalita roṣa kaṭākṣa mokṣaiḥ setuḥ kṛtaḥ sva yaśaḥ ujjvalitā ca laṅkā rakṣaḥ śirāṃsi bhuvi petuḥ iṣu kṣatāni iti vijñāta viijñānam ṛkṣa rājānam acyutaḥ vyājahāra mahā rāja bhagavān devakī sutaḥ abhimṛśya aravinda akṣaḥ pāṇinā śam kareṇa tam kṛpayā parayā bhaktam megha gambhīrayā girā mithyā abhiśāpam pramṛjan ātmanaḥ maṇinā amunā iti uktaḥ svām duhitaram kanyām jāmbavatīm mudā arhaṇa artham sa maṇinā kṛṣṇāya upajahāra ha a dṛṣṭvā nirgamam śaureḥ praviṣṭasya bilam janāḥ pratīkṣya dvādaśa ahāni duḥkhitāḥ sva puram yayuḥ niśamya devakī devī rakmiṇī ānakadundubhiḥ suhṛdaḥ jñātayaḥ aśocan bilāt kṛṣṇam anirgatam satrājitam śapantaḥ te duḥkhitāḥ dvārakā okāḥ upatasthuḥ candrabhāgām durgām kṛṣṇa upalabdhaye teṣām tu devī upasthānāt pratyādiṣṭa āśiṣā sa ca prādurbabhūva siddhārthaḥ sa dāraḥ harṣayan hariḥ upalabhya hṛṣīkeśam mṛtam punar iva āgatam saha patnyā maṇi grīvam sarve jāta mahā utsavāḥ satrājitam samāhūya sabhāyām rāja sannidhau prāptim ca ākhyāya bhagavān maṇim tasmai nyavedayat sa ca ati vrīḍitaḥ ratnam gṛhītvā avāk mukhaḥ tatas katham mṛjāmi ātma rajaḥ prasīdet vā acyutaḥ katham kim kṛtvā sādhu mahyam syāt na śapet vā janaḥ yathā adīrgha darśanam kṣudram mūḍham draviṇa lolupam upāyaḥ ayam samīcīnaḥ tasya śāntiḥ na ca anyathā evam vyavasitaḥ buddhyā satrājit sva sutām śubhām maṇim ca svayam udyamya kṛṣṇāya upajahāra ha tām satyabhāmām bhagavān upayeme yathā vidhi bahubhiḥ yācitām śīla rūpa audārya guṇa anvitām bhagavān āha na maṇim pratīcchāmaḥ vayam nṛpa śrī bādarāyaṇiḥ uvāca vijñāta arthaḥ api govindaḥ dagdhān ākarṇya pāṇḍavān bhīṣmam kṛpam sa viduram gāndhārīm droṇam eva ca tulya duḥkhau ca saṅgamya hā kaṣṭam iti ha ūcatuḥ akrūra kṛtavarmāṇau maniḥ kasmāt na gṛhyate kṛṣṇāya adāt na satrājit kasmāt bhrātaram anviyāt śayānam avadhīt lobhāt sa pāpaḥ kṣīṇa jīvitaḥ strīṇām vikrośamānānām krandantīnām anātha vat hatvā paśūn saunika vat maṇim ādāya jagmivān satyabhāmā ca pitaram hatam vīkṣya śucā arpitā vyalapat tāta tāta iti hā hatā asmi iti muhyatī taila droṇyām mṛtam prāsya jagāma gajasāhvayam kṛṣṇāya vidita arthāya taptā ācakhyau pituḥ vadham tat ākarṇya īśvarau rājan anusṛtya nṛ loka tām aho naḥ paramam kaṣṭam iti asra akṣau vilepatuḥ āgatya bhagavān tasmāt sa bhāryaḥ sa agrajaḥ puram śatadhanvānam ārebhe hantum hartum maṇim tatas saḥ api kṛta udyamam jñātvā bhītaḥ prāṇa parīpsayā sāhāyye kṛtavarmāṇam ayācata sa ca abravīt na aham ī svarayoḥ kuryām helanam rāma kṛṣṇayoḥ kaṃsaḥ sahānugaḥ api itas yad dveṣāt tyājitaḥ śriyā jarāsandhaḥ saptadaśa saṃyugāt virathaḥ gataḥ pratyākhyātaḥ sa ca akrūram pārṣṇi grāham ayācata yaḥ idam līlayā viśvam sṛjati avati hanti ca ceṣṭām viśva sṛjaḥ yasya na viduḥ mohita ājayā yaḥ sapta hāyanaḥ śailam utpāṭya ekena pāṇinā dadhāra līlayā bālaḥ ucchilīndhram iva arbhakaḥ namaḥ tasmai bhagavate kṛṣṇāya adbhuta karmaṇe anantāya ādi bhūtāya kūṭa sthāya ātmane namaḥ pratyākhyātaḥ sa tena api śatadhanvā mahā maṇim anvayātām mahā vegaiḥ aśvaiḥ rājan guru druham padbhyām adhāvat santrastaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ api anvadravat ruṣā alabdha maṇiḥ āgatya kṛṣṇaḥ āha agraja antikam tatas āha balaḥ nūnam sa maṇiḥ śatadhanvanā aham vaideham icchāmi draṣṭum priyatamam mama iti uktvā mithilām rājan viveśa yada nandanaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā sahasā utthāya maithilaḥ prīta mānasaḥ arhayāṃ āsa vidhi vat arhaṇīyam samarhaṇaiḥ uvāsa tasyām katicid mithilāyām samāḥ vibhuḥ tatas aśikṣat gadām kāle dhārtarāṣṭraḥ suyodhanaḥ keśavaḥ dvārakām etya nidhanam śatadhanvanaḥ aprāptim ca maṇeḥ prāha priyāyāḥ priya kṛt vibhuḥ sākam suhṛdbhiḥ bhagavān yāḥ yāḥ syuḥ sāmparāyikīḥ akrūraḥ kṛtavarmā ca śrutvā śatadhanoḥ vadham akrūre proṣite ariṣṭāni āsan vai dvārakā okānām śārīrāḥ mānasāḥ tāpāḥ muhur daivika bhautikāḥ iti aṅga upadiśanti eke vismṛtya prāk udāhṛtam muni vāsa nivāse kim ghaṭeta ariṣṭa darśanam deve a varṣati kāśīśaḥ śvaphalkāya āgatāya vai sva sutām gāṇdinīm prādāt tatas avarṣat sma kāśiṣu devaḥ abhivarṣate tatra na upatāpāḥ na mārīkāḥ iti vṛddha vacaḥ śrutvā na etāvat iha kāraṇam iti matvā samānāyya prāha akrūram janārdanaḥ pūjayitvā abhibhāṣya enam kathayitvā priyāḥ kathāḥ vijña tā akhila citta jñaḥ smayamānaḥ uvāca ha syamantakaḥ maniḥ śrīmān viditaḥ pūrvam eva naḥ satrājitaḥ anapatya tvāt gṛhṇīyuḥ duhituḥ sutāḥ dāyam ninīya apaḥ piṇḍān vimucya ṛṇam ca śeṣitam darśayasva mahā bhāga bandhūnām śāntim āvaha evam sāmabhiḥ ālabdhaḥ śvaphalka tanayaḥ maṇim ādāya vāsasā ācchannaḥ dadau sūrya sama prabham syamantakam darśayitvā jñātibhyaḥ rajaḥ ātmanaḥ vīrya āḍhyam vṛjina haram su maṅgalam ca ākhyānam paṭhati śṛṇoti anusmaret vā duṣkīrtim duritam apohya yāti śāntim śrī śukaḥ uvāca ekadā pāṇḍavān draṣṭum pratītān puruṣottamaḥ indraprastham gataḥ śṛīmān yuyudhāna ādibhiḥ vṛtaḥ dṛṣṭvā tam āgatam pārthāḥ mukundam akhila īśvaram uttasthuḥ yugapad vīrāḥ prāṇāḥ mukhyam iva āgatam pariṣvajya acyutam vīrāḥ aṅga saṅga hata enasaḥ sa anurāga smitam vaktram vīkṣya tasya mudam yayuḥ yudhiṣṭhirasya bhīmasya kṛtvā pāda abhivandanam phālgunam parirabhya atha yamābhyām ca abhivanditaḥ parama āsane āsīnam kṛṣṇā kṛṣṇam aninditā na voḍhā vrīḍitā kiñcid śanais etya abhyavandata tathā eva sātyakiḥ pārthaiḥ pūjitaḥ ca abhivanditaḥ niṣasāda āsane anye ca pūjitāḥ paryupāsata pṛthām samāgatya kṛta abhivādanaḥ tayā ati hārda ārdra dṛśā abhirambhitaḥ āpṛṣṭavān tām kuśalam saha snuṣām pitṛ ṣvasāram paripṛṣṭa bāndhavaḥ smarantī tān bahūn kleśān kleśa āpāya ātma darśanam tadā eva kuśalam naḥ abhūt sa nāthāḥ te kṛtāḥ vayam jñatīn naḥ smaratā kṛṣṇa bhrātā me preṣitaḥ tvayā tathā api smaratām śaśvat kleśān haṃsi hṛdi sthitaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca kim naḥ ācaritam śreyaḥ na veda aham adhīśvara yoga īśvarāṇām durdarśaḥ yat naḥ dṛṣṭaḥ ku medhasām iti vai vārṣikān māsān rājñā saḥ abhyarthitaḥ sukham gāṇḍīvam dhanuḥ ādāya tūṇau ca akṣaya sāyakau sākam kṛṣṇena sannaddhaḥ vihartum vipinam mahat bahu vyāla mṛga ākīrṇam prāviśat para vīra hā tatra avidhyat śaraiḥ vyāghrān śūkarān mahiṣān rurūn śarabhān gavayān khaḍgān hariṇān śaśa śallakān tān ninyuḥ kiṅkarāḥ rājñe medhyān parvaṇi upāgate tṛṣ parītaḥ pariśrāntaḥ bibhatsuḥ yamunām agāt tatra upaspṛśya viśadam pītvā vāri mahā rathau kṛṣṇau dadṛśatuḥ kanyām carantīm cāru darśanām tām āsādya varārohām su dvijām rucira ānanām kā tvam kasya asi su śroṇi kutas vā kim cikīrṣasi śrī kālindī uvāca viṣṇum vareṇyam vara dam tapaḥ paramam āsthitaḥ na anyam patim vṛṇe vīra tam ṛte śrī niketanam tuṣyatām me sa bhagavān mukundaḥ anātha saṃśrayaḥ kālindī iti samākhyātā vasāmi yamunā jale tathā avadat guḍākeśaḥ vāsudevāya saḥ api tām yadā eva kṛṣṇaḥ sandiṣṭaḥ pārthānām parama adbutam kārayām āsa nagaram vicitram viśvakarmaṇā bhagavān tatra nivasan svānām priya cikīrṣayā agnaye khāṇḍavam dātum arjunasya āsa sārathiḥ saḥ agniḥ tuṣṭaḥ dhanuḥ adāt dhayān śvetān ratham nṛpa arjunāya akṣayau tūṇau varma ca abhedyam astribhiḥ sa tena samanujñātaḥ suhṛdbhiḥ ca anumoditaḥ āyayau dvārakām bhūyas sātyaki pramakhaiḥ vṛtaḥ atha upayeme kālindīm su puṇya ṛtu ṛkṣe ūrjite vitanvan parama ānandam svānām parama maṅgalaḥ svayaṃvare sva bhaginīm kṛṣṇe saktām nyaṣedhatām rājādhidevyāḥ tanayām mitravindām pitṛ svasuḥ prasahya hṛtavān kṛṣṇaḥ rājan rājñām prapaśyatām nagnajit nāma kauśalyaḥ āsīt rājā ati dhārmikaḥ tasya satyā bhavat kanyā devī nāgnajitī nṛpa na tām śekuḥ nṛpāḥ voḍhum a jitvā sapta go vṛṣān tīkṣṇa śṛṅgān su durdharṣān vīrya gandha asahān khalān tām śrutvā vṛṣa jit labhyām bhagavān sātvatām patiḥ jagāma kauśalya puram sainyena mahatā vṛtaḥ sa kośala patiḥ prītaḥ pratyutthāna āsana ādibhiḥ arhaṇena api guruṇā pūjayan pratinanditaḥ bhūyāt ayam me patiḥ āśiṣaḥ analaḥ karotu satyāḥ yadi me dhṛtaḥ vrataḥ yat pāda paṅkaja rajaḥ śirasā bibharti śṛīḥ abya jaḥ sa giriśaḥ saha loka pālaiḥ līlā tanuḥ sva kṛta setu parīpsayā yaḥ ātma ānandena pūrṇasya karavāṇi kim alpakaḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca tam āha bhagavān hṛṣṭaḥ kṛta āsana parigrahaḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca tathā api yāce tava sauhṛda icchayā kanyām tvadīyām na hi śulka dāḥ vayam śrī rājā uvāca guṇa eka dhāmnaḥ yasya aṅge śrīḥ vasati anapāyinī kintu asmābhiḥ kṛtaḥ pūrvam samayaḥ sātvata ṛṣabha puṃsām vīrya parīkṣā artham kanyā vara parīpsayā sapta ete go vṛṣāḥ vīra durdāntāḥ duravagrahāḥ etaiḥ bhagnāḥ su bahavaḥ bhinna gātrāḥ nṛpa ātmajāḥ ātmānam saptadhā kṛtvā nyagṛhṇāt līlayā eva tān baddhvā tān dāmabhiḥ śauriḥ bhagna darpān hata ojasaḥ vyakarsat līlayā baddhān bālaḥ dāru mayān yathā tatas prītaḥ sutām rājā dadau kṛṣṇāya vismitaḥ tām pratyagṛhṇāt bhagavān vidhi vat sadṛśīm prabhuḥ rāja patnyaḥ ca duhituḥ kṛṣṇam labdhvā priyam patim śaṅkha bherī ānakāḥ neduḥ gīta vādya dvija āśiṣaḥ narāḥ nāryaḥ pramuditāḥ su vāsaḥ sraj alaṅkṛtāḥ daśa dhenu sahasrāṇi pāribarham adāt vibhuḥ yuvatīnām tri sāhasram niṣka grīva suvāsasam nava nāga sahasrāṇi nāgāt śata guṇān rathān rathāt śata guṇān aśvān aśvāt śata guṇān narān sneha praklinna hṛdayaḥ yāpayām āsa kośalaḥ bhagna vīryāḥ su durmarṣāḥ yadubhiḥ go vṛṣaiḥ purā tān asyataḥ śara vrātān bandhu priya kṛt arjunaḥ gāṇḍīvī kālayām āsa siṃhaḥ kṣudra mṛgān iva pāribarham upāgṛhya dvārakām etya satyayā reme yadūnām ṛṣabhaḥ bhagavān devakī sutaḥ śrutakīrteḥ sutām bhadrām upayeme pitṛ svasuḥ kaikeyīm bhrātṛbhiḥ dattām kṛṣṇaḥ santardana ādibhiḥ sutām ca madra adhipateḥ lakṣmaṇām lakṣaṇaiḥ yatām svayaṃvare jahāra ekaḥ sa suparṇaḥ sudhām iva anyāḥ ca evaṃvidhāḥ bhāryāḥ kṛṣṇasya āsan sahasraśas bhaumam hatvā tad nirodhāt āhṛtāḥ cāru darśanāḥ śrī rājā uvāca yathā hataḥ bhagavatā bhaumaḥ yene ca tāḥ striyaḥ niruddhāḥ etat ācakṣva vikramam śārṅgadhanvanaḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca indreṇa hṛta chatreṇa hṛta kuṇḍala bandhunā hṛta amara adri sthānena jñāpitaḥ bhauma ceṣṭitam sa bhāryaḥ garuḍa ārūḍhaḥ prāk jyotiṣa puram yayau mura pāśa ayutaiḥ ghoraiḥ dṛḍhaiḥ sarvatas āvṛtam gadayā nirbibheda adrīn śastra durgāṇi sāyakaiḥ cakreṇa agnim jalam vāyum mura pāśān tathā asinā śaṅkha nādena yantrāṇi hṛdayāni manasvinām prākāram gadayā gurvyā nirbibheda gadādharaḥ pāñcajanya dhvanim śrutvā yugānta śani bhīṣaṇam muraḥ śayānaḥ uttasthau daityaḥ pañca śirāḥ jalāt tri śūlam udyamya su durnirīkṣaṇaḥ yugānta sūrya anala rociḥ ulbaṇaḥ sa rodasī sarva diśaḥ ambaram mahān āpūrayan aṇḍa kaṭāham āvṛṇot mukheṣu tam ca api śaraiḥ atāḍayat tasmai gadām saḥ api ruṣā vyamuñcata tām āpatantīm gadayā gadām mṛdhe gadāgrajaḥ nirbibhide sahasradhā udyamya bāhūn abhidhāvataḥ ajitaḥ śirāṃsi cakreṇa jahāra līlayā vyasuḥ papāta ambhasi kṛtta śīrṣaḥ nikṛtta śṛṅgaḥ adriḥ iva indra tejasā tasya ātmajāḥ sapta pituḥ vadha āturāḥ pratikriyā āmarṣa juṣaḥ samudyatāḥ tāmraḥ antarikṣaḥ śravaṇaḥ vibhāvasuḥ pīṭham puraskṛtya camū patim mṛdhe bhauma prayuktāḥ niragan dhṛta āyudhāḥ prāyuñjata āsādya śarān asīn gadāḥ śakti ṛṣṭi śūlāni ajite ruṣā ulbaṇāḥ tān pīṭha mukhyān anayat yama kṣayam nikṛtta śīrṣa ūru bhuja aṅghri varmaṇaḥ nirīkṣya durmarṣaṇaḥ āsravan madaiḥ dṛṣṭvā sa bhāryam garuḍa upari sthitam sūrya upariṣṭāt sa taḍit ghanam yathā kṛṣṇam sa tasmai vyasṛjat śata ghnīm vicitra vājaiḥ niśitaiḥ śilīmukhaiḥ nikṛtta bāhu ūru śira udhra vigraham yāni yodhaiḥ prayuktāni śastra astrāṇi kuru udvaha hariḥ tāni acchinat tīkṣṇaiḥ śaraiḥ ekaikaśas trībhiḥ uhyamānaḥ suparṇena pakṣābhyām nighnatā gajān gurutmatā hanyamānāḥ tuṇḍa pakṣa nakheḥ gajāḥ dṛṣṭvā vidrāvitam sainyam garuḍena arditam svakam sa kuṇḍalam cāru kirīṭa bhūṣaṇam babhau pṛthivyām patitam samujjvalam ha ha iti sādhu iti ṛṣayaḥ sura īśvarāḥ mālyaiḥ mukundam vikirantaḥ īdire tatas ca bhūḥ kṛṣṇam upetya kuṇḍale astauṣīt atha viśveśam devī deva vara arcitam prāñjaliḥ praṇatā rājan bhakti pravaṇayā dhiyā bhūmiḥ uvāca namaḥ paṅkaja nābhāya namaḥ paṅkaja māline namaḥ paṅkaja netrāya namaḥ te paṅkaja aṅghraye puruṣāya ādi bījāya pūrṇa bodhāya te namaḥ tvam vai sisṛkṣuḥ ajaḥ utkaṭam prabho tamaḥ nirodhāya bibharṣi asaṃvṛtaḥ kālaḥ pradhānam puruṣaḥ bhavān paraḥ aham payaḥ jyotiḥ atha anilaḥ nabhaḥ mātrāṇi devāḥ manaḥ indriyāṇi tasya ātmajaḥ ayam tava pāda paṅkajam bhītaḥ prapanna ārti hara upasāditaḥ tat pālaya enam kuru hasta paṅkajam śirasi amuṣya akhila kalmaṣa apaham śrī śukaḥ uvāca tatra rājanya kanyānām ṣaṣ sahasra adhika ayutam bhauma āhṛtānām vikramya rājabhyaḥ dadṛśe hariḥ tam praviṣṭam striyaḥ vīkṣya nara varyam vimohitāḥ manasā vavrire abhīṣṭam patim daiva upasāditam bhūyāt patiḥ ayam mahyam dhātā tat anumodatām iti sarvāḥ pṛthak kṛṣṇe bhāvena hṛdayam tāḥ prāhiṇot dvāravatīm su mṛṣṭa virajaḥ ambarāḥ nara yānaiḥ mahā kośān ratha aśvān draviṇam mahāt airāvata kulebhān ca catur dantān tarasvinaḥ pāṇḍurān ca catuḥ ṣaṣṭim prerayām āsa keśavaḥ pūjitaḥ tridaśa indreṇa mahā indryāṇyā ca sa priyaḥ coditaḥ bhāryayā utpāṭya pārījātam garutmanti sthāpitaḥ satyabhāmāyāḥ gṛha udyāna upaśobhanaḥ anvaguḥ bhramarāḥ svargāt tad gandha āsava lampaṭāḥ yayāca ānamya kirīṭa koṭibhiḥ pādau spṛśan acyutam artha sādhanam siddhārthaḥ etena vigṛhyate mahān aho surāṇām ca tamaḥ dhik āḍhya tām atha u muhūrte ekasmin nānā āgāreṣu tāḥ striyaḥ gṛheṣu tāsām anapāyī a tarka kṛt nirasta sāmya atiśayeṣu avasthitaḥ brahma ādayaḥ api na viduḥ padavīm yadīyām hāsa avaloka nava saṃgama jalpa lajjāḥ tāmbūla viśramaṇa vījana gandha mālyaiḥ keśa prasāra śayana snapana upahāryaiḥ dāsī śatāḥ api vibhoḥ vidadhuḥ sma dāsyam śrī bādarāyaṇiḥ uvāca yaḥ tu etat līlayā viśvam sṛjati atti avati īśvaraḥ sa hi jātaḥ sva setūnām gopīthāya yaduṣu ajaḥ pārijāta vana āmoda vāyunā udyāna śālinā upatasthe sukha āsīnam jagatām īśvaram patim vāla vyajanam ādāya ratna daṇḍam sakhī karāt tena vījayatī devī upāsām cakre īśvaram sā upācyutam kvaṇayatī maṇi nūpurābhyām vastra anta gūḍha kuca kuṅkuma śoṇa hāra bhāsā nitamba dhṛtayā ca parārdhya kāñcyā tām rūpiṇīm śrīyam ananya gatim nirīkṣya yā līlayā dhṛta tanoḥ anurūpa rūpā prītaḥ smayan alaka kuṇḍala niṣka kaṇṭha śrī bhagavān uvāca rāja putrī īpsitā bhūpaiḥ loka pāla vibhūtibhiḥ mahā anubhāvaiḥ śrīmadbhiḥ rūpa audārya bala ūrjitaiḥ tān prāptān arthinaḥ hitvā caidya ādīn smara durmadān dattā bhrātrā sva pitrā ca kasmāt naḥ vavṛṣe asamān rājabhyaḥ bibhyataḥ su bhru samudram śaraṇam gatān balavadbhiḥ kṛta dveṣān prāyas tyakta nṛpāsanān aspaṣṭa vartmanām puṃsām aloka patham īyuṣām āsthitāḥ padavīm su bhru prāyas sīdanti yoṣitaḥ niṣkiñcanāḥ vayam śaśvat niṣkiñcana jana priyāḥ tasmāt tprāyeṇa na hi āḍhyāḥ mām bhajanti su madhyame yayoḥ ātma samam vittam janma aiśvarya ākṛtiḥ bhavaḥ vaidarbhi etat a vijñāya tvayā adīrgha samīkṣayā vṛtāḥ vayam guṇaiḥ hīnāḥ bhikṣubhiḥ ślāghitāḥ mudhā yena tvam āśiṣaḥ satyāḥ iha amutra ca lapsyase caidya śālva jarāsandha dantavakra ādayaḥ nṛpāḥ mama dviṣanti vāma ūro rukmī ca api tava agrajaḥ teṣām vīrya mada andhānām dṛptānām smaya nuttaye udāsīnāḥ vayam nūnam na strī apatya artha kāmukāḥ ātma labdhyā āsmahe pūrṇāḥ gehayoḥ jyotiḥ akriyāḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca etāvat uktvā bhagavān ātmānam vallabhām iva manyamānām aviśleṣāt tad darpa ghnaḥ upāramat āśrutya bhītā hṛdi jāta vepathuḥ cintām durantām rudatī jagāma ha padā su jātena nakha aruṇa śrīyā bhuvam likhantī aśruṣu añjana asitaiḥ tasyāḥ su duḥkha bhaya śoka vinaṣṭa buddheḥ tat dṛṣṭvā bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ priyāyāḥ prema bandhanam hāsya prauḍhim a jānantyāḥ karuṇaḥ saḥ anvakampata paryaṅkāt avaruhya āśu tām utthāpya catur bhujaḥ keśān samuhya tad vaktram prāmṛjat padma pāṇinā āśliṣya bāhunā rājan ananya viṣayām satīm sāntvayām āsa sāntva jñaḥ kṛpayā kṛpaṇām prabhuḥ hāsya prauḍhi bhramat cittām a tad arhām satām gatiḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca mā mā vaidarbhi asūyethāḥ jāne tvām mad parāyaṇām tvad vacaḥ śrotu kāmena kṣveḍī ācaritam aṅgane kaṭā kṣepa aruṇa apāṅgam sundara bhru kuṭī taṭam ayam hi paramaḥ lābhaḥ gṛheṣu gṛha medhinām yat narmaiḥ īyate yāmaḥ priyayā bhīro bhāmini śrī śukaḥ uvāca jñātvā tad parihāsa uktim priya tyāga bhayam jahau babhāṣa ṛṣabham puṃsām vīkṣantī bhagavat mukham sa vrīḍa hāsa rucira snigdha apāṅgena bhārata śrī rukmiṇī uvāca kva sve mahimni abhirataḥ bhagavant tryadhīśaḥ kva aham guṇa prakṛtiḥ ajña gṛhīta pādā tvad pāda padma makaranda juṣām munīnām na tvā vidanti asu tṛpaḥ antakam āḍhya tā andhāḥ tvam vai samasta puruṣa artha mayaḥ phala ātmā teṣām vibho samucitaḥ bhavataḥ samājaḥ puṃsaḥ striyāḥ ca ratayoḥ sukha duḥkhinoḥ na ātmā ātma daḥ ca jagatām iti me vṛtaḥ asi jāḍyam vacaḥ tava gadāgraja yaḥ tu bhūpān vidrāvya śārṅga ninadena jahartha mām tvam siṃhaḥ yathā sva balim īśa paśūn sva bhāgam tebhyaḥ bhayāt yat udadhim śaraṇam prapannaḥ yad vāñchayā nṛpa śikhāmaṇayaḥ anga vainya rājyam visṛjya viviśuḥ vanam ambuja akṣa sīdanti te anu padavīm te iha āsthitāḥ kim lakṣmī ālayam tu a vigaṇayya guṇālayasya tam tvā anurūpam abhajam jagatām adhīśam syāt me tava aṅghriḥ araṇam sṛtibhiḥ bhramantyā tasyāḥ syuḥ acyuta nṛpāḥ bhavatā upadiṣṭāḥ strīṇām gṛheṣu khara go śva viḍāla bhṛtyāḥ yat karṇa mūlam an karṣaṇa na upayāyāt yuṣmad kathā mṛḍa viriñca sabhāsu gītā māṃsa asthi rakta kṛmi viṣ kapha pitta vātam jīvat śavam bhajati kānta matiḥ vimūḍhā astu ambuja akṣa mama te caraṇa anurāga ātman ratasya mayi ca anatirikta dṛṣṭeḥ mām īkṣase tat u ha naḥ paramā anukampā ambāyāḥ eva hi prāyas kanyāyāḥ syāt ratiḥ kvacid vyūḍhāyāḥ ca api puṃścalyāḥ manaḥ abhyeti navam navam budhaḥ asatīm na bibhṛyāt tām bibhrat ubhaya cyutaḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca yān yān kāmayase kāmān mayi akāmāya bhāmini yat vākyaiḥ cālyamānāyāḥ na dhīḥ mayi apakarṣitā kāma ātmānaḥ apavarga īśam mohitāḥ mama māyayā mām prāpya māninī apavarga sampadam te manda bhāgāḥ niraye api ye nṛṇām mātrā ātmaka tvāt nirayaḥ su saṅgamaḥ diṣṭyā gṛheśvari asakṛt mayi tvayā kṛta anuvṛttiḥ bhava mocanī khalaiḥ su duṣkarā asau sutarām durāśiṣaḥ hi asum bharāyāḥ nikṛtim juṣaḥ striyāḥ na tvādṛśīm praṇayinīm gṛhiṇīm gṛheṣu paśyāmi mānini yayā sva vivāha kāle prāptān nṛpān na vigaṇayya rahaḥ haraḥ me prodvāha parvaṇi ca tad vadham akṣa goṣṭhyām na eva abravīḥ kim api tena vayam jitāḥ te matvā jihāse idam aṅgam ananya yogyam śrī śukaḥ uvāca evam saurata saṃlāpaiḥ bhagavant jagat īśvaraḥ tathā anyāsām api vibhuḥ gṛhesu gṛhavān iva āsthitaḥ gṛha medhīyān dharmān loka guruḥ hariḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca ekaikaśas tāḥ kṛṣṇasya putrān daśa daśa abaāḥ gṛhāt anapagam vīkṣya rāja putryaḥ acyutam sthitam preṣṭham nyamaṃsata svam svam na tad tattva vidaḥ striyaḥ smāyā avaloka lava darśita bhāva hāri bhrū maṇḍala prahita saurata mantra śauṇḍaiḥ patnyaḥ tu śoḍaśa sahasram anaṅga bāṇaiḥ brahma ādayaḥ api na viduḥ padavīm yadīyām hāsa avaloka nava saṅgama lālasa ādyam pratyudgama āsana vara arhaṇa pāda śauca tāmbūla viśramaṇa vījana gandha mālyaiḥ keśa prasāra śayana snapana upahāryaiḥ dāsī śatāḥ api vibhoḥ vidadhuḥ sma dāsyam tāsām yāḥ daśa putrāṇām kṛṣṇa strīṇām purā uditāḥ aṣṭau mahiṣyaḥ tad putrān pradyumna ādīn gṛṇāmi te cārudeṣṇaḥ sudeṣṇaḥ ca cārudehaḥ ca vīryavān sucāruḥ cāruguptaḥ ca bhadracāruḥ tathā aparaḥ cārucandraḥ vicāruḥ ca cāruḥ ca daśamaḥ hareḥ pradyumna pramukhāḥ jātāḥ rukmiṇyām na avamāḥ pituḥ bhānuḥ subhānuḥ svarbhānuḥ prabhānuḥ bhānumant tathā candrabhānuḥ bṛhadbhānuḥ atibhānuḥ tathā aṣṭamaḥ śrībhānuḥ pratibhānuḥ ca satyabhāmā ātmajāḥ daśa viyayaḥ citraketuḥ ca vasumant draviḍaḥ kratuḥ jāmbavatyāḥ sutāḥ hi ete sāmba ādyāḥ pitṛ sammatāḥ vīraḥ candraḥ aśvasenaḥ ca citraguḥ vegavant vṛṣaḥ āmaḥ śaṅkuḥ vasuḥ śrīmān kuntiḥ nāgnajiteḥ sutāḥ śrutaḥ kaviḥ vṛṣaḥ vīraḥ subāhuḥ bhadraḥ ekalaḥ śāntiḥ darśaḥ pūrṇamāsaḥ kālindyāḥ somakaḥ avaraḥ praghoṣaḥ gātravān siṃhaḥ balaḥ prabalaḥ ūrdhagaḥ mādryāḥ putrāḥ mahāśaktiḥ sahaḥ ojaḥ aparājitaḥ mahāṃsaḥ pāvanaḥ vahniḥ mitravinda ātmajāḥ kṣudhiḥ saṅgrāmajit bṛhatsenaḥ śūraḥ praharaṇaḥ ari jit jayaḥ subhadraḥ bhadrāyāḥ vāmaḥ āyūḥ ca satyakaḥ dīptimant tāmratapta ādyāḥ rohiṇyāḥ tanayāḥ hareḥ pradyamnāt ca aniruddhaḥ abhūt rukmavatyām mahā balaḥ putryām tu rukmiṇaḥ rājan nāmnā bhojakaṭe pure eteṣām putra pautrāḥ ca babhūvuḥ koṭiśas nṛpa mātaraḥ kṛṣṇa jātīnām sahasrāṇi ca ṣoḍaśa śrī rājā uvāca kṛṣṇena paribhūtaḥ tam hantum randhram pratīkṣate viprakṛṣṭam vyavahitam samyak paśyanti yoginaḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca vṛtaḥ svayaṃvare sākṣāt anaṇgaḥ aṇga yutaḥ tayā yadi api anusmaran vairam rukmī kṛṣṇa avamānitaḥ rukmiṇyāḥ tanayām rājan kṛtavarma sutaḥ balī upayeme viśāla akṣīm kanyām cārumatīm kila dauhitrāya aniruddhāya pautrīm rukmī ādadāt hareḥ rocanām baddha vairaḥ api svasuḥ priya cikīrṣayā jānan adharmam tat yaunam sneha pāśa anubandhanaḥ puram bhoja kaṭam jagmuḥ sāmba pradyumnaka ādayaḥ tasmin nivṛtte udvāhe kāliṅga pramukhāḥ nṛpāḥ śatam sahasram ayutam rāmaḥ tatra ādade paṇam dantān sandarśayan uccais na amṛṣyat tat halāyudhaḥ tatas lakṣam rukmī agṛhṇāt glaham tatra ajayat balaḥ jitavān aham iti āha rukmī kaitavam āśritaḥ manyunā kṣubhitaḥ śrīmān samudraḥ iva parvaṇi jātyā aruṇa akṣaḥ ati ruṣā nyarbudam glaham ādade tam ca api jitavan rāmaḥ dharmeṇa chalam āśritaḥ rukmī jitam mayā atra ime vadantu prāśnikāḥ iti tadā bravīt nabhaḥ vāṇī balena eva jitaḥ glahaḥ tām an ādṛtya vaidarbhaḥ duṣṭa rājanya coditaḥ saṅkarṣaṇam parihasan babhāṣe kāla coditaḥ na eva akṣa kovidāḥ yūyam gopālāḥ vana gocarāḥ akṣaiḥ dīvyanti rājānaḥ bāṇaiḥ ca na bhavādṛśāḥ rukmiṇā evam adhikṣiptaḥ rājabhiḥ ca upahāsitaḥ kaliṅga rājam tarasā gṛhītvā daśame pade anye nirbhinna bāhu ūru śirasaḥ rudhira ukṣitāḥ rājānaḥ dudravar bhītāḥ balena paṅgha arditāḥ nihate rukmiṇi śyāle na abravīt sādhu asādhu vā tatas aniruddham saha sūryayā varam ratham samāropya yayuḥ kuśasthalīm rāma ādayaḥ bhoja kaṭāt daśārhāḥ siddha akhila arthāḥ madhusūdana āśrayāḥ śrī rājā uvāca bāṇasya tanayām ūṣām upayeme yadu uttamaḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca bāṇaḥ putra śata jyeṣṭhaḥ baleḥ āsīt mahātmanaḥ yena vāmana rūpāya haraye adāyi medinī tasya aurasaḥ sutaḥ bānaḥ śiva bhakti rataḥ sadā mānyaḥ vadānyaḥ dhīmān ca satya sandhaḥ dṛḍha vrataḥ tasya śambhoḥ prasādena kiṅkarāḥ iva te amarāḥ sahasra bāhuḥ vādyena tāṇdave atoṣayat mṛḍam bhagavān sarva bhūta īśaḥ śaraṇyaḥ bhakta vatsalaḥ saḥ ekadā āha giriśam pārśva stham vīrya durmadaḥ kirīṭena arka varṇena saṃspṛśan tad pada ambujam namasye tvām mahā deva lokānām gurum īśvaram puṃsām a pūrṇa kāmānām kāma pūra amara aṅghripam dos sahasram tvayā dattam param bhārāya me abhavat ādyāyām cūrṇayan adrīn bhītāḥ te api pradudruvuḥ iti uktaḥ kumatiḥ hṛṣṭaḥ sva gṛham prāviśat nṛpa pratīkṣan giriśa ādeśam sva vīrya naśanam kudhīḥ tasya uṣā nāma duhitā svapne prādyumninā ratim kanyā alabhata kāntena prāk adṛṣṭa śrutena sā sā tatra tam a paśyantī kva asi kāntaiḥ iti vādinī sakhīnām madhye uttasthau vihvalā vrīḍitā bhṛśam bāṇasya mantrī kumbhāṇḍaḥ citralekhā ca tad sutā sakhī apṛcchat sakhīm ūṣām kautūhala samanvitā kam tvam mṛgayase su bhru kīdṛśaḥ te manorathaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ kaścid naraḥ svapne śyāmaḥ kamala locanaḥ pīta vāsāḥ bṛhat bāhuḥ yoṣitām hṛdayaṃgamaḥ tam aham mṛgaye kāntam pāyayitvā adharam madhu kvāpi yātaḥ spṛhayatīm kṣiptvā mām vṛjina arṇave vyasanam te apakarṣāmi tri lokyām yadi bhāvyate tam āneṣye varam yaḥ te manaḥ hartā tam ādiśa daitya vidyādharān yakṣān manujān ca yathā alikhat manujeṣu ca sā vṛṣnīn śūram ānakadundubhim vyalikhat rāma kṛṣṇau ca pradyumnam vīkṣya lajjitā aniruddham vilikhitam vīkṣya uṣā vāc mukhī hriyā saḥ asau asau iti prāha smayamānā mahī pate citralekhā tam ājñāya pautram kṛṣṇasya yoginī yayau vihāyasā rājan dvārakām kṛṣṇa pālitām gṛhītvā śoṇita puram sakhyai priyam adarśayat parārdhya vāsaḥ sraj gandha dhūpa dīpa āsana ādibhiḥ pāna bhojana bhakṣyaiḥ ca vākyaiḥ śuśrūṣaṇa arcitaḥ gūḍhaḥ kanyā pure śaśvat pravṛddha snehayā tayā na ahar gaṇān sa bubudhe ūṣayā apahṛta indriyaḥ tām tathā yadu vīreṇa bhujyamānām hata vratām hetubhiḥ cakruḥ āpṛītām duravacchadaiḥ bhaṭāḥ āvedayām cakruḥ rājan te duhituḥ vayam viceṣṭitam lakṣayāma kanyāyāḥ kula dūṣaṇam anapāyibhiḥ asmābhiḥ guptāyāḥ ca gṛhe prabho kanyāyāḥ dūṣaṇam pumbhiḥ duṣprekṣyāyāḥ na vidmahe tatas pravyathitaḥ bāṇaḥ duhituḥ śruta dūṣaṇaḥ tvaritaḥ kanyakāgāram prāptaḥ adrākṣīt yadu udvaham kāma ātmajam tam bhuvana eka sundaram śyāmam piśaṅga ambaram ambuja īkṣaṇam bṛhat bhujam kuṇḍala kuntala tviṣā smita avalokena ca maṇḍita ānanam dīvyantam akṣaiḥ priyayā abhinṛmṇayā tad aṅga saṅga stana kuṅkuma srajam bāhvoḥ dadhānam madhu mallikā āśritām tasya agre āsīnam avekṣya vismitaḥ sa tam praviṣṭam vṛtam ātatāyibhiḥ bhaṭaiḥ anīkaiḥ avalokya mādhavaḥ jighṛkṣayā tān paritas prasarpataḥ śunaḥ yathā śūkara yūthapaḥ ahanat ūṣā bhṛśam śoka viṣāda vihvalā baddham niśamya aśru kala akṣā arautsīt śṛī śukaḥ uvāca apaśyatām ca aniruddham tad bandhūnām ca bhārata catvāraḥ vārṣikāḥ māsāḥ vyatīyuḥ anuśocatām nāradāt tat upākarṇya vārttām baddhasya karma ca prayayuḥ śoṇita puram vṛṣṇayaḥ kṛṣṇa daivatāḥ pradyumnaḥ yuyudhānaḥ ca gadaḥ sāmbaḥ atha sāraṇaḥ nanda upananda bhadra ādyāḥ rāma kṛṣṇa anuvartinaḥ akṣauhiṇībhiḥ dvādaśabhiḥ sametāḥ sarvatas diśam rurudhuḥ bāṇa nagaram samantāt sātvata ṛṣabhāḥ bhajyamāna pura udyāna prākāra aṭṭāla gopuram prekṣamāṇaḥ ruṣā āviṣṭaḥ tulya sainyaḥ abhiniryayau bāṇa arthe bhagavant rudraḥ sa sutaḥ pramathaiḥ vṛtaḥ āruhya nandi vṛṣabham yuyudhe rāma kṛṣṇayoḥ āsīt su tumulam yuddham adbhutam roma harṣaṇam kṛṣṇa śaṅkarayoḥ rājan pradyumna guhayoḥ api kumbhāṇḍa kūpakarṇābhyām balena saha saṃyugaḥ sāmbasya bāṇa putreṇa bāṇena saha sātyakeḥ brahma ādayaḥ sura adhīśāḥ munayaḥ siddha cāraṇāḥ gandharva apsarasaḥ yakṣāḥ vimānaiḥ draṣṭum āgaman śaṅkara anucarān śauriḥ bhūta pramatha guhyakān ḍākinīḥ yātudhānān ca vetālān sa vināyakān preta mātṛ piśācān ca kuṣmāṇḍān brahma rākṣasān drāvayām āsa tīkṣṇa agraiḥ śaraiḥ śārṅga dhanuḥ cyutaiḥ pṛthagvidhāni prāyuṅkta piṇākī astrāṇi śārṅgiṇe prati astraiḥ śamayām āsa śārṅga pāṇiḥ avismitaḥ āgneyasya ca pārjanyam naijam pāśupatasya ca mohayitvā tu giriśam jṛmbhaṇa astreṇa jṛmbhitam bāṇasya pṛtanām śauriḥ jaghāna asi gadā iṣubhiḥ asṛj vimuñcan gātrebhyaḥ śikhinā apakramat raṇāt kumbhāṇḍa kūpakarṇaḥ ca petatuḥ musala arditau viśīryamāṇam sva balam dṛṣṭvā bāṇaḥ ati amarṣitaḥ dhanūṃṣi ākṛṣya yugapad bāṇaḥ pañca śatāni vai sārathim ratham aśvān ca hatvā śaṅkham apūrayat tad mātā koṭarā nāma nagnā makta śiroruhā puras avatasthe kṛṣṇasya putra prāṇa rirakṣayā bāṇaḥ ca tāvat virathaḥ chinna dhanvā aviśat puram vidrāvite bhūta gaṇe jvaraḥ tu trī śirāḥ trī pād abhyadhāvata dāśārham dahan iva diśaḥ daśa atha nārāyaṇaḥ devaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā vyasṛjat jvaram māheśvaraḥ vaiṣṇavaḥ ca yuyudhāte jvarau ubhau māheśvaraḥ samākrandan vaiṣṇavena bala arditaḥ śaraṇa arthī hṛṣīkeśam tuṣṭāva prayata añjaliḥ namāmi tvā ananta śaktim para īśam sarva ātmānam kevalam jñapti mātram kālaḥ daivam karma jīvaḥ svabhāvaḥ dravyam kṣetram prāṇaḥ ātmā vikāraḥ tad saṅghātaḥ bīja roha pravāhaḥ tvad māyā eṣā tad niṣedham prapadye nānā bhāvaiḥ līlayā eva upapannaiḥ devān sādhūn loka setūn bibharṣi haṃsi unmārgān hiṃsayā vartamānān janma etat te bhāra hārāya bhūmeḥ taptaḥ aham te tejasā duḥsahena śānta ugreṇa ati ulbaṇena jvareṇa tāvat tāpaḥ dehinām te anghri mūlam no severan yāvat āśā anubaddhāḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca bāṇaḥ tu ratham ārūḍhaḥ prāgāt yotsyan janārdanam mumoca parama kruddhaḥ bāṇān cakra āyudhe nṛpa tasya asyataḥ astrāṇi asakṛt cakreṇa kṣura neminā ciccheda bhagavān bāhūn śākhāḥ iva vanaspateḥ bāhuṣu chidyamāneṣu bāṇasya bhagavān bhavaḥ śrī rudraḥ uvāca tvam hi brahma param jyotiḥ gūḍham brahmaṇi vāc maye yam paśyanti amala ātmānaḥ ākāśam iva kevalam dyauḥ śīrṣam āśāḥ śrutiḥ aṅghriḥ urvī romāṇi yasya oṣadhayaḥ ambu vāhāḥ keśāḥ viriñcaḥ dhiṣaṇā visargaḥ tvam ekaḥ ādyaḥ puruṣaḥ advitīyaḥ turyaḥ sva dṛś dhetuḥ ahetuḥ īśaḥ yathā eva sūryaḥ pihitaḥ chāyayā svayā chāyām ca rūpāṇi ca sañcakāsti evam guṇena apihitaḥ guṇān tvam ātma pradīpaḥ guṇinaḥ ca bhūman yat māyā mohita dhiyaḥ putra dāra gṛha ādiṣu yaḥ tvām visṛjate martyaḥ ātmānam priyam īśvaram aham brahmā atha vibudhāḥ munayaḥ ca amala āśayāḥ sarva ātmanā prapannāḥ tvām ātmānam preṣṭham īśvaram samam suhṛd ātma daivam śrī bhagavān uvāca darpa upaśamanāya asya pravṛkṇāḥ bāhavaḥ mayā sūditam ca balam bhūri yat ca bhārāyitam bhuvaḥ catvāraḥ asya bhujāḥ śiṣṭāḥ bhaviṣyati ajara amaraḥ iti labdhvā abhayam kṛṣṇam praṇamya śirasā asuraḥ akṣauhiṇyā parivṛtam su vāsaḥ samalaṅkṛtam sva rājadhānīm samalaṅkṛtām dhvajaiḥ yaḥ evam kṛṣṇa vijayam śaṅkareṇa ca saṃyugam śrī bādarāyaṇiḥ uvāca vihartum sāmba pradyumna cāru bhānu gada ādayaḥ krīḍitvā su ciram tatra vicinvantaḥ pipāsitāḥ kṛkalāsam giri nibham vīkṣya vismita mānasāḥ carma jaiḥ tāntavaiḥ pāśaiḥ baddhvā patitam arbhakāḥ na aśaknuran samuddhartum kṛṣṇāya ācakhyuḥ utsukāḥ tatra āgatya aravinda akṣaḥ bhagavān viśva bhāvanaḥ vīkṣya ujjahāra vāmena tam kareṇa sa līlayā saḥ uttamaḥ śloka kara abhimṛṣṭaḥ vihāya sadyas kṛkalāsa rūpam santapta cāmīkara cāru varṇaḥ svargī adbhuta alaṅkaraṇa ambara sraj kaḥ tvam mahā bhāga vareṇya rūpaḥ deva uttamam tvām gaṇayāmi nūnam daśām imām vā katamena karmaṇā samprāpitaḥ asi a tad arhaḥ su bhadra śrī śukaḥ uvāca iti sma rājā sampṛṣṭaḥ kṛṣṇena ananta mūrtinā mādhavam praṇipatya āha kirīṭena arka varcasā nṛgaḥ uvāca dāniṣu ākhyāyamāneṣu yadi te karṇam aspṛśam kim nu te aviditam nātha sarva bhūta ātma sākṣiṇaḥ kālena avyāhata dṛśaḥ vakṣye atha api tava ājñayā yāvatyaḥ sikatāḥ bhūmeḥ yāvatyaḥ divi tārakāḥ yāvatyaḥ varṣa dhārāḥ ca tāvatīḥ adadam sma gāḥ payasvinīḥ taruṇīḥ śīla rūpa guṇa upapannāḥ kapilāḥ hema sṛṅgīḥ nyāya arjitāḥ rūpya khurāḥ sa vatsāḥ dukūla mālā ābharaṇāḥ dadau aham su alaṅkṛtebhyaḥ guṇa śīlavadbhyaḥ sīdat kuṭumbebhyaḥ ṛta vratebhyaḥ go bhū hiraṇya āyatana aśva hastinaḥ kanyāḥ sa dāsīḥ tila rūpya śayyāḥ vāsāṃsi ratnāni paricchadān rathān iṣṭam ca yajñaiḥ caritam ca pūrtam sampṛktā a viduṣā sā ca mayā dattā dvijātaye tām nīyamānām tad svāmī dṛṣṭrā uvāca mama iti tam gavām lakṣam prakṛṣṭānām dāsyāmi eṣā pradīyatām bhavantau anugṛhṇītām kiṅkarasya a vijānataḥ samuddharatam mām kṛcchrāt patantam niraye aśucau na aham pratīcche vai rājan iti uktvā svāmī apākramat pūrvam tvam aśubham bhuṅkṣe uta aho nṛpate śubham pūrvam deva aśubham bhuñje iti prāha pata iti saḥ tāvat adrākṣam ātmānam kṛkalāsam patan prabho smṛtiḥ na adya api vidhvastā bhavat sandarśana arthinaḥ sa tvam katham mama vibho akṣi pathaḥ parātmā yogeśvaraḥ śruti dṛśām alam hṛt vibhāvyaḥ sākṣāt adhokṣajaḥ uru vyasana andha buddheḥ nārāyaṇa hṛṣīkeśa puṇya śloka acyuta avyaya anujānīhi mām kṛṣṇa yāntam deva gatim prabho kṛṣṇāya vāsudevāya yogānām pataye namaḥ iti uktvā tam parikramya pādau spṛṣṭvā sva maulinā anujñātaḥ vimāna agryam āruhat paśyatām nṛṇām kṛṣṇaḥ parijanam prāha bhagavān devakī sutaḥ brahmaṇyadevaḥ dharma ātmā rājanyān anuśikṣayan tejīyasaḥ api kim uta rājñām īśvara māninām na aham hālāhalam manye viṣam yasya pratikriyā kulam sa mūlam dahati brahma sva araṇi pāvakaḥ brahma svam duranujñātam bhuktam hanti tri pūruṣam prasahya tu balāt bhuktam daśa pūrvān daśa aparān rājānaḥ rāja lakṣmyā andhāḥ na ātma pātam vicakṣate nirayam ye abhimanyante brahma svam sādhu bāliśāḥ gṛhṇanti yāvataḥ pāṃśūn krandatām aśru bindavaḥ viprāṇām hṛta vṛttīnām vadānyānām kuṭumbinām rājānaḥ rāja kulyāḥ ca tāvataḥ abdān niraṅkuśāḥ kumbhī pākeṣu pacyante brahma dāya apahāriṇaḥ sva dattām para dattām vā brahma vṛttim haret ca yaḥ ṣaṣṭi varṣa sahasrāṇi viṣṭhāyām jāyate kṛmiḥ na me brahma dhanam bhūyāt yat gṛdhvā alpa āyuṣaḥ narāḥ parājitāḥ cyutāḥ rājyāt bhavanti udvejinaḥ ahayaḥ vipram kṛta āgasam api na eva druhyata māmakāḥ yathā aham praṇame viprān anukālam samāhitaḥ tathā namata yūyam ca yaḥ anyathā me sa daṇḍa bhāj brāhmaṇa arthaḥ hi apahṛtaḥ hartāram pātayati adhas a jānantam api hi enam nṛgam brāhmaṇa gauḥ iva evam viśrāvya bhagavān mukundaḥ dvārakā okasaḥ pāvanaḥ sarva lokānām viveśa nija mandiram śrī śukaḥ uvāca balabhadraḥ kuru śreṣṭha bhagavān ratham āsthitaḥ rāmaḥ abhivādya pitarā āśīrbhiḥ abhinanditaḥ ciram naḥ pāhi dāśārha sa anujaḥ jagat īśvaraḥ iti āropya aṅkam āliṅgya netraiḥ siṣicatuḥ jalaiḥ gopa vṛddhān ca vidhi vat yaviṣṭhaiḥ abhivanditaḥ samupetya atha gopālān hāsya hasta graha ādibhiḥ viśrāntam sukham āsīnam papracchuḥ paryupāgatāḥ pṛṣṭāḥ ca anāmayam sveṣu prema gadgadayā girā kṛṣṇe kamala pattra akṣe sannyasta akhila rādhasaḥ kaccit smaratha naḥ rāma yūyam dāra suta anvitāḥ diṣṭyā kaṃsaḥ hataḥ pāpaḥ diṣṭyā muktāḥ suhṛd janāḥ nihatya nirjitya ripūn diṣṭyā durgam samāśrītāḥ gopyaḥ hasantyaḥ papracchuḥ rāma sandarśana ādṛtāḥ kaccit āste sukham kṛṣṇaḥ pura strī jana vallabhaḥ api asau mātaram draṣṭum sakṛt api āgamiṣyati api vā smarate asmākam anusevām mahā bhujaḥ mātaram pitaram bhrātṝn patīn putrān svasṝn api tāḥ naḥ sadyas parityajya gataḥ sañchinna sauhṛdaḥ katham nu tādṛśam strībhiḥ na śraddhīyeta bhāṣitam vacaḥ kṛta ghnasya budhāḥ pura striyaḥ kim naḥ tad kathayā gopyaḥ kathāḥ kathayata aparāḥ iti prahasitam śaureḥ jalpitam cāru vīkṣitam saṅkarṣaṇaḥ tāḥ kṛṣṇasya sandeśaiḥ hṛdayam gamaiḥ sāntvayām āsa bhagavant nānā anunaya kovidaḥ dvau māsau tatra ca avātsīt madhum mādhavam eva ca rāmaḥ kṣapāsu bhagavān gopīnām ratim āvahan pūrṇa candra kalā mṛṣṭe kaumudī gandha vāyunā varuṇa preṣitā devī vāruṇī vṛkṣa koṭarāt tam gandham madhu dhārāyāḥ vāyunā upahṛtam balaḥ upagīyamānaḥ gandharvaiḥ vanitā śobhi maṇḍale reme kareṇu yūtha īśaḥ māhendraḥ iva vāraṇaḥ gandharvāḥ munayaḥ rāmam tad vīryaiḥ īḍire tadā saḥ ājuhāva yamunām jala krīḍā artham īśvaraḥ nijam vākyam an ādṛtya mattaḥ iti āpagām balaḥ anāgatām hala agreṇa kupitaḥ vicakarṣa ha pāpe tvam mām avajñāya yat na ayāsi mayā a hutā neṣye tvām lāṅgala agreṇa śatadhā kāma cāriṇīm uvāca cakitā vācam patitā pādayoḥ nṛpa yasya eka aṃśena vidhṛtā jagatī jagataḥ pate param bhāvam bhagavataḥ bhagavat mām a jānatīm tatas vyamuñcat yamunām yācitaḥ bhagavān balaḥ vijagāha jalam strībhiḥ kareṇubhiḥ iva ibha rāj kāmam vihṛtya salilāt uttīrṇāya āsīta ambare bhūṣaṇāni mahārhāṇi dadau kāntiḥ śubhām srajam vasitvā vāsasī nīle mālām āmucya kāñcanīm reye su alaṅkṛtaḥ liptaḥ māhendraḥ iva vāraṇaḥ adya api dṛśyate rājan yamunā ākṛṣṭa vartmanā balasya ananta vīryasya vīryam sūcayati iva hi evam sarvā niśā yātāḥ ekā iva ramataḥ vraje śrī śukaḥ uvāca nanda vrajam gate rāme karūṣa adhipatiḥ nṛpa vāsudevaḥ aham iti ajñaḥ dūtam kṛṣṇāya prāhiṇot tvam vāsudevaḥ bhagavān avatīṛnaḥ jagat patiḥ dūtam ca prāhiṇot mandaḥ kṛṣṇāya avyakta vartmane dvārakāyām yathā bālaḥ nṛpaḥ bāla kṛtaḥ abudhaḥ dūtaḥ tu dvārakām etya sabhāyām āsthitam prabhum kṛṣṇam kamala pattra akṣam rāja sandeśam abravīt bhūtānām anukampā artham tvam tu mithyā abhidhām tyaja tyaktvā ehi mām tvam śaraṇam no ced dehi mama āhavam śrī śukaḥ uvāca katthanam tat upākarṇya pauṇḍrakasya alpa medhasaḥ uvāca dūtam bhagavān parihāsa kathām anu mukham tat apidhāya ājña kaṅka gṛdhra vaṭaiḥ vṛtaḥ śayiṣyase hataḥ tatra bhavitā śaraṇam śunām iti dūtaḥ tam ākṣepam svāmine sarvam āharat kṛṣṇaḥ api ratham āsthāya kāśīm upajagāma ha akṣauhiṇībhyām saṃyuktaḥ niścakrāma purāt drutam tasya kāśī patiḥ mitram pārṣṇi grāhaḥ anvayāt nṛpa akṣauhiṇībhiḥ tisṛbhiḥ apaśyat pauṇḍrakam hariḥ śaṅkha ari asi gadā śārṅga śrīvatsa ādi upalakṣitam bibhrāṇam kaustubha maṇim vana mālā vibhūṣitam kauśeya vāsasī pīte vasānam garuḍa dhvajam dṛṣṭvā tam ātmanaḥ tulyam veṣam kṛtrimam āsthitam yathā naṭam raṅga gatam vijahāsa bhṛśam harīḥ śulaiḥ gadābhiḥ parighaiḥ śakti ṛṣṭi prāsa tomaraiḥ asibhiḥ paṭṭiśaiḥ bāṇaiḥ prāharan arayaḥ harim kṛṣṇaḥ tu tat pauṇḍraka kāśirājayoḥ gadā asi cakra iṣubhiḥ ārdayat bhṛśam yathā yuga ante huta bhuj pṛthak prajāḥ āyodhanam tat ratha vāji kuñjara dvipad khara uṣṭraiḥ ariṇa avakhaṇḍitaiḥ babhau citam moda vaham manasvinām ākrīḍanam bhūta pateḥ iva ulbaṇam atha āha pauṇḍrakam śauriḥ bho bho pauṇḍraka yat bhavān dūta vākyena mām āha tāni astraṇi utsṛjāmi te tyājayiṣye abhidhānam me yat tvayā ājña mṛṣā dhṛtam iti kṣiptvā śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ virathīkṛtya pauṇḍrakam śiraḥ avṛścat rathāṅgena vajreṇa indraḥ yathā gireḥ tathā kāśī pateḥ kāyāt śiraḥ utkṛtya patribhiḥ nyapātayat kāśi puryām padma kośam iva anilaḥ evam matsariṇam hatvā pauṇḍrakam sa sakham hariḥ dvārakām āviśat siddhaiḥ gīyamāna kathā amṛtaḥ śiraḥ patitam ālokya rāja dvāre sa kuṇḍalam kim idam kasya vā vaktram iti saṃśiśire janāḥ rājñaḥ kāśī pateḥ jñātvā mahiṣyaḥ putra bāndhavāḥ paurāḥ ca hā hatāḥ rājan nātha nātha iti prārudan sudakṣiṇaḥ tasya sutaḥ kṛtvā saṃsthā vidhim pateḥ nihatya pitṛ hantāram yāsyāmi apacitim pituḥ iti ātmanā abhisandhāya sa upādhyāyaḥ maheśvaram su dakṣiṇaḥ arcayām āsa parameṇa samādhinā dakṣiṇāgnim paricara brāhmaṇaiḥ samam ṛtvijam abhicāra vidhānena sa ca agniḥ pramathaiḥ vṛtaḥ iti ādiṣṭaḥ tathā cakre kṛṣṇāya abhicaran vratī tatas agniḥ utthitaḥ kuṇḍāt mūrtimān ati bhīṣaṇaḥ tapta tāmra śikhā śmaśruḥ aṅgāra udgāri locanaḥ daṃṣṭra ugra bhru kuṭī daṇḍa kaṭhora āsyaḥ sva jihvayā ālihan sṛkvaṇī nagnaḥ vidhunvan tri śikham jvalat padbhyām tāla pramāṇābhyām kampayan avanī talam saḥ abhyadhāvat vṛtaḥ bhūtaiḥ dvārakām pradahan diśaḥ tam ābhicāra dahanam āyāntam dvārakā okāḥ akṣaiḥ sabhāyām krīḍantam bhagavantam bhaya āturāḥ śrutvā tat jana vaiklavyam dṛṣṭvā svānām ca sādhvasam śaraṇyaḥ samprahasya āha mā bhaiṣṭa iti avitāsmi aham sarvasya antar bahis sākṣī kṛtyām māheśvarīm vibhuḥ vijñāya tad vighāta artham pārśva stham cakram ādiśat kṛtyā analaḥ pratihataḥ sa rathānga pāṇeḥ vārāṇasīm parisametya sudakṣiṇam tam cakram ca viṣṇoḥ tad anupraviṣṭam vārānasīm sa aṭṭa sabhā ālaya āpaṇām sa gopura aṭṭālaka koṣṭha saṅkulām sa kośa hasti aśva ratha anna śālinīm dagdhvā vārāṇasīm sarvām viṣṇoḥ cakram sudarśanam bhūyas pārśvam upātiṣṭhat kṛṣṇasya akliṣṭa karmaṇaḥ samāhitaḥ vā śṛṇuyāt sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate śrī rājā uvāca bhuyaḥ aham śrotum icchāmi rāmasya adbhuta karmaṇaḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca pura grāma ākarān ghoṣān adahat vahnim utsṛjan kvacid sa śailān utpāṭya taiḥ deśān samacūrṇayat ānartān sutarām eva yatra āste mitra hā hariḥ deśāt nāga ayuta prāṇaḥ velā kūle nyamajjayat āśramān ṛṣi mukhyānām kṛtvā bhagna vanaspatīn adūṣayat śakṛt mūtraiḥ agnīn vaitānikān khalaḥ puruṣān yoṣitaḥ dṛptaḥ kṣmābhṛt dronī guhāsu saḥ nikṣipya ca api adhāt śailaiḥ peśaṣkārī iva kīṭakam evam deśān viprakurvan dūṣayan ca kula striyaḥ śrutvā su lalitam gītam girim raivatakam yayau tatra apaśyat yadu patim rāmam puṣkara mālinam su darśanīya sarva aṅgam lalanā yūtha madhya gam gāyantam vāruṇīm pītvā mada vihvala locanam vibhrājamānam vapuṣā prabhinnam iva vāraṇam duṣṭaḥ śākhā mṛgaḥ śākhām ārūḍhaḥ kampayan drumān cakre kilakilā śabdam ātmānam sampradarśayan tasya dhārṣṭyam kapeḥ vīkṣya taruṇyaḥ jāti cāpalāḥ tāḥ helayām āsa kapiḥ bhrū kṣepaiḥ sammukha ādibhiḥ darśayan sva gudam tāsām rāmasya ca nirīkṣitaḥ tam grāvṇā prāharat kruddhaḥ balaḥ praharatām varaḥ sa vañcayitvā grāvāṇam madirā kalaśam kapiḥ gṛhītvā helayām āsa dhūrtaḥ tam kopayan hasan nirbhidya kalaśam duṣṭaḥ vāsāṃsi āsphālayat balam tam tasya avinayam dṛṣṭvā deśān ca tad upadrutān kruddhaḥ musalam ādatta halam ca ari jighāṃsayā dvividaḥ api mahā vīryaḥ śālam udyamya pāṇinā tam tu saṅkarṣaṇaḥ mūrdhni patantam acalaḥ yathā mūṣala āhata mastiṣkaḥ vireje rakta dhārayā punar anyam samutkṣipya kṛtvā niṣpattram ojasā tatas anyena ruṣā jaghne tam ca api śatadhā ācchinat ākṛṣya sarvatas vṛkṣān nirvṛkṣam akarot vanam tat sarvam cūrṇayām āsa līlayā musalāyudhaḥ sa bāhū tāla saṅkāśau muṣṭī kṛtya kapi īśvaraḥ āsādya rohiṇī putram tābhyām vakṣasi arūrujat yādava indraḥ api tam dorbhyām tyaktvā musala lāṅgale parvataḥ kuru śārdūla vāyunā nauḥ iva ambhasi jaya śabdaḥ namaḥ śabdaḥ sādhu sādhu iti ca ambare sura siddha muni indrāṇām āsīt kusuma varṣiṇām saṃstūyamānaḥ bhagavān janaiḥ sva puram āviśat śrī śukaḥ uvāca duryodhana sutām rājan lakṣmaṇām samitiṃjayaḥ svayaṃvara sthām aharat sāmbaḥ jāmbavatī sutaḥ kauravāḥ kupitāḥ ūcuḥ durvinītaḥ ayam arbhakaḥ kadarthīkṛtya naḥ kanyām akāmām aharat balāt badhnīta imam durvinītam kim kariṣyanti vṛṣṇayaḥ ye asmad prasāda upacitām dattām naḥ bhuñjate mahīm nigṛhītam sutam śrutvā yadi eṣyanti iha vṛṣṇayaḥ bhagna darpāḥ śamam yānti prāṇāḥ iva su saṃyatāḥ iti karṇaḥ śalaḥ bhūriḥ yajñaketuḥ suyodhanaḥ sāmbam ārebhire yoddhum kuru vṛddha anumoditāḥ dṛṣṭvā anudhāvataḥ sāmbaḥ dhārtarāṣṭrān mahā rathaḥ tam te jighṛkṣavaḥ kruddhāḥ tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti bhāṣiṇaḥ āsādya dhanvinaḥ bāṇaiḥ karṇāgraṇyaḥ samākiran na amṛṣyat tat acintya arbhaḥ siṃha kṣudra mṛgaiḥ iva visphūrjya ruciram cāpam sarvān vivyādha sāyakaiḥ karṇa ādīn ṣaṭ rathān vīraḥ tāvadbhiḥ yugapad pṛthak tam tu te viratham cakruḥ catvāraḥ caturaḥ hayān kumāram svasya kanyām ca sva puram jayinaḥ aviśan sāntvayitvā tu tān rāmaḥ sannaddhān vṛṣṇi puṅgavān na aicchat kurūṇām vṛṣṇīnām kalim kali mala apahaḥ brāhmaṇaiḥ kula vṛddhaiḥ ca vṛtaḥ candraḥ iva grahaiḥ gatvā gajāhvayam rāmaḥ bāhya upavanam āsthitaḥ uddhavam preṣayām āsa dhṛtarāṣṭram bubhutsayā saḥ abhivandya ambikā putram bhīṣmam droṇam ca bāhlikam te ati prītāḥ tam ākarṇya prāptam rāmam suhṛttamam tam arcayitvā abhiyayuḥ sarve maṅgala pāṇayaḥ tam saṅgamya yathā nyāyam gām arghyam ca nyavedayan teṣām ye tad prabhāva jñāḥ praṇemuḥ śirasā balam bandhūn kuśalinaḥ śrutvā pṛṣṭvā śivam anāmayam ugrasenaḥ kṣiteśa īśaḥ yat vaḥ ājñāpayat prabhuḥ abadhnīta atha tat mṛṣye bandhūnām aikya kāmyayā ete yaunena sambaddhāḥ saha śayyā āsana aśanāḥ vṛṣṇayaḥ tulya tām nītāḥ asmad datta nṛpāsanāḥ cāmara vyajane śaṅkham ātapatram ca pāṇḍuram kirīṭam āsanam śayyām bhuñjate asmad upekṣayā alam yadūnām naradeva lāñchanaiḥ dātuḥ pratīpaiḥ phaṇinām iva amṛtam śrī bādarāyaṇiḥ uvāca āśrāvya rāmam durvācyam asabhyāḥ puram āviśan dṛṣṭvā kurūnām dauḥśīlyam śrutvā avācyāni ca acyutaḥ nūnam nānā mada unnaddhāḥ śāntim na icchanti asādhavaḥ teṣām hi praśamaḥ daṇḍaḥ paśūnām laguḍaḥ yathā aho yadūn su saṃrabdhān kṛṣṇam ca kupitam śanais sāntvayitvā aham eteṣām śamam icchan iha āgataḥ te ime manda matayaḥ kalaha abhiratāḥ khalāḥ tam mām avajñāya muhur durbhāṣān māninaḥ abruvan śakra ādayaḥ loka pālāḥ yasya ādeśa anuvartinaḥ sudharmā ākramyate yena pārijātaḥ amara aṅghripaḥ ānīya bhujyate saḥ asau na kila adhyāsana arhaṇaḥ yasya pāda yugam sākṣāt śrīḥ upāste akhila īśvarā brahmā bhavaḥ aham api yasya kalāḥ kalāyāḥ śrīḥ ca udvahema ciram asya nṛpāsanam kva bhuñjate kurubhiḥ dattam bhū khaṇḍam vṛṣṇayaḥ kila upānahaḥ kila vayam svayam tu kuravaḥ śiraḥ aho aiśvarya mattānām mattānām iva māninām asaṃbaddhāḥ giṛaḥ rukṣāḥ kaḥ saheta anuśāsīta adya niṣkauravam pṛthvīm kariṣyāmi iti amarṣitaḥ lāṅgala agreṇa nagaram udvidārya gajāhvayam vicakarṣa sa gaṅgāyām prahariṣyan amarṣitaḥ jala yānam iva āghūrṇam gaṅgāyām nagaram patat ākṛṣyamāṇam ālokya kauravāḥ jāta sambhramāḥ tam eva śaraṇam jagmuḥ sa kuṭumbāḥ jijīviṣavaḥ sa lakṣmaṇam puras kṛtya sa ambam prāñjalayaḥ prabhum rāma rāma akhila ādhāra prabhāvam na vidāma te mūḍhānām naḥ ku buddhīnām kṣantum arhasi atikramam lokān krīḍanakān īśa krīḍataḥ te vadanti hi tvam eva mūrdhni idam ananta līlayā bhū maṇḍalam bibharṣi sahasra mūrdhan ante ca yaḥ sva ātma niruddha viśvaḥ śeṣe advitīyaḥ pariśiṣyamāṇaḥ kopaḥ te akhila śikṣā artham na dveṣāt na ca matsarāt viśva karman namaḥ te astu tvām vayam śaraṇam gatāḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca duryodhanaḥ pāribarham kuñjarān ṣaṣṭi hāyanān dadau ca dvādaśa śatāni ayutāni turaṅgamān rathānām ṣaṣ sahasrāṇi raukmāṇām sūrya varcasām dāsīnām niṣka kaṇṭhīnām sahasram duhitṛ vatsalaḥ sa sutaḥ sa snuṣaḥ prāyāt suhṛdbhiḥ abhinanditaḥ tatas praviṣṭaḥ sva puram halāyudhaḥ śaśaṃsa sarvam yadu puṅgavānām madhye sabhāyām kuruṣu sva ceṣṭitam samunnatam dakṣiṇatas gaṅgāyām anudṛśyate śrī śukaḥ uvāca narakam nihatam śrutvā tathā udvāham ca yoṣitām kṛṣṇena ekena bahvīnām tad didṛkṣuḥ sma nāradaḥ gṛheṣu dvi aṣṭa sāhasram striyaḥ eke udāvahat iti utsukaḥ dvāravatīm devarṣiḥ draṣṭum āgamat puṣpita upavana ārāma dvija ali kula nāditām churiteṣu saraḥsu uccais kūjitām haṃsa sārasaiḥ prāsāda lakṣaiḥ navabhiḥ juṣṭām sphāṭika rājataiḥ vibhakta rathyā patha catvara āpaṇaiḥ śālā sabhābhiḥ rucirām surālayaiḥ saṃsikta mārga aṅgana vīthi dehalīm patat patāka dhvaja vārita ātapām tasyām antaḥpuram śrīmat arcitam sarva dhiṣṇya paiḥ hareḥ sva kauśalam yatra tvaṣṭrā kārtsnyena darśitam tatra ṣoḍaśabhiḥ sadma sahasraiḥ samalaṅkṛtam viveśa ekatomam śaureḥ patnīnām bhavanam mahat indranīla mayaiḥ kuḍyaiḥ jagatyā ca ahata tviṣā vitānaiḥ nirmitaiḥ tvaṣṭrā muktā dāma vilambibhiḥ dāntaiḥ āsana paryaṅkaiḥ maṇi uttama pariṣkṛtaiḥ dāsībhiḥ niṣka kaṇṭhībhiḥ su vāsobhiḥ alaṅkṛtam pumbhiḥ sa kañcuka uṣṇīṣa su vastra maṇi kuṇḍalaiḥ tasmin samāna guṇa rūpa vayaḥ su veṣa dāsī sahasra yutayā anusavam gṛhiṇyā daṇḍena sātvata patim parivījayantyā tam san nirīkṣya bhagavān sahasā utthita śrī paryaṅkataḥ sakala dharma bhṛtām variṣṭhaḥ ānamya pāda yugalam śirasā kirīṭa juṣṭena sa añjaliḥ avīviśat āsane sve sampūjya deva ṛṣi varyam ṛṣiḥ purāṇaḥ vāṇyā abhibhāṣya mitayā amṛta miṣṭayā tam śrī nāradaḥ uvāca maitrī janeṣu sakaleṣu damaḥ khalānām niḥśreyasāya hi jagat sthiti rakṣaṇābhyām svaira avatāraḥ urugāya vidāma suṣṭhu dṛṣṭam tava aṅghri yugalam janatā apavargam saṃsāra kūpa patita uttaraṇa avalambam dhyāyan carāmi anugṛhāṇa yathā smṛtiḥ syāt tatas anyat āviśat geham kṛṣṇa patnyāḥ sa nāradaḥ yogeśvara īśvarasya aṅga yoga māyā vivitsayā pūjitaḥ parayā bhaktyā pratyutthāna āsana ādibhiḥ pṛṣṭaḥ ca avidvasā iva asau kadā āyātaḥ bhavān iti kriyate kim nu pūrṇānām apūrṇaiḥ asmad ādibhiḥ sa tu vismitaḥ utthāya tūṣṇīm anyat agāt gṛham tatra api acaṣṭa govindam lālayantam sutān śiśūn juhvantam ca vitāna agnīn yajantam pañcabhiḥ makhaiḥ bhojayantam dvijān kvāpi bhuñjānam avaśeṣitam kvāpi sandhyām upāsīnam japantam brahma vāc yatam kvacid śayānam paryaṅke stūyamānam ca vandibhiḥ jala krīḍā ratam kvāpi vāramukhyā bala āvṛtam kutracid dvija mukhyebhyaḥ dadatam gāḥ su alaṅkṛtāḥ itihāsa purāṇāni śṛṇvantam maṅgalāni ca hasantam hāsa kathayā kadācid priyayā gṛhe dhyāyantam ekam āsīnam puruṣam prakṛteḥ param śuśrūṣantam gurūn kvāpi kāmaiḥ bhogaiḥ saparyayā kutra api saha rāmeṇa cintayantam satām śivam putrāṇām duhitṝṇām ca kāle vidhi upayāpanam dāraiḥ varaiḥ tad sadṛśaiḥ kalpayantam vibhūtibhiḥ vīkṣya yogeśvara īśasya yeṣām lokāḥ visismire pūrtayantam kvacid dharmam kūrpārāma maṭha ādibhiḥ ghnantam tatra paśūn medhyān parītam yadu puṅgavaiḥ avyakta lingam prakṛtiṣu antar pura gṛha ādiṣu atha uvāca hṛṣīkeśam nāradaḥ prahasan iva yoga māyā udayam vīkṣya mānuṣām īyivasaḥ gatim vidāma yoga māyāḥ te durdarśāḥ api māyinām yoga īśvara ātman nirbhātā bhavat pāda niṣevayā anujānīhi mām deva lokān te yaśasā āplutān paryaṭāmi tava udgāyan līlāḥ bhuvana pāvanīḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca śrī śukaḥ uvāca iti ācarantam sat dharmān pāvanān gṛha medhinām kṛṣṇasya ananta vīryasya yoga māyā mahā udayam muhur dṛṣṭvā ṛṣiḥ abhūt vismitaḥ jāta kautukaḥ iti artha kāma dharmeṣu kṛṣṇena śraddhita ātmanā evam manuṣya padavīm anuvartamānaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ akhila bhavāya gṛhīta śaktiḥ reme aṇga ṣoḍaśa sahasra vara aṅganānām sa vrīḍa sauhṛda nirīkṣaṇa hāsa juṣṭaḥ yāni iha viśva vilaya udbhava vṛtti hetuḥ karmāṇi ananya viṣayāṇi harīḥ cakāra yaḥ tu aṅga gāyati śṛṇoti anumodate vā śrī śukaḥ uvāca atha uṣasi upavṛttāyām kukkuṭān kūjataḥ aśapan gṛhīta kaṇṭhyaḥ patibhiḥ mādhavyaḥ viraha āturāḥ vayāṃsi aroruvan kṛṣṇam bodhayanti iva vandinaḥ gāyatsu aliṣu anidrāṇi mandāra vana vāyubhiḥ muhūrtam tam tu vaidarbhī na amṛṣyat ati śobhanam parirambhaṇa viśleṣāt priya bāhu antaram gatā brāhme muhūrte utthāya vāri upaspṛśya mādhavaḥ kriyā kalāpam paridhāya vāsasī upasthāya arkam udyantam tarpayitvā ātmanaḥ kalāḥ devān ṛṣīn pitṝn vṛddhān viprān abhyarcya ca ātmavān dhenūnām rukma śṛṅgīnām sādhvīnām mauktika srajām payasvinīnām gṛṣṭīnām sa vatsānām su vāsasām dadau rūpya khura agrāṇām kṣauma ajina tilaiḥ saha go vipra devatā vṛddha gurūn bhūtāni sarvaśas namaskṛtya ātma sambhūtīḥ maṅgalāni samaspṛśat ātmānam bhūṣayām āsa nara loka vibhūṣaṇam vāsobhiḥ bhūṣaṇaiḥ svīyaiḥ divya sraj anulepanaiḥ avekṣya ājyam tathā ādarśam go vṛṣa dvija devatāḥ kāmān ca sarva varṇānām paura antar pura cāriṇām pradāpya prakṛtīḥ kāmaiḥ pratoṣya pratyanandata saṃvibhajya agratas viprān sraj tāmbūla anulepanaiḥ suhṛdaḥ prakṛtīḥ dārān upāyuṅkta tatas svayam tāvat sūtaḥ upānīya syandanam parama adbhutam gṛhītvā pāṇinā pāṇī sāratheḥ tam atha āruhat sātyaki uddhava saṃyuktaḥ pūrva adrim iva bhāskaraḥ īkṣitaḥ antar pura strīṇām sa vrīḍa prema vīkṣitaiḥ kṛcchrāt visṛṣṭaḥ niragāt jāta hāsaḥ haran manaḥ sudharma ākhyām sabhām sarvaiḥ vṛṣṇibhiḥ parivāritaḥ prāviśat yat niviṣṭānām na santi aṅga ṣaṭ ūrmayaḥ vṛtaḥ nṛ siṃhaiḥ yadubhiḥ yadu uttamaḥ yathā uḍu rājaḥ divi tārakā gaṇaiḥ upatasthuḥ naṭa ācāryāḥ nartakyaḥ tāṇḍavaiḥ pṛthak mṛdaṅga vīṇā muraja veṇu tāla dara svanaiḥ nanṛtuḥ jaguḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ ca sūta māgadha vandinaḥ tatra āhuḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kecid āsīnāḥ brahma vādinaḥ pūrveṣām puṇya yaśasām rājñām ca akathayan kathāḥ tatra ekaḥ puruṣaḥ rājan āgataḥ apūrva darśanaḥ vijñāpitaḥ bhagavate pratīhāraiḥ praveśitaḥ sa namaskṛtya kṛṣṇāya pareśāya kṛtāñjaliḥ rājñām āvedayat duḥkham jarāsandha nirodha jam rājānaḥ ūcuḥ kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa aprameya ātman prapanna bhaya bhañjana vayam tvām śaraṇam yāmaḥ bhava bhītāḥ pṛthak dhiyaḥ yaḥ tāvat asya balavān iha jīvita āśām loke bhavān jagat inaḥ kalayā avatīrṇaḥ sat rakṣaṇāya khala nigrahaṇāya ca anyaḥ kaścid tvadīyam atiyāti nideśam īśa kim vā janaḥ sva kṛtam ṛcchati tat na vidmaḥ svapnāyitam nṛpa sukham para tantram īśa śaśvat bhayena mṛtakena dhuram vahāmaḥ kliśyāmahe ati kṛpaṇāḥ tava māyayā iha baddhān viyuṅkṣva magadha āhvaya karma pāśāt bibhrat rurodha bhavane mṛga rāj iva āvīḥ jitvā nṛ loka niratam sakṛt ūḍha darpaḥ dūtaḥ uvāca iti māgadha saṃruddhāḥ bhavat darśana kaṅkṣiṇaḥ prapannāḥ pāda mūlam te dīnānām śam vidhīyatām śrī śukaḥ uvāca rāja dūte bruvati evam devarṣiḥ parama dyutiḥ bibhrat piṅga jaṭā bhāram prādurāsīt yathā raviḥ tam dṛṣṭvā bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ sarva loka īśvara īśvaraḥ vavanda utthitaḥ śīrṣṇā sa sabhyaḥ sa anugaḥ mudā babhāṣe su nṛtaiḥ vākyaiḥ śraddhayā tarpayan munim api svid adya lokānām trayāṇām akutobhayam nanu bhūyān bhagavataḥ lokān paryaṭataḥ guṇaḥ na hi te aviditam kiñcid lokeṣu īśvara kartṛṣu atha pṛcchāmahe yuṣmān pāṇḍavānām cikīrṣitam śrī nāradaḥ uvāca dṛṣṭā māyā te bahuśas duratyayā māyāḥ vibho viśva sṛjaḥ ca māyinaḥ jīvasya yaḥ saṃsarataḥ vimokṣaṇam na jānataḥ anartha vahāt śarīrataḥ līlāvatāraiḥ sva yaśaḥ pradīpakam prājvālayat tvā tam aham prapadye rājñaḥ paitṛṣvasreyasya bhaktasya ca cikīrṣitam yakṣyati tvām makha indreṇa rājasūyena pāṇḍavaḥ pārameṣṭhya kāmaḥ nṛpatiḥ tat bhavān anumodatām didṛkṣavaḥ sameṣyanti rājānaḥ ca yaśasvinaḥ śravaṇāt kīrtanāt dhyānāt pūyante antevasāyinaḥ yasya amalam divi yaśaḥ prathitam rasāyām gaṅgā iti ca iha caraṇa ambu punāti viśvam śrī śukaḥ uvāca tatra teṣu ātma pakṣeṣu a gṛṇatsu vijigīṣayā vācaḥ smayan bhṛtyam uddhavam prāha keśavaḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca tvam hi naḥ paramam cakṣuḥ suhṛd mantra artha tattva vid atha atra brūhi anuṣṭheyam śraddadhmaḥ karavāma tat nideśam śirasā ādhāya uddhavaḥ pratyabhāṣata śrī śukaḥ uvāca iti udīritam ākarṇya devaṛṣeḥ uddhavaḥ abravīt sabhyānām matam ājñāya kṛṣṇasya ca mahā matiḥ śrī uddhavaḥ uvāca yat uktam ṛṣinā deva sācivyam yakṣyataḥ tvayā kāryam paitṛ ṣvasreyasya rakṣā ca śaraṇa eṣiṇām yaśaḥ ca tava govinda rājñaḥ baddhān vimuñcataḥ balinām api ca anyeṣām bhīmam sama balam vinā dvai rathe sa tu jetavyaḥ mā śata akṣauhiṇī yutaḥ brahma veṣa dharaḥ gatvā tam bhikṣeta vṛkodaraḥ hiraṇyagarbhaḥ śarvaḥ ca kālasya arūpiṇaḥ tava rājñām sva śatru vadham ātma vimokṣaṇam ca gopyaḥ ca kuñjara pateḥ janakātmajāyāḥ pitroḥ ca labdha śaraṇāḥ munayaḥ vayam ca jarāsandha vadhaḥ kṛṣṇa bhūri arthāya upakalpate prāyas pāka vipākena tava ca abhimataḥ kratuḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca devarṣiḥ yadu vṛddhāḥ ca kṛṣṇaḥ ca pratyapūjayan atha ādiśat prayāṇāya bhagavant devakī sutaḥ bhṛtyān dāruka jaitra ādīn anujñāpya gurūn vibhuḥ saṅkarṣaṇam anujñāpya yadu rājam ca śatru han karālayā parivṛtaḥ ātma senayā mṛdaṅga bherī ānaka śaṅkha gomukhaiḥ nṛ vāji kāñcana śibikābhiḥ acyutam saha ātmajāḥ patim anu su vratāḥ yayuḥ vara ambara ābharaṇa vilepana srajaḥ su saṃvṛtāḥ nṛbhiḥ asi carma pāṇibhiḥ nara uṣṭra go mahiṣa khara aśvatarī anaḥ kareṇubhiḥ parijana vāra yoṣitaḥ su alaṅkṛtāḥ kaṭa kuṭi kambala ambara ādi vara āyudha ābharaṇa kirīṭa varmabhiḥ yathā arṇavaḥ kṣubhita timiṅgila ūrmibhiḥ rāja dūtam uvāca idam bhagavān prīṇayan girā mā bhaiṣṭa dūta bhadram vaḥ ghātayiṣyāmi māgadham te api sandarśanam śaureḥ pratyaikṣan yat mumukṣavaḥ ānarta sauvīra marūn tīrtvā vinaśanam hariḥ girīn nadīḥ atīyāya pura grāma vraja ākarān tatas dṛṣadvatīm tīrtvā mukundaḥ atha sarasvatīm pañcālān atha matsyān ca śakraprastham atha agamat tam upāgatam ākarṇya prītaḥ durdarśanam nṛnām ajāta śatruḥ niragāt sa upadhyāyaḥ suhṛd vṛtaḥ gīta vāditra ghoṣeṇa brahma ghoṣeṇa bhūyasā abhyayāt sa hṛṣīkeśam prāṇāḥ prāṇam iva ādṛtaḥ dṛṣṭvā viklinna hṛdayaḥ kṛṣṇam snehena pāṇḍavaḥ cirāt dṛṣṭam priyatamam sasvaje atha punar punar dorbhyām pariṣvajya ramā amala ālayam mukunda gātram nṛpatiḥ hata aśubhaḥ yamau kirīṭī ca suhṛttamam mudā pravṛddha bāṣpāḥ parirebhire acyutam brāhmaṇebhyaḥ namaskṛtya vṛddhebhyaḥ ca yathārhatas māninaḥ mānayām āsa kuru sṛñjaya kaikayān mṛdaṅga śaṅkha paṭaha vīṇā paṇava gomukhaiḥ brāhmaṇāḥ ca aravinda akṣam tuṣṭuvuḥ nanṛtuḥ jaguḥ evam suhṛdbhiḥ paryastaḥ puṇya śloka śikhāmaṇiḥ saṃstūyamānaḥ bhagavān viveśa alaṅkṛtam puram mṛṣṭa ātmabhiḥ nava dukūla vibhūṣaṇa sraj juṣṭam dadarśa bhavanaiḥ kuru rāja dhāma kṛṣṇam sa bhāryam upalabhya gṛha adhirūḍhāḥ ūcuḥ striyaḥ pathi nirīkṣya mukunda patnīḥ tārā yathā uḍupa sahāḥ kim akāri amūbhiḥ yat cakṣuṣām puruṣa mauliḥ udāra hāsa tatra tatra upasaṅgamya paurāḥ maṅgala pāṇayaḥ cakruḥ saparyām kṛṣṇāya śreṇi mukhyāḥ hata enasaḥ pṛthā vilokya bhrātreyam kṛṣṇam tri bhuvana īśvaram prīta ātmā utthāya paryaṅkāt sa snuṣā pariṣasvaje govindam gṛham ānīya deva deveśam ādṛtaḥ pūjāyām na avidat kṛtyam pramoda upahataḥ nṛpaḥ pitṛ svasuḥ guru strīṇām kṛṣṇaḥ cakre abhivādanam svayam ca kṛṣṇayā rājan bhaginyā ca abhivanditaḥ śvaśṛvā sañcoditā kṛṣṇā kṛṣṇa patnīḥ ca sarvaśas ānarca rukmiṇīm satyām bhadrām jāmbavatīm tathā kālindīm mitravindām ca śaibyām nāgnajitīm satīm anyāḥ ca abhyāgatāḥ yāḥ tu vāsaḥ sraj maṇḍana ādibhiḥ sukham nivāsayām āsa dharma rājaḥ janārdanam sa sainyam sa anuga amatyam sa bhāryam ca navam navam tarpayitvā khāṇḍavena vahnim phālguna saṃyutaḥ mocayitvā mayam yena rājñe divyā sabhā kṛtā uvāsa katicid māsān rājñaḥ priya cikīrṣayā śrī śukaḥ uvāca brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyaiḥ vaiśyaiḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ ca yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ācāryaiḥ kula vṛddhaiḥ ca jñāti sambandhi bāndhavaiḥ śṛṇvatām eva ca eteṣām ābhāṣya idam uvāca ha śrī yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca kratu rājena govinda rājasūyena pāvanīḥ āśāsate yadi te āśiṣaḥ īśa na anye sevā anubhāvam iha paśyatu lokaḥ eṣaḥ niṣṭhām pradarśaya vibho kuru sṛñjayānām sarva ātmanaḥ sama dṛśaḥ sva sukha anubhūteḥ saṃsevatām sura taroḥ iva te prasādaḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca kalyāṇī yena te kīrtiḥ lokān anubhaviṣyati ṛṣīṇām pitṛ devānām suhṛdām api naḥ prabho sarveṣām api bhūtānām īpsitaḥ kratu rāj ayam vijitya nṛpatīn sarvān kṛtvā ca jagatīm vaśe ete te bhrātaraḥ rājan loka pāla aṃśa sambhavāḥ jitaḥ asmi ātmavatā te aham durjayaḥ yaḥ akṛtātmabhiḥ na kaścid mad param loke tejasā yaśasā śriyā śrī śukaḥ uvāca niśamya bhagavat gītam prītaḥ phulla mukha ambujaḥ bhrātṝn diś vijaye ayuṅkta viṣṇu teja upabṛṃhitān sahadevam dakṣiṇasyām ādiśat saha sṛñjayaiḥ diśi pratīcyām nakulam udīcyām savyasācinam prācyām vṛkodaram matsyaiḥ kekayaiḥ saha madrakaiḥ te vijitya nṛpān vīrāḥ ājahruḥ digbhyaḥ ojasā ajāta śatrave bhūri draviṇam nṛpa yakṣyate śrutvā ajitam jarāsandham nṛpateḥ dhyāyataḥ hariḥ bhīmasenaḥ arjunaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ brahma linga dharāḥ trayaḥ te gatvā ātithya velāyām gṛheṣu gṛha medhinam brahmaṇyam samayāceran rājanyāḥ brahma liṅginaḥ rājan viddhi atithīn prāptān arthinaḥ dūram āgatān kim durmarṣam titikṣūṇām kim akāryam asādhubhiḥ kim na deyam vadānyānām kaḥ paraḥ sama darśinām yaḥ anityena śarīreṇa satām geyam yaśaḥ dhruvam na ācinoti svayam kalpaḥ sa vācyaḥ śocyaḥ eva saḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca svaraiḥ ākṛtibhiḥ tān tu prakoṣṭhaiḥ jyā hataiḥ api rājanya bandhūn vijñāya dṛṣṭa pūrvān acintayat baleḥ nu śrūyate kīrtiḥ vitatā dikṣu akalmaṣā aiśvaryāt bhraṃśitasya api vipra vyājena viṣṇunā śriyam jihīrṣatā indrasya viṣṇave dvija rūpiṇe jānan api mahīm prādāt vāryamāṇaḥ api daitya rāj jīvatā brāhmaṇa arthāya kaḥ nu arthaḥ kṣatra bandhunā iti udāra matiḥ prāha kṛṣṇa arjuna vṛkodarān he viprāḥ vriyatām kāmaḥ dadāmi ātma śiraḥ api vaḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca yuddha arthinaḥ vayam prāptāḥ rājanyāḥ na anya kāṅkṣiṇaḥ anayoḥ mātuleyam mām kṛṣṇam jānīhi te ripum evam āveditaḥ rājā jahāsa uccais sma māgadhaḥ āha ca amarṣitaḥ mandāḥ yuddham tarhi dadāmi vaḥ mathurām sva purīm tyaktvā samudram śaraṇam gataḥ iti uktvā bhīmasenāya prādāya mahatīm gadām dvitīyām svayam ādāya nirjagāma purāt bahis jaghnatuḥ vajra kalpābhyām gadābhyām raṇa durmadau maṇḍalāni vicitrāṇi savyam dakṣiṇam eva ca caratoḥ śuśubhe yuddham naṭayoḥ iva raṅgiṇoḥ tatas caṭa caṭā śabdaḥ vajra niṣpesa sannibhaḥ cūrṇībabhūvatuḥ upetya yathā arka śākhe kruddhau sva muṣṭibhiḥ ayaḥ sparaśaiḥ apiṣṭām tayoḥ evam praharatoḥ sama śikṣā bala ojasoḥ nirviśeṣam abhūt yuddham akṣīṇa javayoḥ nṛpa śatroḥ janma mṛtī vidvān jīvitam ca jarā kṛtam sañcintya arī vadha upāyam bhīmasya amogha darśanaḥ darśayām āsa viṭapam pāṭayan iva saṃjñayā tat vijñāya mahā sattvaḥ bhīmaḥ praharatām varaḥ gṛhītvā pādayoḥ śatrum pātayām āsa bhū tale ekam pādam padā ākramya dorbhyām anyam pragṛhya saḥ gudataḥ pāṭayām āsa śākham iva mahā gajaḥ eka pāda ūru vṛṣaṇa kaṭi pṛṣṭha stana aṃsake eka bāhu akṣi bhrū karṇe śakale dadṛśuḥ prajāḥ hāhā kāraḥ mahān āsīt nihate magadha īśvare pūjayām āsatuḥ bhīmam parirabhya jaya acyatau sahadevam tad tanayam bhagavān bhūta bhāvanaḥ abhyaṣiñcat ameya ātmā magadhānām patim prabhuḥ mocayām āsa rājanyān saṃruddhāḥ māgadhena ye śrī śukaḥ uvāca ayute dve śatāni aṣṭau niruddhāḥ yudhi nirjitāḥ te nirgatāḥ giri droṇyām malināḥ mala vāsasaḥ kṣudh kṣāmāḥ śuṣka vadanāḥ saṃrodha parikarśitāḥ dadṛśuḥ te ghana śyāmam pīta kauśeya vāsasam śrīvatsa aṅkam catur bāhum padma garbha aruṇa īkṣaṇam padma hastam gadā śaṅkha rathāṅgaiḥ upalakṣitam kirīṭa hāra kaṭaka kaṭi sūtra aṅgada āñcitam bhrājat vara maṇi grīvam nivītam vana mālayā praṇemuḥ hata pāpmānaḥ mūrdhabhiḥ pādayoḥ hareḥ kṛṣṇa sandarśana āhlāda dhvasta saṃrodhana klamāḥ praśaśaṃsuḥ hṛṣīkeśam gīrbhiḥ prāñjalayaḥ nṛpāḥ rājānaḥ ūcuḥ prapannān pāhi naḥ kṛṣṇa nirviṇṇān ghora saṃsṛteḥ na enam nātha anusūyāmaḥ māgadham madhusūdana mṛga tṛṣṇām yathā bālāḥ manyante udakāśayam evam vaikārikīm māyām ayuktāḥ vastu cakṣate vayam purā śrī mada naṣṭa dṛṣṭayaḥ jigīṣayā asyāḥ itaretara spṛdhaḥ ghnantaḥ prajāḥ svāḥ ati nirghṛṇāḥ prabho mṛtyum puras tvā a vigaṇayya durmadāḥ te eva kṛṣṇa adya gabhīra raṃhasā durante vīryeṇa vicālitāḥ śriyaḥ kālena tanvā bhavataḥ anukampayā vinaṣṭa darpāḥ caraṇau smarāma te atho na rājyam mṛga tṛṣṇi rūpitam dehena śaśvat patatā rujām bhuvā tam naḥ samādiśa upāyam yena te caraṇa abjayoḥ kṛṣṇāya vāsudevāya haraye paramātmane praṇata kleśa nāśāya govindāya namaḥ namaḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca tān āha karuṇaḥ tāta śaraṇyaḥ ślakṣṇayā girā śrī bhagavān uvāca su dṛḍhā jāyate bhaktiḥ bāḍham āśaṃsitam tathā diṣṭyā vyavasitam bhūpāḥ bhavantaḥ ṛta bhāṣiṇaḥ śrīi aiśvarya mada unnāham paśya unmādakam nṛṇām śrī madāt bhraṃśitāḥ sthānāt deva daitya nareśvarāḥ mām yajantaḥ adhvaraiḥ yuktāḥ prajāḥ dharmeṇa rakṣyatha udāsīnāḥ ca deha ādau ātma ārāmāḥ dhṛta vratāḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca iti ādiśya nṛpān kṛṣṇaḥ bhagavant bhuvaneśvaraḥ teṣām nyayuṅkta puruṣān striyaḥ majjana karmaṇi saparyām kārayām āsa sahadevena bhārata bhojayitvā vara annena su snātān samalaṅkṛtān bhogaiḥ ca vividhaiḥ yuktān tāmbūla ādyaiḥ nṛpa ucitaiḥ te pūjitāḥ mukundena rājānaḥ mṛṣṭa kuṇḍalāḥ virejuḥ mocitāḥ kleśāt prāvṛṣ ante yathā grahāḥ rathān sat aśvān āropya maṇi kāñcana bhūṣitān prīṇayya su nṛtaiḥ vākyaiḥ sva deśān pratyayāpayat te evam mocitāḥ kṛcchrāt kṛṣṇena su mahātmanā jagaduḥ prakṛtibhyaḥ te mahā puruṣa ceṣṭitam yathā anvaśāsat bhagavān tathā cakruḥ atandritāḥ jarāsandham ghātayitvā bhīmasenena keśavaḥ pārthābhyām saṃyutaḥ prāyāt sahadevena pūjitaḥ gatvā te khāṇḍavaprastham śaṅkhān dadhmuḥ jita arayaḥ harṣayantaḥ sva suhṛdaḥ durhṛdām ca asukha āvahāḥ menire māgadham śāntam rājā ca āpta manorathaḥ abhivandya atha rājānam bhīma arjuna janārdanāḥ sarvam āśrāvayām cakruḥ ātmanā yat anuṣṭhitam ānanda aśru kalām muñcan premṇā na uvāca kiṃcana śrī śukaḥ uvāca evam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā jarāsandha vadham vibhoḥ kṛṣṇasya ca anubhāvam tam śrutvā prītaḥ tam abravīt śrī yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca vahanti durlabham śirasā eva anuśāsanam sa bhavān aravinda akṣaḥ dīnānām īśa māninām tvam tava iti ca nānā dhīḥ paśūnām iva vaikṛtī śrī śukaḥ uvāca iti uktvā yajñiye kāle vavre yuktān saḥ ṛtvijaḥ kṛṣṇa anumoditaḥ pārthaḥ brāhmaṇān brahma vādinaḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ cyavanaḥ kaṇvaḥ maitreyaḥ kavaṣaḥ tritaḥ viśvāmitraḥ vāmadevaḥ sumatiḥ jaiminiḥ kratuḥ atharvā kaśyapaḥ dhaumyaḥ rāmaḥ bhārgavaḥ āsuriḥ vītihotraḥ madhucchandāḥ vīrasenaḥ akṛtavraṇaḥ upahūtāḥ tathā ca anye droṇa bhīṣma kṛpa ādayaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ saha sutaḥ viduraḥ ca mahā matiḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ yajña didṛkṣavaḥ tatra iyuḥ sarva rājānaḥ rājñām prakṛtayaḥ nṛpa tatas te deva yajanam brāhmaṇāḥ svarṇa lāṅgalaiḥ kṛṣṭvā tatra yathāmnāyam nṛpam haimāḥ kila upakaraṇāḥ varuṇasya yathā purā indra ādayaḥ loka pālāḥ viriñci bhava saṃyutāḥ sa gaṇāḥ siddha gandharvāḥ vidyādhara mahā uragāḥ munayaḥ yakṣa rakṣāṃsi khaga kinnara cāraṇāḥ rājānaḥ ca samāhūtāḥ rāja patnyaḥ ca sarvaśas rājasūyam samīyuḥ sma rājñaḥ pāṇḍu sutasya vai menire kṛṣṇa bhaktasya sūpapannam avismitāḥ ayājayat mahā rājam yājakāḥ deva varcasaḥ sūtye ahani avanī pālaḥ yājakān sadasas patīn apūjayat mahā bhāgān yathā vat su samāhitaḥ sadasya agrya arhaṇa arham vai vimṛśantaḥ sabhā sadaḥ arhati hi acyutaḥ śraiṣṭhyam bhagavān sātvatām patiḥ eṣa vai devatāḥ sarvāḥ deśa kāla dhana ādayaḥ yad ātmakam idam viśvam kratavaḥ ca yad ātmakāḥ agniḥ āhutayaḥ mantrāḥ sāṅkhyam yogaḥ ca yat paraḥ ātmanā ātma āśrayaḥ sabhyāḥ sṛjati avati hanti ajaḥ vividhāni iha karmāṇi janayan yad avekṣayā īhate yat ayam sarvaḥ śreyaḥ dharma ādi lakṣaṇam tasmāt kṛṣṇāya mahate dīyatām parama arhaṇam evam ced sarva bhūtānām ātmanaḥ ca arhaṇam bhavet sarva bhūta ātma bhūtāya kṛṣṇāya ananya darśine deyam śāntāya pūrṇāya dattasya ānantyam icchatā iti uktvā sahadevaḥ abhūt tūṣṇīm kṛṣṇa anubhāva vid tat śrutvā tuṣṭuvuḥ sarve sādhu sādhu iti sattamāḥ śrutvā dvija īritam rājā jñātvā hārdam sabhā sadām samarhayat dhṛṣīkeśam prītaḥ praṇaya vihvalaḥ tad pādau avanijya apaḥ śirasā loka pāvanīḥ sa bhāryaḥ sa anuja amātyaḥ sa kuṭumbaḥ vahan mudā vāsobhiḥ pīta kauṣeyaiḥ bhūṣaṇaiḥ ca mahā dhanaiḥ arhayitvā aśru pūrṇa akṣaḥ na aśakat samavekṣitum ittham sabhājitam vīkṣya sarve prāñjalayaḥ janāḥ namaḥ jaya iti nemuḥ tam nipetuḥ puṣpa vṛṣṭayaḥ ittham niśamya damaghoṣa sutaḥ sva pīṭhāt utthāya kṛṣṇa guṇa varṇana jāta manyuḥ utkṣipya bāhum idam āha sadasi amarṣī saṃśrāvayan bhagavate paruṣāṇi abhītaḥ īśaḥ duratyayaḥ kālaḥ iti satyavatī srutiḥ yūyam pātra vidām śreṣṭhāḥ mā mandhvam bāla bhāṣītam parama ṛṣīn brahma niṣṭhān loka pālaiḥ ca pūjitān sadas patīn atikramya gopālaḥ kula pāṃsanaḥ yathā kākaḥ puroḍāśam saparyām katham arhati varṇa āśrama kula apetaḥ sarva dharma bahiṣ kṛtaḥ yayātinā eṣām hi kulam śaptam sadbhiḥ bahis kṛtam vṛthak pāna ratam śaśvat saparyām katham arhati samudram durgam āśritya bādhante dasyavaḥ prajāḥ evam ādīni abhadrāṇi babhāṣe naṣṭa maṅgalaḥ na uvāca kiñcid bhagavān yathā siṃhaḥ śivā rutam bhagavat nindanam śrutvā duḥsaham tat sabhā sadaḥ karṇau pidhāya nirjagmuḥ śapantaḥ cedi pam ruṣā nindām bhagavataḥ śṛṇvan tad parasya janasya vā tatas na apaiti yaḥ saḥ api yāti adhas sukṛtāt cyutaḥ tatas pāṇḍu sutāḥ
