kruddhāḥ matsya kaikaya sṛñjayāḥ udāyudhāḥ samuttasthuḥ śiśupāla jighāṃsavaḥ bhartsayan kṛṣṇa pakṣīyān rājñaḥ sadasi bhārata tāvat utthāya bhagavān svān nivārya svayam ruṣā śiraḥ kṣura anta cakreṇa jahāra patataḥ ripoḥ śabdaḥ kolāhalaḥ atha āsīt śiśupāle hate mahān tasya anuyāyinaḥ bhūpāḥ dudruvuḥ jīvita eṣiṇaḥ paśyatām sarva bhūtānām ulkā iva bhuvi khāt cyutā dhyāyan tad maya tām yātaḥ bhāvaḥ hi bhava kāraṇam ṛtvigbhyaḥ sa sadasyebhyaḥ dakṣinām vipulām adāt sādhayitvā kratuḥ rājñaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ yoga īśvara īśvaraḥ uvāsa katicid māsān suhṛdbhiḥ abhiyācitaḥ tatas anujñāpya rājānam an icchantam api īśvaraḥ yayau sa bhāryaḥ sa amātyaḥ sva puram devakī sutaḥ varṇitam tat upākhyānam mayā te bahu vistaram vaikuṇṭha vāsinoḥ janma vipra śāpāt punar punar rājasūya āvabhṛthyena snātaḥ rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ brahma kṣatra sabhā madhye śuśubhe sura rāj iva rājñā sabhājitāḥ sarve sura mānava khecarāḥ kṛṣṇam kratum ca śaṃsantaḥ sva dhāmāni yayuḥ mudā yaḥ na sehe śrīyam sphītām dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍu sutasya tām rāja mokṣam vitānam ca sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate śrī rājā uvāca ajāta śatroḥ tam dṛṣṭvā rājasūya mahā udayam duryodhanam varjayitvā rājānaḥ sa ṛṣayaḥ surāḥ iti śrutam naḥ bhagavan tatra kāraṇam ucyatām śrī bādarāyaṇiḥ uvāca pitāmahasya te yajñe rājasūye mahātmanaḥ bāndhavāḥ paricaryāyām tasya āsan prema bandhanāḥ bhīmaḥ mahānasa adhyakṣaḥ dhanādhyakṣaḥ suyodhanaḥ guru śuśrūṣaṇe jiṣṇuḥ kṛṣṇaḥ pāda avanejane pariveṣaṇe drupada jā karṇaḥ dāne mahā manāḥ yuyudhānaḥ vikarṇaḥ ca hārdikyaḥ vidura ādayaḥ vāhlīka putrāḥ bhūri ādyāḥ ye ca santardana ādayaḥ nirūpitāḥ mahā yajñe nānā karmasu te tadā pravartante sma rāja indra rājñaḥ priya cikīrṣavaḥ su iṣṭeṣu sūnṛta samarhaṇa dakṣiṇābhiḥ caidye ca sātvata pateḥ caraṇam praviṣṭe mṛdaṅga śaṅkha paṇava dhundhurī ānaka gomukhāḥ vāditrāṇi vicitrāṇi neduḥ ā avabhṛtha utsave nārtakyaḥ nanṛtuḥ hṛṣṭāḥ gāyakāḥ yūthaśas jaguḥ vīṇā veṇu tala unnādaḥ teṣām sa divam aspṛśat su alaṅkṛtaiḥ bhaṭaiḥ bhūpāḥ niryayuḥ rukma mālinaḥ yadu sṛñjaya kāmboja kuru kekaya kośalāḥ sadasyartvij dvija śreṣṭhāḥ brahma ghoṣeṇa bhūyasā devarṣi pitṛ gandharvāḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ puṣpa varṣiṇaḥ su alaṇkṛtāḥ narāḥ nāryaḥ gandha sraj bhūṣaṇa ambaraiḥ tāḥ mātuleya sakhibhiḥ pariṣicyamānāḥ sa vrīḍa hāsa vikasat vadanāḥ virejuḥ tāḥ devarān uta sakhīn siṣicuḥ dṛtībhiḥ klinna ambarāḥ vivṛta gātra kuca ūru madhyāḥ kṣobham mala dhiyām ruciraiḥ vihāraiḥ sa samrāj ratham āruḍhaḥ sat aśvam rukma mālinam patnī samyāja āvabhṛthyaiḥ caritvā te tam ṛtvijaḥ ācāntam cakruḥ gaṅgāyām saha kṛṣṇayā mumucuḥ puṣpa varṣāṇi devarṣi pitṛ mānavāḥ sasnuḥ tatra tatas sarve varṇa āśrama yutāḥ narāḥ atha rājā ahate kṣaume paridhāya su alaṅkṛtaḥ ṛtvij sadasya vipra ādīn ānarca ābharaṇa ambaraiḥ bandhūn jñātīn nṛpāt mitra suhṛdaḥ anyān ca sarvaśas abhīkṣnam pūjayām āsa nārāyaṇa paraḥ nṛpaḥ sarve janāḥ sura rucaḥ maṇi kuṇḍala sraj uṣṇīṣa kañcuka dukūla mahā arghya hārāḥ nāryaḥ ca kuṇḍala yuga alaka vṛnda juṣṭa atha ṛtvijaḥ mahā śīlāḥ sadasyāḥ brahma vādinaḥ brahma kṣatriya viś śudra rājānaḥ ye samāgatāḥ devarṣi pitṛ bhūtāni loka pālāḥ saha anugāḥ pūjitāḥ tam anujñāpya sva dhāmāni yayuḥ nṛpa na eva atṛpyan praśaṃsantaḥ piban martyaḥ amṛtam yathā tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā suhṛd sambandhi bāndhavān premṇā nivārayām āsa kṛṣṇam ca tyāga kātaraḥ bhagavān api tatra aṅga nyāvātsīt tad priyaṃkaraḥ prasthāpya yadu vīrān ca sāmba ādīn ca kuśasthalīm su dustaram samuttīrya kṛṣṇena āsīt gata jvaraḥ atapyat rājasūyasya mahi tvam ca acyuta ātmanaḥ nānā vibhānti kila viśva sṛjā upakḷptāḥ yasyām viṣakta hṛdayaḥ kuru rāj atapyat śroṇī bhareṇa śanakais kvaṇat aṅghri śobham madhye su cāru kuca kuṅkuma śoṇa hāram śrīmat mukham pracala kuṇḍala kuntala āḍhyam sabhāyām maya kḷptāyām kvāpi dharma sutaḥ adhirāj vṛtaḥ anugaiḥ bandhubhiḥ ca kṛṣṇena api sva cakṣuṣā āsīnaḥ kāñcane sākṣāt āsane maghavān iva pārameṣṭhya śrīyā juṣṭaḥ stūyamānaḥ ca vandibhiḥ tatra duryodhanaḥ mānī parītaḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ nṛpa kirīṭa mālī nyaviśat asi hastaḥ kṣipan ruṣā jahāsa bhīmaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā striyaḥ pare nivāryamāṇāḥ api aṅga rājñā kṛṣṇa anumoditāḥ sa vrīḍitaḥ avak vadanaḥ ruṣā jvalan niṣkramya tūṣṇīm prayayau gajāhvayam hā hā iti śabdaḥ su mahān abhūt satām ajāta śatruḥ vimanāḥ iva abhavat babhūva tūṣṇīm bhagavān bhuvaḥ bharam samujjihīrṣuḥ bhramati sma yad dṛśā etat te abhihitam rājan yat pṛṣṭaḥ aham iha tvayā śrī śukaḥ uvāca atha anyat api kṛṣṇasya śṛṇu karma adbhutam nṛpa krīḍā nara śarīrasya yathā saubha patiḥ hataḥ śiśupāla sakhaḥ śālvaḥ rukmiṇī udvāhe āgataḥ śālvaḥ pratijñām akarot śṛṇvatām sarva bhūbhujām a yādavām kṣmām kariṣye pauruṣam mama paśyata iti mūḍhaḥ pratijñāya devam paśu patim prabhum ārādhayām āsa nṛpaḥ pāṃśu muṣṭim sakṛt grasan saṃvatsara ante bhagavān āśu toṣaḥ umāpatiḥ vareṇa chandayām āsa śālvam śaraṇam āgatam deva asura manuṣyāṇām gandharva uraga rakṣasām abhedyam kāma gam vavre sa yānam vṛṣṇi bhīṣaṇam tathā iti giriśa ādiṣṭaḥ mayaḥ para puraṃjayaḥ puram nirmāya śālvāya prādāt saubham ayaḥ mayam sa labdhvā kāma gam yānam tamaḥ dhāma durāsadam yayaḥ dvāravatīm śālvaḥ vairam vṛṣṇi kṛtam smaran purīm babhañja upavanān udyānāni ca sarvaśas sa gopurāṇi dvārāṇi prāsāda aṭṭāla tolikāḥ vihārān sa vimāna agryān nipetuḥ śastra vṛṣṭayaḥ śilā drumāḥ ca aśanayaḥ sarpāḥ āsāra śarkarāḥ pracaṇḍaḥ cakra vātaḥ abhūt rajasā ācchāditāḥ diśaḥ iti ardyamānā saubhena kṛṣṇasya nagarī bhṛśam na abhyapadyata śam rājan tri pureṇa yathā mahī pradyumnaḥ bhagavān vīkṣya bādhyamānāḥ nijāḥ prajāḥ mā bhaiṣṭa iti abhyadhāt vīraḥ ratha ārūḍhaḥ mahā yaśāḥ sātyakiḥ cārudeṣṇaḥ ca sāmbaḥ akrūraḥ sahānujaḥ hārdikyaḥ bhānuvindaḥ ca gadaḥ ca śuka sāraṇau apare ca mahā iṣu āsāḥ ratha yūthapa yūthapāḥ niryayuḥ daṃśitāḥ guptāḥ ratha ibha aśva padātibhiḥ tatas pravavṛte yuddham śālvānām yadubhiḥ saha yathā asurāṇām vibudhaiḥ tumulam loma harṣaṇam tāḥ ca saubha pateḥ māyāḥ divya astraiḥ rukmiṇī sutaḥ kṣaṇena nāśayām āsa naiśam tamaḥ iva uṣṇaguḥ vivyādha pañca viṃśatyā svarṇa puṅkhaiḥ ayaḥ mukhaiḥ śālvasya dhvajinī pālam śaraiḥ sannata parvabhiḥ śatena atāḍayat śālvam ekaikena asya sainikān dṛṣṭvā tam pūjayām āsuḥ sarve sva para sainikāḥ bahu rūpa eka rūpam tat dṛśyate na ca dṛśyate māyā mayam maya kṛtam durvibhāvyam paraiḥ abhūt śālvaḥ tatas tatas amuñcan śarān sātvata yūthapāḥ śaraiḥ agni arka saṃsparśaiḥ āśī viṣa durāsadaiḥ pīḍyamāna pura anīkaḥ śālvaḥ amuhyat para īritaiḥ śālva anīkapa śastra oghaiḥ vṛṣṇi vīrāḥ bhṛśa arditāḥ na tatyajuḥ raṇam svam svam loka dvaya jigīṣavaḥ śālva amātyaḥ dyumān nāma pradyumnam prak prapīḍitaḥ āsādya gadayā maurvyā vyāhatya vyanadat balī pradyumnam gadayā sīrṇa vakṣaḥ sthalam ariṃ damam apovāha raṇāt sūtaḥ dharma vid dāruka ātmajaḥ labdha samjñaḥ muhūrtena kārṣṇiḥ sārathim abravīt aho asādhu idam sūta yat raṇāt mama apasarpaṇam na yadūnām kule jātaḥ śrūyate raṇa vicyutaḥ vinā mat klība cittena sūtena prāpta kilbiṣāt yuddhāt samyak apakrāntaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ tatra ātmanaḥ kṣamam klaibyam katham katham vīra tava anyaiḥ kathyatām mṛdhe sārathiḥ uvāca dharmam vijānatā āyuṣman kṛtam etat mayā vibho sūtaḥ kṛcchra gatam rakṣet rathinam sārathim rathī etat viditvā tu bhavān mayā apovāhitaḥ raṇāt upasṛṣṭaḥ pareṇa iti mūrcchitaḥ gadayā hataḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca saḥ upaspṛśya salilam daṃśitaḥ dhṛta kārmukaḥ naya mām dyumataḥ pārśvam vīrasya iti āha sārathim dvābhyam dhanuḥ ca ketum ca śareṇa anyena vai śiraḥ evam yadūnām śālvānām nighnatām itaretaram indraprastham gataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ āhūtaḥ dharma sūnunā rājasūye atha nivṛtte śiśupāle ca saṃsthite kuru vṛddhān anujñāpya munīn ca sa sutām pṛthām nimittāni ati ghorāṇi paśyan dvāravatīm yayau āha ca aham iha āyātaḥ ārya miśra abhisaṅgataḥ rājanyāḥ caidya pakṣīyāḥ nūnam hanyuḥ purīm mama vīkṣya tat kadanam svānām nirūpya pura rakṣaṇam saubham ca śālva rājam ca dārukam prāha keśavaḥ ratham prāpaya me sūta śālvasya antikam āśu vai iti uktaḥ codayām āsa ratham āsthāya dārukaḥ viśantam dadṛśuḥ sarve svāḥ pare ca aruṇānujam śālvaḥ ca kṛṣṇam ālokya hata prāya bala īśvaraḥ prāharat kṛṣṇa sūtaye śaktim bhīma ravām mṛdhe tām āpatantīm nabhasi mahā ulkām iva raṃhasā bhāsayantīm diśaḥ śauriḥ sāyakaiḥ śatadhā ācchinat tam ca ṣoḍaśabhiḥ viddhvā bānaiḥ saubham ca khe bhramat śālvaḥ śaureḥ tu dos savyam sa śārṅgam śārṅga dhanvanaḥ hāhā kāraḥ mahān āsīt bhūtānām tatra paśyatām yat tvayā mūḍha naḥ sakhyuḥ bhrātuḥ bhāryā hṛtā īkṣatām pramattaḥ sa sabhā madhye tvayā vyāpāditaḥ sakhā tam tvā adya niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ aparājita māninam nayāmi apunar āvṛttim yadi tiṣṭheḥ mama agratas śrī bhagavān uvāca paurusam darśayanti sma śūrāḥ na bahu bhāṣiṇaḥ iti uktvā bhagavān śālvam gadayā bhīma vegayā gadāyām sannivṛttāyām śālvaḥ tu antaradhīyata tatas muhūrte āgatya puruṣaḥ śirasā acyutam kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa mahā bāho pitā te pitṛ vatsala baddhvā apanītaḥ śālvena saunikena yathā paśuḥ niśamya vipriyam kṛṣṇaḥ mānusīm prakṛtim gataḥ vimanaskaḥ ghṛṇī snehāt babhāṣe prākṛtaḥ yathā katham rāmam asambhrāntam jitvā ajeyam sura asuraiḥ śālvena alpīyasā nītaḥ pitā me balavān vidhiḥ vasudevam iva ānīya kṛṣṇam ca idam uvāca saḥ vadhiṣye vīkṣataḥ te amum īśaḥ ced pāhi bāliśa evam nirbhartsya māyāvī khaḍgena ānakadundubheḥ utkṛtya śiraḥ ādāya kha stham saubham samāviśat tatas muhūrtam prakṛtau upaplutaḥ sva bodhaḥ āste sva jana anuṣaṅgāt mahā anubhāvaḥ tat abudhyat āsurīm māyām sa śālva prasṛtām mayā uditām svāpnam yathā ca ambara cāriṇam ripum saubha stham ālokya nihantum udyataḥ evam vadanti rājarṣe ṛṣayaḥ ke ca na anvitāḥ kva śoka mohau snehaḥ vā bhayam vā ye ajña sambhavāḥ kva ca akhaṇḍita vijñāna jñāna aiśvaryaḥ tu akhaṇḍitaḥ tam śastra pūgaiḥ praharantam ojasā śālvam śaraiḥ śauriḥ amogha vikramaḥ tat kṛṣṇa hasta īritayā vicūrṇitam papāta toye gadayā sahasradhā jahāra tena eva śiraḥ sa kuṇḍalam kirīṭa yuktam puru māyinaḥ hariḥ vajreṇa vṛtrasya yathā purandaraḥ babhūva hāhā iti vacaḥ tadā nṛṇām śrī śukaḥ uvāca śiśupālasya śālvasya pauṇḍrakasya api durmatiḥ para loka gatānām ca kurvan pārokṣya sauhṛdam ekaḥ padātiḥ saṅkruddhaḥ gadā pāṇiḥ prakampayan padbhyām imām mahā rāja mahā sattvaḥ vyadṛśyata tam tathā āyāntam ālokya gadām ādāya sa tvaraḥ avaplutya rathāt kṛṣṇaḥ sindhum velā iva pratyadhāt gadām udyamya kārūṣaḥ mukundam prāha durmadaḥ diṣṭyā diṣṭyā bhavān adya mama dṛṣṭi patham gataḥ tvam mātuleyaḥ naḥ kṛṣṇa mitra druh mām jighāṃsasi tarhi ānṛṇyam upaimi ajña mitrāṇām mitra vatsalaḥ bandhu rūpam arim hatvā vyādhim deha caram yathā evam rūkṣaiḥ tudan vākyaiḥ kṛṣṇam totraiḥ iva dvipam kṛṣṇaḥ api tam ahan gurvyā kaumodakyā stanāntare prasārya keśa bāhu aṅghrīn dharaṇyām nyapatat vyasuḥ tatas sūkṣmataram jyotiḥ kṛṣṇam āviśat adbhutam paśyatām sarva bhūtānām yathā caidya vadhe nṛpa vidūrathaḥ tu tad bhrātā bhrātṛ śoka pariplutaḥ āgacchat asi carmābhyām ucchvasan tad jighāṃsayā tasya ca āpatataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ cakreṇa kṣura neminā śiraḥ jahāra rāja indra sa kirīṭam sa kuṇḍalam evam saubham ca śālvam ca dantavakram sahānujam hatvā durviṣahān anyaiḥ īḍitaḥ sura mānavaiḥ apsarobhiḥ pitṛ gaṇaiḥ yakṣaiḥ kinnara cāraṇaiḥ vṛtaḥ ca vṛṣṇi pravaraiḥ viveśa alaṅkṛtām purīm evam yogeśvaraḥ kṛṣṇaḥ bhagavān jagat īśvaraḥ īyate paśu dṛṣṭīnām nirjitaḥ jayati iti saḥ śrutvā yuddha udyamam rāmaḥ kurūṇām saha pāṇḍavaiḥ snātvā prabhāse santarpya deva ṛṣi pitṛ mānavān sarasvatīm prati srotam yayau brāhmaṇa saṃvṛtaḥ pṛthūdakam bindu saraḥ tritakūpam sudarśanam viśālam brahma tīrtham ca cakram prācīm sarasvatīm jagāma naimiṣam yatra ṛṣayaḥ satram āsate saḥ arcitaḥ sa parīvāraḥ kṛta āsana parigrahaḥ romaharṣaṇam āsīnam mahā ṛṣeḥ śiṣyam aikṣata a pratyutthāyinam sūtam a kṛta prahvaṇa añjalim adhyāsīnam ca tān viprān cukopa udvīkṣya mādhavaḥ yasmāt asau imān viprān adhyāste pratiloma jaḥ ṛṣeḥ bhagavataḥ bhūtvā śiṣyaḥ adhītya bahūni ca sa itihāsa purāṇāni dharma śāstrāṇi sarvaśas adāntasya avinītasya vṛthak paṇḍita māninaḥ na guṇāya bhavanti sma naṭasya iva ajita ātmanaḥ bhāvi tvāt tam kuśa agreṇa kara sthena ahanat prabhuḥ hāhā iti vādinaḥ sarve munayaḥ khinna mānasāḥ ūcuḥ saṅkarṣaṇam devam adharmaḥ te kṛtaḥ prabho āyuḥ ca ātma aklamam tāvat yāvat satram samāpyate yadi etat brahma hatyāyāḥ pāvanam loka pāvana śrī bhagavān uvāca cariṣye vadha nirveśam loka anugraha kāmyayā āśāsitam yat tat brūte sādhaye yoga māyayā ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ yathā bhavet vacaḥ satyam tathā rāma vidhīyatām śrī bhagavān uvāca kim vaḥ kāmaḥ muni śreṣṭhāḥ brūta aham karavāṇi atha a jānataḥ tu apacitim yathā me cintyatām budhāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ tam pāpam jahi dāśārha tat naḥ śuśrūṣaṇam param pūya śoṇita vid mūtra surā māṃsa abhivarṣiṇam tatas ca bhāratam varṣam parītya su samāhitaḥ caritvā dvādaśa māsān tīrtha snāyī viśudhyasi śrī śukaḥ uvāca tatas parvaṇi upāvṛtte pracaṇḍaḥ pāṃśu varṣaṇaḥ bhīmaḥ vāyuḥ abhūt rājan pūya gandhaḥ tu sarvaśas abhavat yajña śālāyām saḥ anvadṛśyata śūla dhṛk tam vilokya bṛhat kāyam bhinnāñjana caya upamam tapta tāmra śikhā śmaśrum daṃṣṭra ugra bhru kuṭī mukham sasmāra mūṣalam rāmaḥ para sainya vidāraṇam tam ākṛṣya hala agreṇa balvalam gagane caram muñcan ārta svaram śailaḥ yathā vajra hataḥ aruṇaḥ saṃstutya munayaḥ rāmam prayujya avitatha āśiṣaḥ abhyaṣiñcat mahā bhāgā vṛtra ghnam vibudhāḥ yathā vaijayantīm daduḥ mālām śrī dhāma amlāna paṅkajām rāmāya vāsasī divye divyāni ābharaṇāni ca atha taiḥ abhyanujñātaḥ kauśikīm etya brāhmaṇaiḥ snātvā sarovaram agāt yatas sarayūḥ āsravat snātvā santarpya deva ādīn jagāma pulaha āśramam gomatīm gaṇḍakīm snātvā vipāśām śoṇaḥ āplutaḥ gayām gatvā pitṝn iṣṭvā gaṅgā sāgara saṅgame upaspṛśya mahendra adrau rāmam dṛṣṭvā abhivādya ca sapta godāvarīm veṇām pampām bhīmarathām tatas skandam dṛṣṭvā yayau rāmaḥ śrī śailam giriśa ālayam draviḍeṣu mahā puṇyam dṛṣṭvā adrim veṅkaṭam prabhuḥ kāma koṣṇīm purīm kāñcīm kāverīm ca sarit varām śrī ranga ākhyam mahā puṇyam yatra sannihitaḥ hariḥ ṛṣabhādrim hareḥ kṣetram dakṣiṇām mathurām tathā sāmudram setum agamat mahā pātaka nāśanam tatra ayutam adāt dhenūḥ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ halāyudhaḥ kṛtamālām tāmraparṇīm malayam ca kula acalam tatra agastyam samāsīnam namaskṛtya abhivādya ca yojitaḥ tena ca anujñātaḥ gataḥ arṇavam dakṣiṇam tatra kanyā ākhyām durgām devīm dadarśa saḥ tatas phālgunam āsādya pañcāpsarasam uttamam viṣṇuḥ sannihitaḥ yatra snātvā asparśat go ayutam gokarṇa ākhyam śiva kṣetram sāṃnidhyam yatra dhūrjaṭeḥ āryām dvaipāyanīm dṛṣṭvā śūrpārakam agāt balaḥ tāpīm payoṣṇīm nirvindhyām upaspṛśya atha daṇḍakam praviśya revām agamat yatra māhiṣmatī purī manu tīrtham upaspṛśya prabhāsam punar āgamat śrutvā dvijaiḥ kathyamānam kuru pāṇḍava saṃyuge sarva rājanya nidhanam bhāram mene hṛtam bhuvaḥ vārayiṣyan vinaśanam jagāma yadu nandanaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tu tam dṛṣṭvā yamau kṛṣṇa arjunau api abhivādya abhavan tuṣṇīm kim vivakṣuḥ iha āgataḥ gadā pāṇī ubhau dṛṣṭvā saṃrabdhau vijaya eṣiṇau maṇḍalāni vicitrāṇi carantau idam abravīt ekam prāṇa adhikam manye uta ekam śikṣayā adhikam anusmarantau anyonyam duruktam duṣkṛtāni ca diṣṭam tat anumanvānaḥ rāmaḥ dvāravatīm yayau ugrasena ādibhiḥ prītaiḥ jñātibhiḥ samupāgataḥ tam punar naimiṣam prāptam ṛṣayaḥ ayājayan mudā tebhyaḥ viśuddham vijñānam bhagavān vyatarat vibhuḥ yena eva ātmani adaḥ viśvam ātmānam viśva gam viduḥ sva patyā avabhṛtha snātaḥ jñāti bandhu suhṛd vṛtaḥ reje sva jyotsnayā iva induḥ su vāsāḥ suṣṭhu alaṅkṛtaḥ īdṛgvidhāni asaṅkhyāni balasya bala śālinaḥ sāyam prātar anantasya viṣṇoḥ sa dayitaḥ bhavet śrī rājā uvāca kaḥ nu śrutvā asakṛt brahman uttamaḥśloka sat kathāḥ virameta viśeṣa jñaḥ viṣaṇṇaḥ kāma mārgaṇaiḥ sā vāc yayā tasya guṇān gṛṇīte karau ca tad karma karau manaḥ ca smaret vasantam sthira jaṅgameṣu śṛṇoti tad puṇya kathāḥ sa karṇaḥ aṅgāni viṣṇoḥ atha tad janānām pāda udakam yāni bhajanti nityam sūtaḥ uvāca viṣṇu rātena sampṛṣṭaḥ bhagavān bādarāyaṇiḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca kṛṣṇasya āsīt sakhā kaścid brāhmaṇaḥ brahma vittamaḥ viraktaḥ indriya artheṣu praśānta ātmā jita indriyaḥ yadṛcchayā upapannena vartamānaḥ gṛhāśramī tasya bhāryā ku cailasya kṣudh kṣāmā ca tathāvidhā pati vratā patim prāha mlāyatā vadanena sā daridram sīdamānā vai vepamānā abhigamya ca nanu brahman bhagavataḥ sakhā sākṣāt śriyaḥ patiḥ brahmaṇyaḥ ca śaraṇyaḥ ca bhagavān sātvata ṛṣabhaḥ tam upaihi mahā bhāga sādhūnām ca parāyaṇam dāsyati draviṇam bhūri sīdate te kuṭumbine āste adhunā dvāravatyām bhoja vṛṣṇi andhaka īśvaraḥ kim nu artha kāmān bhajataḥ na ati abhīṣṭān jagad-guruḥ saḥ evam bhāryayā vipraḥ bahuśas prārthitaḥ muhur api asti upāyanam kiñcid gṛhe kalyāṇi dīyatām yācitvā caturaḥ muṣṭīn viprān pṛthuka taṇḍulān caila khaṇḍena tān baddhvā bhartre prādāt upāyanam sa tān ādāya vipra agryaḥ prayayau dvārakām kila kṛṣṇa sandarśanam mahyam katham syāt iti cintayan trīṇi gulmāni atīyāya tisraḥ kakṣāḥ ca sa dvijaḥ vipraḥ agamyā andhaka vṛṣṇīnām gṛheṣu acyuta dharmiṇām gṛham dvi aṣṭa sahasrāṇām mahiṣīṇām hareḥ dvijaḥ viveśa ekatamam śrīmat brahma ānandam gataḥ yathā tam vilokya acyutaḥ dūrāt priyā paryaṅkam āsthitaḥ sakhyuḥ priyasya viprarṣeḥ aṅga saṅga ati nirvṛtaḥ prītaḥ vyamuñcat ap bindūn netrābhyām puṣkarekṣaṇaḥ upahṛtya avanijya asya pādau pāda avanejanīḥ agrahīt śirasā rājan bhagavān loka pāvanaḥ arcitvā āvedya tāmbūlam gām ca svāgatam abravīt antaḥpura janaḥ dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇena amala kīrtinā vismitaḥ abhūt ati prītyā avadhūtam sabhājitam kim anena kṛtam puṇyam avadhūtena bhikṣuṇā yaḥ asau tri loka guruṇā śrī nivāsena sambhṛtaḥ paryaṅka sthām śriyam hitvā pariṣvaktaḥ agra jaḥ yathā cakratuḥ gāthāḥ pūrvāḥ guru kule satoḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca samāvṛttena dharma jña bhāryā ūḍhā sadṛśī na vā prāyas gṛheṣu te cittam akāma vihitam tathā tyajantaḥ prakṛtīḥ daivīḥ yathā aham loka saṅgraham dvijaḥ vijñāya vijñeyam tamasaḥ pāram aśnute sa vai sat karmaṇām sākṣāt dvijāteḥ iha sambhavaḥ ādyaḥ aṅga yatra āśramiṇām yathā aham jñāna daḥ guruḥ ye mayā guruṇā vācā taranti añjas bhava arṇavam na aham ijyā prajātibhyām tapasā upaśamena vā tuṣyeyam sarva bhūta ātmā guru śuśrūṣayā yathā praviṣṭānām mahā araṇyam apartau su mahat dvija vāta varṣam abhūt tīvram niṣṭhurāḥ stanayitnavaḥ sūryaḥ ca astam gataḥ tāvat tamasā ca āvṛtāḥ diśaḥ nimnam kūlam jala mayam na prājñāyata kiñcana diśaḥ a vidantaḥ atha parasparam vane gṛhīta hastāḥ paribabhrima āturāḥ anveṣamāṇaḥ naḥ śiṣyān ācāryaḥ apaśyat āturān ātmā vai prāṇinām preṣṭhaḥ tam an ādṛtya mad pare yat vai viśuddha bhāvena sarva artha ātma arpaṇam gurau tuṣṭaḥ aham bho dvija śreṣṭhāḥ satyāḥ santu manorathāḥ itthaṃvidhāni anekāni vasatām guru veśmani guroḥ anugraheṇa eva pumān pūrṇaḥ praśāntaye śrī brāhmaṇaḥ uvāca bhavatā satya kāmena yeṣām vāsaḥ guroḥ abhūt śreyasām tasya guruṣu vāsaḥ atyanta viḍambanam śrī śukaḥ uvāca brahmaṇyaḥ brāhmaṇam kṛṣṇaḥ bhagavān prahasan priyam premṇā nirīkṣaṇena eva prekṣan khalu satām gatiḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca kim upāyanam ānītam brahman me bhavatā gṛhāt aṇu api upāhṛtam bhaktaiḥ premṇā bhurī eva me bhavet tat aham bhakti upahṛtam aśnāmi prayata ātmanaḥ pṛthuka prasṛtim rājan na prāyacchat avāk mukhaḥ sarva bhūta ātma dṛś sākṣāt tasya āgamana kāraṇam na ayam śrī kāmaḥ mā ābhajat purā patnyāḥ pati vratāyāḥ tu sakhā priya cikīrṣayā svayam jahāra kim idam iti pṛthuka taṇḍulān tarpayanti aṅga mām viśvam ete pṛthuka taṇḍulāḥ iti muṣṭim sakṛt jagdhvā dvitīyām jagdhum ādade tāvat śrīḥ jagṛhe hastam tad parā parameṣṭhinaḥ etāvatā alam viśvātman sarva sampad samṛddhaye brāhmaṇaḥ tām tu rajanīm uṣitvā acyuta mandire bhuktvā pītvā sukham mene ātmānam svar gatam yathā sa ca a labdhvā dhanam kṛṣṇāt na tu yācitavan svayam sva gṛhān vrīḍitaḥ agacchat mahat darśana nirvṛtaḥ aho brahmaṇya devasya dṛṣṭā brahmaṇya tā mayā yat daridratamaḥ lakṣmīm āśliṣṭaḥ bibhratā urasi kva aham daridraḥ pāpīyān kva kṛṣṇaḥ śrī niketanaḥ nivāsitaḥ priyā juṣṭe paryaṅke bhrātaraḥ yathā mahiṣyā vījitaḥ śrāntaḥ bāla vyajana hastayā śuśrūṣayā paramayā pāda saṃvāhana ādibhiḥ svarga apavargayoḥ puṃsām rasāyām bhuvi sampadām sarvāsām api siddhīnām mūlam tad caraṇa arcanam iti kāruṇikaḥ nūnam dhanam me abhūri na adadāt sūrya anala indu saṅkāśaiḥ vimānaiḥ sarvatas vṛtam juṣṭam su alaṅkṛtaiḥ pumbhiḥ strībhiḥ ca hariṇa akṣibhiḥ evam mīmāṃsamānam tam narāḥ nāryaḥ amara prabhāḥ pratyagṛhṇan mahā bhāgam gīta vādyena bhūyasā niścakrāma gṛhāt tūrṇam rūpiṇī śrīḥ iva ālayāt pati vratā patim dṛṣṭvā prema utkaṇṭhā aśru locanā mīlita akṣā anamat buddhyā manasā pariṣasvaje patnīm vīkṣya visphurantīm devīm vaimānikīm iva dāsīnām niṣka kaṇṭhīnām madhye bhāntīm sa vismitaḥ prītaḥ svayam tayā yuktaḥ praviṣṭaḥ nija mandiram payaḥ phena nibhāḥ śayyā dāntā rukma paricchadāḥ paryaṅkāḥ hema daṇḍāni cāmara vyajanāni ca āsanāni ca haimāni mṛdu upastaraṇāni ca svaccha sphaṭika kuḍyeṣu mahā mārakateṣu ca ratna dīpān bhrājamānān lalanāḥ ratna saṃyutāḥ nanu abruvāṇaḥ diśate samakṣam yāciṣṇave bhūri api bhūri bhojaḥ parjanya vat tat svayam īkṣamāṇaḥ dāśārhakāṇām ṛṣabhaḥ sakhā me suhṛd kṛtam phalgu api bhūri kārī mayā upaṇītam pṛthuka eka muṣṭim mahā anubhāvena guṇa ālayena viṣajjataḥ tat puruṣa prasaṅgaḥ adīrgha bodhāya vicakṣaṇaḥ svayam paśyan nipātam dhaninām mada udbhavam viṣayān jāyayā tyakṣyan bubhuje na ati lampaṭaḥ evam sa vipraḥ bhagavat suhṛd tadā dṛṣṭvā sva bhṛtyaiḥ ajitam parājitam etat brahmaṇya devasya śrutvā brahmaṇya tām naraḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca atha ekadā dvāravatyām vasataḥ rāma kṛṣṇayoḥ sūrya uparāgaḥ su mahān āsīt kalpa kṣaye yathā tam jñātvā manujāḥ rājan purastāt eva sarvatas samanta pañcakam kṣetram yayuḥ śreyaḥ vidhitsayā niḥkṣatriyām mahīm kurvan rāmaḥ śastra bhṛtām varaḥ nṛpāṇām rudhira ogheṇa yatra cakre mahā hradān īje ca bhagavān rāmaḥ yatra a spṛṣṭaḥ api karmaṇā lokam saṅgrāhayan īśaḥ yathā anyaḥ agha apanuttaye mahatyām tīrtha yātrāyām tatra agan bhāratīḥ prajāḥ vṛṣṇayaḥ ca tathā akrūra vasudeva āhuka ādayaḥ yayuḥ bhārata tat kṣetram svam agham kṣapayiṣṇavaḥ gada pradyumna sāmba ādyāḥ sucandra śuka sāraṇaiḥ āste aniruddhaḥ rakṣāyām kṛtavarmā ca yūtha paḥ vyarocanta mahā tejāḥ pathini kāñcana mālinaḥ tatra snātvā mahā bhāgāḥ upoṣya su samāhitāḥ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ daduḥ dhenūḥ vāsaḥ sraj rukma mālinīḥ rāma hradeṣu vidhi vat punar āplutya vṛṣṇayaḥ svayam ca tad anujñātāḥ vṛṣṇayaḥ kṛṣṇa devatāḥ bhuktvā upaviviśuḥ kāmam snigdha chāyā aṅghripa aṅghriṣu tatra āgatān te dadṛśuḥ suhṛd sambandhinaḥ nṛpān matsya uśīnara kauśalya vidarbha kuru sṛñjayān kāmboja kaikayān madrān kuntīn ānarta keralān anyān ca eva ātma pakṣīyān parān ca śataśas nṛpa nanda ādīn suhṛdaḥ gopān gopīḥ ca utkaṇṭhitāḥ ciram āśliṣya gāḍham nayanaiḥ sravat jalāḥ hṛṣyat tvacaḥ ruddha giraḥ yayuḥ mudam striyaḥ ca saṃvīkṣya mithas ati sauhṛda smita amala apāṅga dṛśaḥ abhirebhire stanaiḥ stanān kuṅkuma paṅka rūṣitān nihatya dorbhiḥ praṇaya aśru locanāḥ tatas abhivādya te vṛddhān yaviṣṭhaiḥ abhivāditāḥ su āgatam kuśalam pṛṣṭvā cakruḥ kṛṣṇa kathāḥ mithas pṛthā bhrātṝn svasṝḥ vīkṣya tad putrān pitarau api bhrātṛ patnīḥ mukundam ca jahau saṅkathayā śucaḥ ārya bhrātar aham manye ātmānam a kṛta āśiṣam yat vai āpatsu mad vārttām na anusmaratha sattamāḥ suhṛdaḥ jñātayaḥ putrāḥ bhrātaraḥ pitarau api śrī vasudevaḥ uvāca amba mā asmān asūyethāḥ daiva krīḍanakān narān īśasya hi vaśe lokaḥ kurute kāryate atha vā kaṃsa pratāpitāḥ sarve vayam yātāḥ diśam diśam etarhi eva punar sthānam daivena āsāditāḥ svasaḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca āsan acyuta sandarśa parama ānanda nirvṛtāḥ bhīṣmaḥ droṇaḥ ambikā putraḥ gāndhārī sa sutā tathā sa dārāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kuntī sañjayaḥ viduraḥ kṛpaḥ kuntībhojaḥ virāṭaḥ ca bhīṣmakaḥ nagnajit mahān purujit drupadaḥ śalyaḥ dhṛṣṭaketuḥ sa kāśi rāj yudhāmanyuḥ suśarmā ca sa sutāḥ bāhlika ādayaḥ rājānaḥ ye ca rāja indra yudhiṣṭhiram anuvratāḥ śrī niketam vapuḥ śaureḥ sa strīkam vīkṣya vismitāḥ atha te rāma kṛṣṇābhyām samyak prāpta samarhaṇāḥ praśaśaṃsuḥ mudā yuktāḥ vṛṣṇīn kṛṣṇa parigrahān aho bhoja pate yūyam janma bhājaḥ nṛṇām iha yat paśyatha asakṛt kṛṣṇam durdarśam api yoginām yat viśrutiḥ śruti nutā idam alam punāti pādāvanejana payaḥ ca vacaḥ ca śāstram śayyā āsana aśana sayauna sapiṇḍa bandhaḥ yeṣām gṛhe niraya vartmani vartatām vaḥ svarga apavarga viramaḥ svayam āsa viṣṇuḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca nandaḥ tatra yadūn prāptān jñātvā kṛṣṇa purogamān tatra agamat vṛtaḥ gopaiḥ anaḥ stha arthaiḥ didṛkṣayā tam dṛṣṭvā vṛṣṇayaḥ hṛṣṭāḥ tanvaḥ prāṇam iva utthitāḥ pariṣasvajire gāḍham cira darśana kātarāḥ smaran kaṃsa kṛtān kleśān putra nyāsam ca gokule kṛṣṇa rāmau pariṣvajya pitarā abhivādya ca na kiñcana ūcatuḥ premṇā sa aśru kaṇṭhau kuru udvaha tau ātma āsanam āropya bāhubhyām parirabhya ca yaśodā ca mahā bhāgā sutau vijahatuḥ śucaḥ rohiṇī devakī ca atha pariṣvajya vrajeśvarīm smarantyau tad kṛtām maitrīm bāṣpa kaṇṭhyau samūcatuḥ kā vismareta vām maitrīm anivṛttām vrajeśvari etau adṛṣṭa pitarau yuvayoḥ sma pitroḥ samprīṇana abhyudaya poṣaṇa pālanāni śrī śukaḥ uvāca gopyaḥ ca kṛṣṇam upalabhya cirāt abhīṣṭam yad prekṣaṇe dṛśiṣu pakṣma kṛtam śapanti dṛgbhiḥ hṛdī kṛtam alam parirabhya sarvāḥ tad bhāvam āpuḥ api nitya yujām durāpam bhagavān tāḥ tathā bhūtāḥ viviktaḥ upasaṅgataḥ āśliṣya anāmayam pṛṣṭvā prahasan idam abravīt api smaratha naḥ sakhyaḥ svānām artha cikīrṣayā gatān cirāyitān śatru pakṣa kṣapaṇa cetasaḥ api avadhyāyatha asmān svid akṛta jñā viśaṅkayā vāyuḥ yathā ghana anīkam tṛṇam tūlam rajāṃsi ca saṃyojya ākṣipate bhūyas tathā bhūtāni bhūta kṛt diṣṭyā yat āsīt mad snehaḥ bhavatīnām mad āpanaḥ aham hi sarva bhūtānām ādiḥ antaḥ antaram bahis bhautikānām yathā kham vār bhūḥ vāyuḥ jyotiḥ aṅganāḥ evam hi etāni bhūtāni bhūteṣu ātma ātmanā tatas śrī śukaḥ uvāca adhyātma śikṣayā gopyaḥ evam kṛṣṇena śikṣitāḥ āhuḥ ca te nalina nābha pada aravindam saṃsāra kūpa patita uttaraṇa avalambam geham juṣām api manasi udiyāt sadā naḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca tathā anugṛhya bhagavān gopīnām sa guruḥ gatiḥ yudhiṣṭhiram atha apṛcchat sarvān ca suhṛdaḥ avyayam te evam loka nāthena paripṛṣṭāḥ su sat kṛtāḥ pratyūcuḥ hṛṣṭa manasaḥ tad pāda īkṣā hata aṃhasaḥ kutas aśivam tvad caraṇa ambuja āsavam mahat manastaḥ mukha niḥsṛtam kvacid kāla upasṛṣṭa nigama avana ātta yoga māyā ākṛtim paramahaṃsa gatim natāḥ sma śrī ṛṣiḥ uvāca iti uttamaḥ śloka śikhā maṇim janeṣu tri loka gītāḥ śṛṇu varṇayāmi te śrī draupadī uvāca he satyabhāme kālindi śaibye rohiṇi lakṣmaṇe śrī rukmiṇī uvāca rājasu ajeya bhaṭa śekharita aṅghri reṇuḥ ninye mṛgendraḥ iva bhāgam aja avi yūthāt śrī satyabhāmā uvāca liptā abhiśāpam apamārṣṭum upājahāra bhītaḥ pitā ādiśata mām prabhave api dattām śrī jāmbavatī uvāca prājñāya deha kṛt amum nija nātha daivam jñātvā parīkṣitaḥ upāharat arhaṇam mām pādau pragṛhya maṇinā aham amuṣya dāsī śrī kālindī uvāca tapaḥ carantīm ājñāya sva pāda sparśana āśayā sakhyā upetya agrahīt pāṇim yaḥ aham tad gṛha mārjanī śrī mitravindā uvāca ninye śva yūtha gam iva ātma balim dvipāriḥ bhrātṝn ca me apakurutaḥ sva puram śriyaukaḥ śrī satyā uvāca sapta ukṣaṇaḥ ati bala vīrya su tīkṣṇa śṛṅgān pitrā kṛtān kṣitipa vīrya parīkṣaṇāya krīḍan babandha ha yathā śiśavaḥ aja tokān yaḥ ittham vīrya śulkām mām dāsībhiḥ catur angiṇīm śrī bhadrā uvāca pitā me mātuleyāya svayam āhūya dattavān kṛṣṇe kṛṣṇāya tad cittām akṣauhiṇyā sakhī janaiḥ karmabhiḥ bhrāmyamāṇāyāḥ yena tat śreyaḥ ātmanaḥ śrī lakṣmaṇā uvāca jñātvā mama matam sādho pitā duhitṛ vatsalaḥ yathā svayaṃvare rājñi matsyaḥ pārtha īpsayā kṛtaḥ sarva astra śastra tattva jñāḥ sa upādhyāyāḥ sahasraśas pitrā sampūjitāḥ sarve yathā vīryam yathā vayaḥ ādaduḥ sa śaram cāpam veddhum parṣadi mad dhiyaḥ ādāya vyasṛjan kecid sajyam kartum anīśvarāḥ ā koṣṭham jyām samutkṛṣya petuḥ eke amunā āhatāḥ sajyam kṛtvā apare vīrāḥ māgadha ambaṣṭha cedipāḥ matsya ābhāsam jale vīkṣya jñātvā ca tad avasthitim pārthaḥ yattaḥ asṛjat bāṇam na ācchinat paspṛśe param rājanyeṣu nivṛtteṣu bhagna māneṣu māniṣu bhagavān dhanuḥ ādāya sajyam kṛtvā atha līlayā tasmin sandhāya viśikham matsyam vīkṣya sakṛt jale chittvā iṣuṇā apātayat tam sūrye ca abhijiti sthite devāḥ ca kusuma āsārān mumucuḥ harṣa vihvalāḥ tat raṅgam āviśam aham kala nūpurābhyām nūtne nivīya paridhāya ca kauśika agrye sa vrīḍa hāsa vadanā kavarī dhṛta sraj gaṇḍa sthalam śiśira hāsa kaṭākṣa mokṣaiḥ rājñaḥ nirīkṣya paritas śanakais murāreḥ aṃse anurakta hṛdayā nidadhe sva mālām tāvat mṛdaṅga paṭahāḥ śaṅkha bherī ānaka ādayaḥ evam vṛte bhagavati mayā īśe nṛpa yūthapāḥ na sehire yājñaseni spardhantaḥ hṛd śaya āturāḥ mām tāvat ratham āropya haya ratna catuṣṭayam dārukaḥ codayām āsa kāñcana upaskaram ratham miṣatām bhū bhujām rājñi mṛgāṇām mṛga rāj iva saṃyattāḥ uddhṛteṣu āsāḥ grāma siṃhāḥ yathā harim te śārṅga cyuta bāṇa oghaiḥ kṛtta bāhu aṅghri kandharāḥ tatas purīm yadu patiḥ ati alaṅkṛtām kuśasthalīm divi bhuvi ca abhisaṃstutām pitā me pūjayām āsa suhṛd sambandhi bāndhavān mahārha vāsaḥ alaṅkāraiḥ śayyā āsana paricchadaiḥ āyudhāni mahārhāni dadau pūrṇasya bhaktitaḥ ātma ārāmasya tasya imāḥ vayam vai gṛha dāsikāḥ sarva saṅga nivṛttyā addhā tapasā ca babhūvima mahiṣyaḥ ūcuḥ jñātvā atha naḥ kṣiti jaye jita rāja kanyāḥ pāda ambujam pariṇināya yaḥ āpta kāmaḥ na vayam sādhvi sāmrājyam svārājyam bhaujyam api uta vairājyam pārameṣṭhyam ca ānantyam vā hareḥ padam kāmayāmahe etasya śrīmat pāda rajaḥ śriyaḥ kuca kuṅkuma gandha āḍhyam mūrdhnā voḍhum gadā bhṛtaḥ gāvaḥ cārayataḥ gopāḥ pada sparśam mahātmanaḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca śrutvā pṛthā subala putrī atha yājñasenī kṛṣṇe akhilātmani harau praṇaya anubandham sarvāḥ visismyuḥ alam aśru kalā ākula akṣyaḥ iti sambhāṣamāṇāsu strībhiḥ strīṣu nṛbhiḥ nṛṣu āyayuḥ munayaḥ tatra kṛṣṇa rāma didṛkṣayā viśvāmitraḥ śatānandaḥ bharadvājaḥ atha gautamaḥ rāmaḥ sa śiṣyaḥ bhagavān vasiṣṭhaḥ gālavaḥ bhṛguḥ pulastyaḥ kaśyapaḥ atriḥ ca mārkaṇḍeyaḥ bṛhaspatiḥ dvitaḥ tritaḥ ca ekataḥ ca brahma putrāḥ tathā aṅgirāḥ tān dṛṣṭvā sahasā utthāya prāk āsīnāḥ nṛpa ādayaḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kṛṣṇa rāmau ca praṇemuḥ viśva vanditān svāgata āsana pādya arghya mālya dhūpa anulepanaiḥ uvāca sukham āsīnān bhagavān dharma gup tanuḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca devānām api duṣprāpam yat yogeśvara darśanam kim su alpa tapasām nṝṇām arcāyām deva cakṣuṣām na hi am mayāni tīrthāni na devāḥ mṛd śilā mayāḥ na bhūḥ jalam kham śvasanaḥ atha vāc manaḥ sva dhīḥ kalatra ādiṣu bhaumaḥ ijya dhīḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca niśamya ittham bhagavataḥ kṛṣṇasya akuṇtha medhasaḥ vacaḥ duranvayam viprāḥ tūṣṇīm āsan bhramat dhiyaḥ ciram vimṛśya munayaḥ īśvarasya īśitavya tām śrī munayaḥ ūcuḥ yad māyayā tattva vid uttamāḥ vayam vimohitāḥ viśva sṛjām adhīśvarāḥ yat gūḍhe īhayā aho vicitram bhagavat viceṣṭitam bhaumaiḥ hi bhūmiḥ bahu nāma rūpiṇī aho vibhūmnaḥ caritam viḍambanam sva līlayā veda patham sanātanam varṇa āśrama ātmā puruṣaḥ paraḥ bhavān brahma te hṛdayam śuklam tapaḥ svādhyāya saṃyamaiḥ sabhājayasi sat dhāma tat brahmaṇya agraṇī bhavān adya naḥ janma sāphalyam vidyāyāḥ tapasaḥ dṛśaḥ tvayā saṅgamya sat gatyā yat antaḥ śreyasām paraḥ namaḥ tasmai bhagavate kṛṣṇāya akuṇṭha medhase na yam vidanti amī bhū pāḥ eka ārāmāḥ ca vṛṣṇayaḥ māyā javanikā ācchannam ātmānam kālam īśvaram yathā śayānaḥ puruṣaḥ ātmānam guṇa tattva dṛś nāma mātra indriya ābhātam na veda rahitam param evam tvā nāma mātreṣu viṣayeṣu indriya īhayā tasya adya te dadṛśima aṅghrim agha ogha marṣa tīrtha āspadam hṛdi kṛtam su vipakva yogaiḥ utsikta bhakti upahata āśaya jīva kośā śrī śukaḥ uvāca iti anujñāpya dāśārham dhṛtarāṣṭram yudhiṣṭhiram rājarṣe sva āśramān gantum munayaḥ dadhire manaḥ tat vīkṣya tān upavrajya vasudevaḥ mahā yaśāḥ praṇamya ca upasaṅgṛhya babhāṣa idam su yantritaḥ śrī vasudevaḥ uvāca śrī nāradaḥ uvāca kṛṣṇam matvā arbhakam yat naḥ pṛcchati śreyaḥ ātmanaḥ sannikarṣaḥ atra martyānām anādaraṇa kāraṇam gāṅgam hitvā yathā anya ambhaḥ tatratyaḥ yāti śuddhaye yasya anubhūtiḥ kālena laya utpatti ādinā asya vai tam kleśa karma paripāka guṇa pravāhaiḥ avyāhata anubhavam īśvaram advitīyam sarveṣām śṛṇvatām rājñām tathā eva acyuta rāmayoḥ karmaṇā karma nirhāraḥ eṣa sādhu nirūpitaḥ yat śraddhayā yajet viṣṇum sarva yajña īśvaram makhaiḥ cittasya upaśamaḥ ayam vai kavibhiḥ śāstra cakṣusā darśitaḥ su gamaḥ yogaḥ dharmaḥ ca ātma mud āvahaḥ vitta eṣaṇām yajña dānaiḥ gṛhaiḥ dāra suta eṣaṇām ātma loka eṣaṇām deva kālena visṛjet budhaḥ grāme tyakta eṣaṇāḥ sarve yayuḥ dhīrāḥ tapaḥ vanam ṛṇaiḥ tribhiḥ dvijaḥ jātaḥ deva ṛṣi pitṝṇām prabho tvam tu adya muktaḥ dvābhyām vai ṛṣi pitroḥ mahā mate yajñaiḥ deva ṛṇam unmucya nirṛṇaḥ aśaraṇaḥ bhava jagatām īśvaram prārcaḥ sa yat vām putra tām gataḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca iti tat vacanam śrutvā vasudevaḥ mahā manāḥ tān ṛṣīn ṛtvijaḥ vavre mūrdhnā ānamya prasādya ca te enam ṛṣayaḥ rājan vṛtāḥ dharmeṇa dhārmikam tad dīkṣāyām pravṛttāyām vṛṣṇayaḥ puṣkara srajaḥ snātāḥ su vāsasaḥ rājan rājānaḥ suṣṭhu alaṅkṛtāḥ tad mahiṣyaḥ ca muditāḥ niṣka kaṇṭhyaḥ su vāsasaḥ dīkṣā śālām upājagmuḥ āliptāḥ vastu pāṇayaḥ neduḥ mṛdaṅga paṭaha śaṅkha bherī ānaka ādayaḥ nanṛtuḥ naṭa nartakyaḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ sūta māgadhāḥ jaguḥ su kaṇṭhyaḥ gandharvyaḥ saṅgītam saha bhartṛkāḥ patnībhiḥ aṣṭādaśabhiḥ soma rājam iva uḍubhiḥ tābhiḥ dukūla valayaiḥ hāra nūpura kuṇḍalaiḥ su alaṅkṛtābhiḥ vibabhau dīkṣitaḥ ajina saṃvṛtaḥ tadā rāmaḥ ca kṛṣṇaḥ ca svaiḥ svaiḥ bandhubhiḥ anvitau īje anu yajñam vidhinā agni hotra ādi lakṣaṇaiḥ atha ṛtvigbhyaḥ adadāt kāle yathāmnātam sa dakṣiṇāḥ su alaṅkṛtebhyaḥ alaṅkṛtya go bhū kanyāḥ mahā dhanāḥ patnī saṃyāja āvabhṛthyaiḥ caritvā te mahā ṛṣayaḥ sasnuḥ rāma hrade viprāḥ yajamāna puraḥsarāḥ snātaḥ alaṅkāra vāsāṃsi vandibhyaḥ adāt tathā striyaḥ tatas su alaṅkṛtaḥ varṇān ā śvabhyaḥ annena pūjayat bandhūn sa dārān sa sutān pāribarheṇa bhūyasā vidarbha kośala kurūn kāśi kekaya sṛñjayān sadasyartvij sura gaṇān nṛ bhūta pitṛ cāraṇān śrī niketam anujñāpya śaṃsantaḥ prayayuḥ kratum dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ anujaḥ pārthāḥ bhīṣmaḥ droṇaḥ pṛthā yamau nāradaḥ bhagavān vyāsaḥ suhṛd sambandhi bāndhavāḥ yayuḥ viraha kṛcchreṇa sva deśān ca apare janāḥ nandaḥ tu saha gopālaiḥ bṛhatyā pūjayā arcitaḥ kṛṣṇa rāma ugrasena ādyaiḥ nyavātsīt bandhu vatsalaḥ suhṛd vṛtaḥ prīta manāḥ nandam āha kare spṛśan śrī vasudevaḥ uvāca bhrātar īśa kṛtaḥ pāśaḥ nṛnām yaḥ sneha saṃjñitaḥ tam dustyajam aham manye śūrāṇām api yoginām asmāsu apratikalpā iyam yat kṛta ājñeṣu sattamaiḥ prāk akalpāt ca kuśalam bhrātar vaḥ na ācarāma hi adhunā śrī mada andha akṣāḥ na paśyāmaḥ puras sataḥ mā rājya śrīḥ abhūt puṃsaḥ śreyaḥ kāmasya māna da sva janān uta bandhūn vā na paśyati yayā andha dṛś śrī śukaḥ uvāca ruroda tad kṛtām maitrīm smaran aśru vilocanaḥ adya śvas iti māsān trīn yadubhiḥ mānitaḥ avasat tatas kāmaiḥ pūryamāṇaḥ sa vrajaḥ saha bāndhavaḥ parārdhya ābharaṇa kṣauma nānā anarghya paricchadaiḥ vasudeva ugrasenābhyām kṛṣṇa uddhava bala ādibhiḥ manaḥ kṣiptam punar hartum anīśāḥ mathurām yayuḥ bandhuṣu pratiyāteṣu vṛṣṇayaḥ kṛṣṇa devatāḥ vīkṣya prāvṛṣam āsannāt yayuḥ dvāravatīm punar yat āsīt tīrtha yātrāyām suhṛd sandarśana ādikam śrī bādarāyaṇiḥ uvāca vasudevaḥ abhinandya āha prītyā saṅkarṣaṇa acyutau munīnām sa vacaḥ śrutvā putrayoḥ dhāma sūcakam tad vīryaiḥ jāta viśrambhaḥ paribhāṣya abhyabhāṣata kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa mahā yogin saṅkarṣaṇa sanātana jāne vām asya yat sākṣāt pradhāna puruṣau parau syāt idam bhagavān sākṣāt pradhāna puruṣa īśvaraḥ etat nānā vidham viśvam ātma sṛṣṭam adhokṣaja ātmanā anupraviśya ātman prāṇaḥ jīvaḥ bibharṣi aja prāṇa ādīnām viśva sṛjām śaktayaḥ yāḥ parasya tāḥ pāratantryāt vaisādṛṣyāt dvayoḥ ceṣṭā eva ceṣṭatām yat sthairyam bhū bhṛtām bhūmeḥ vṛttiḥ gandhaḥ arthatas bhavān tarpaṇam prāṇanam apām deva tvam tāḥ ca tad rasaḥ ojaḥ sahaḥ balam ca iṣṭā gatiḥ vāyoḥ tava īśvara diśām tvam avakāśaḥ asi diśaḥ kham sphoṭaḥ āśrayaḥ nādaḥ varṇaḥ tvam oṃkāraḥ ākṛtīnām pṛthak kṛtiḥ indriyam tu indriyāṇām tvam devāḥ ca tad anugrahaḥ avabodhaḥ bhavān buddheḥ jīvasya anusmṛtiḥ satī bhūtānām asi bhūtādiḥ indriyāṇām ca taijasaḥ vaikārikaḥ vikalpānām pradhānam anuśāyinam yathā dravya vikāreṣu dravya mātram nirūpitam sattvam rajaḥ tamaḥ iti guṇāḥ tad vṛttayaḥ ca yāḥ tvam ca amīṣu vikāreṣu hi anyadā āvyāvahārikaḥ gatim sūkṣmām abodhena saṃsaranti iha karmabhiḥ yadṛcchayā nṛtām prāpya su kalpām iha durlabhām yuvām na naḥ sutau sākṣāt pradhāna puruṣa īśvarau bhū bhāra kṣatra kṣapaṇa avatīrṇau tathā āttha ha āpanna saṃsṛti bhaya apaham ārta bandho sūtī gṛhe nanu jagāda bhavān ajaḥ nau kaḥ veda bhūmnaḥ uru gāya vibhūti māyām śrī śukaḥ uvāca ākarṇya ittham pituḥ vākyam bhagavān sātvata ṛṣabhaḥ pratyāha praśraya ānamraḥ prahasan ślakṣṇayā girā śrī bhagavān uvāca yat naḥ putrān samuddiśya tattva grāmaḥ udāhṛtaḥ aham yūyam asau āryaḥ ime ca dvārakā okāḥ sarve api evam yadu śreṣṭha vimṛgyāḥ sa carācaram ātmā hi ekaḥ svayam jyotiḥ nityaḥ anyaḥ nirguṇaḥ guṇaiḥ ātma sṛṣṭaiḥ tad kṛteṣu bhūteṣu bahudhā īyate kham vāyuḥ jyotiḥ āpaḥ bhūḥ tad kṛteṣu yathāśayam āvis tiras alpa bhūri ekaḥ nānātvam yāti asau api śrī śukaḥ uvāca evam bhagavatā rājan vasudevaḥ udāhṛtaḥ śrutvā vinaṣṭa nānā dhīḥ tūṣṇīm prīta manāḥ abhūt śrutvā ānītam guroḥ putram ātmajābhyām su vismitā kṛṣṇa rāmau samāśrāvya putrān kaṃsa vihiṃsitān smarantī kṛpaṇam prāha vaiklavyāt aśru locanā śrī devakī uvāca rāma rāma aprameya ātman kṛṣṇa yogeśvara īśvara veda aham vām viśva sṛjām īśvarau ādi pūruṣau kala vidhvasta sattvānām rājñām ucchāstra vartinām bhūmeḥ bhārāyamāṇānām avatīrṇau kila adya me yasya aṃśa aṃśa aṃśa bhāgena viśva utpatti laya udayāḥ bhavanti kila viśvātman tam tvā adya aham gatim gatā cirāt mṛta sutā dāne guruṇā kila coditau āninyathuḥ pitṛ sthānāt gurave guru dakṣiṇām tathā me kurutam kāmam yuvām yoga īśvara īśvarau bhoja rāja hatān putrān kāmaye draṣṭum āhṛtān ṛṣiḥ uvāca evam sañcoditau mātrā rāmaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ ca bhārata sutalam saṃviviśatuḥ yoga māyām upāśritau tasmin praviṣṭau upalabhya daitya rāj viśvātma daivam sutarām tathā ātmanaḥ tad darśana āhlāda paripluta āśayaḥ sadyas samutthāya nanāma sa anvayaḥ tayoḥ samānīya varāsanam mudā niviṣṭayoḥ tatra mahātmanoḥ tayoḥ tāmbūla dīpa amṛta bhakṣaṇa ādibhiḥ sva gotra vitta ātma samarpaṇena ca uvāca ha ānanda jala ākula īkṣaṇaḥ prahṛṣṭa romā nṛpa gadgada akṣaram namaḥ anantāya bṛhate namaḥ kṛṣṇāya vedhase sāṅkhya yoga vitānāya brahmaṇe paramātmane darśanam vām hi bhūtānām duṣprāpam ca api adurlabham rajaḥ tamaḥ svabhāvānām yat naḥ prāptau yadṛcchayā daitya dānava gandharvāḥ siddha vidyādhra cāraṇāḥ yakṣa rakṣaḥ piśācāḥ ca bhūta pramatha nāyakāḥ viśuddha sattva dhāmni addhā tvayi śāstra śarīriṇi nityam nibaddha vairāḥ te vayam ca anye ca tādṛśāḥ na tathā sattva saṃrabdhāḥ sannikṛṣṭāḥ sura ādayaḥ pāda aravinda dhiṣaṇā anya gṛha andha kūpāt niṣkramya viśva śaraṇa aṅghri upalabdha vṛttiḥ śādhi asmān īśitavya īśa niṣpāpān kuru naḥ prabho pumān yat śraddhayā a tiṣṭhan codanāyāḥ vimucyate śrī bhagavān uvāca āsan marīceḥ ṣaṭ putrāḥ ūrṇāyām prathame antare hiraṇyakaśipoḥ jātāḥ nītāḥ te yoga māyayā devakyāḥ udare jātāḥ rājan kaṃsa vihiṃsitāḥ sā tān śocati ātmajān svān te ime adhyāsate antike itas etān praṇeṣyāmaḥ mātṛ śoka apanuttaye tatas śāpāt vinirmaktāḥ lokam yāsyanti vijvarāḥ smara udgīthaḥ pariṣvaṅgaḥ pataṅgaḥ kṣudrabhṛt ghṛṇī punar dvāravatīm etya mātuḥ putrān ayacchatām tān dṛṣṭvā bālakān devī putra sneha snuta stanī pariṣvajya aṅkam āropya mūrdhni ajighrat abhīkṣṇaśas mohitāḥ māyayā viṣṇoḥ yayā sṛṣṭiḥ pravartate pītvā amṛtam payaḥ tasyāḥ pīta śeṣam gadā bhṛtaḥ nārāyaṇa aṅga saṃsparśa pratilabdha ātma darśanāḥ miṣatām sarva bhūtānām yayuḥ dhāma divaukasām tam dṛṣṭvā devakī devī mṛta āgamana nirgamam mene su vismitā māyām kṛṣṇasya racitām nṛpa evaṃvidhāni adbhutāni kṛṣṇasya paramātmanaḥ śrī sūtaḥ uvāca yaḥ idam anuśṛṇoti śrāvayet vā murāreḥ caritam amṛta kīrteḥ varṇitam vyāsa putraiḥ śrī rājā uvāca brahman veditum icchāmaḥ svasārām rāma kṛṣṇayoḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca arjunaḥ tīrtha yātrāyām paryaṭan avanīm prabhuḥ gataḥ prabhāsam aśṛṇot mātuleyīm saḥ ātmanaḥ duryodhanāya rāmaḥ tām dāsyati iti na ca apare tad lipsuḥ sa yatiḥ bhūtvā tri daṇḍī dvārakām agāt tatra vai vārṣitān māsān avātsīt sva artha sādhakaḥ pauraiḥ sabhājitaḥ abhīkṣṇam rāmeṇa a jānatā ca saḥ saḥ apaśyat tatra mahatīm kanyām vīra manaḥ harām prīti utphulla īkṣaṇaḥ tasyām bhāva kṣubdham manaḥ dadhe sā api tam cakame vīkṣya nārīṇām hṛdayaṃgamam hasantī vrīḍita apaṅgā tad nyasta hṛdaya īkṣaṇā na lebhe śam bhramat cittaḥ kāmena ati balīyasā mahatyām deva yātrāyām ratha sthām durga nirgatām jahāra anumataḥ pitroḥ kṛṣṇasya ca mahā rathaḥ ratha sthaḥ dhanuḥ ādāya śūrān ca arundhataḥ bhaṭān vidrāvya krośatām svānām sva bhāgam mṛga rāj iva tat śrutvā kṣubhitaḥ rāmaḥ parvaṇi iva mahā arṇavaḥ gṛhīta pādaḥ kṛṣṇena suhṛdbhiḥ ca anusāntvitaḥ prāhiṇot pāribarhāṇi vara vadhvoḥ mudā balaḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca kṛṣṇasya āsīt dvija śreṣṭhaḥ śrutadevaḥ iti śrutaḥ kṛṣṇa eka bhaktyā pūrṇa arthaḥ śāntaḥ kaviḥ alampataḥ saḥ uvāsa videheṣu mithilāyām gṛha āśramī na adhikam tāvatā tuṣṭaḥ kriyāḥ cakre yathā ucitāḥ tathā tad rāṣṭra pālaḥ aṅga bahulāśvaḥ iti śrutaḥ tayoḥ prasannaḥ bhagavān dārukeṇa āhṛtam ratham nāradaḥ vāmadevaḥ atriḥ kṛṣṇaḥ rāmaḥ asitaḥ aruṇiḥ aham bṛhaspatiḥ kaṇvaḥ maitreyaḥ cyavana ādayaḥ tatra tatra tam āyāntam paurāḥ jānapadāḥ nṛpa pāñcāla kunti madhu kekaya kośala arṇāḥ snigdha īkṣaṇam nṛpa papuḥ dṛśibhiḥ nṛ nāryaḥ tebhyaḥ sva vīkṣaṇa vinaṣṭa tamisra dṛgbhyaḥ śṛṇvan diś anta dhavalam sva yaśaḥ aśubha ghnam te acyutam prāptam ākarṇya paurāḥ jānapadāḥ nṛpa abhīyuḥ muditāḥ tasmai gṛhīta arhaṇa pāṇayaḥ dṛṣṭvā te uttamaḥ ślokam prīti utphula ānana āśayāḥ kaiḥ dhṛtāñjalibhiḥ nemuḥ śruta pūrvān tathā munīn maithilaḥ śrutadevaḥ ca pādayoḥ petatuḥ prabhoḥ nyamantrayetām dāśārham ātithyena saha dvijaiḥ maithilaḥ śrutadevaḥ ca yugapad saṃhata añjalī ubhayoḥ āviśat geham ubhābhyām tad alakṣitaḥ śrāntān api atha tān dūrāt janakaḥ sva gṛha āgatān ānīteṣu āsana agryeṣu sukha āsīnān mahā manāḥ pravṛddha bhaktyā uddharṣa hṛdaya asra āvila īkṣaṇaḥ natvā tad aṅghrīn prakṣālya tad apaḥ loka pāvanīḥ sa kuṭumbaḥ vahan mūrdhnā cakre īśvarān gandha mālya ambara ākalpa dhūpa dīpa arghya go vṛṣaiḥ vācā madhurayā prīṇan idam āha anna tarpitān pādau aṅka gatau viṣṇoḥ saṃspṛśan śanakais mudā śrī bahulāśvaḥ uvāca bhavān hi sarva bhūtānām ātmā sākṣī sva dṛś vibho atha naḥ tvad pada ambhojam smaratām darśanam gataḥ yat āttha ekānta bhaktāt me na anantaḥ śrīḥ ajaḥ priyaḥ niṣkiñcanānām śāntānām munīnām yaḥ tvam ātma daḥ yaḥ avatīrya yadoḥ vaṃśe nṛṇām saṃsaratām iha namaḥ tubhyam bhagavate kṛṣṇāya akuṇṭha medhase nārāyaṇāya ṛṣaye su śāntam tapaḥ īyuṣe sametaḥ pāda rajasā punīhi idam nimeḥ kulam iti upāmantritaḥ rājñā bhagavān loka bhāvanaḥ uvāsa kurvan kalyāṇam mithilā nara yoṣitām śrutadevaḥ acyutam prāptam sva gṛhān janakaḥ yathā natvā munīn su saṃhṛṣṭaḥ dhunvan vāsaḥ nanarta ha tṛṇa pīṭha bṛṣīṣu etān ānīteṣu upaveśya saḥ svāgatena abhinandya aṅghrīn sa bhāryaḥ avanije mudā tad ambhasā mahābhāgaḥ ātmānam sa gṛha anvayam phala arhaṇa uśīra śivā amṛtā ambuṣu mṛdā surabhyā tulasī kuśa ambuyaiḥ yaḥ sarva tīrtha āspada pāda reṇubhiḥ kṛṣṇena ca asya ātma niketa bhūsuraiḥ su upaviṣṭān kṛta ātithyān śrutadevaḥ upasthitaḥ sa bhāryā sva janāpatyaḥ uvāca aṅghri abhimarśanaḥ na adya naḥ darśanam prāptaḥ param parama pūruṣaḥ yarhi idam śaktibhiḥ sṛṣṭvā praviṣṭaḥ hi ātma sattayā yathā śayānaḥ puruṣaḥ manasā eva ātma māyayā sṛṣṭvā lokam param svāpnam anuviśya avabhāsate śṛṇvatām gadatām śaśvat arcatām tvā abhivandatām saṃvadatām antar hṛdi bhāsi amala ātmanām sa kāraṇa akāraṇa liṅgam īyuṣe sva māyayā asaṃvṛta ruddha dṛṣṭaye sa tvam śādhi sva bhṛtyān naḥ kim deva karavāma he etad antaḥ nṛṇām kleśaḥ yat bhavān akṣi gocaraḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca tat uktam iti upākarṇya bhagavān praṇata ārti hā gṛhītvā pāṇinā pāṇim prahasan tam uvāca ha śrī bhagavān uvāca sañcaranti mayā lokān punantaḥ pāda reṇubhiḥ devāḥ kṣetrāṇi tīrthāni darśana sparśana arcanaiḥ brāhmaṇaḥ janmanā śreyān sarveṣām prāṇinām iha tapasā vidyayā tuṣṭyā kim u mad kalayā yutaḥ duṣprajñāḥ a viditvā evam avajānanti asūyavaḥ gurum mām vipram ātmānam arcā ādau ijya dṛṣṭayaḥ carācaram idam viśvam bhāvāḥ ye ca asya hetavaḥ mad rūpāṇi iti cetasi ādhatte vipraḥ mad īkṣayā evam ced arcitaḥ asmi addhā na anyathā bhūri bhūtibhiḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca saḥ ittham prabhunā ādiṣṭaḥ saha kṛṣṇān dvijottamān uṣitvā ādiśya sat mārgam punar dvāravatīm agāt śrī parīkṣit uvāca katham caranti śrutayaḥ sākṣāt sat asataḥ pare śrī śukaḥ uvāca buddhīndriya manaḥ prāṇān janānām asṛjat prabhuḥ mātrā artham ca bhava artham ca ātmane akalpanāya ca sā eṣā hi upaniṣad brāhmī pūrva īśām pūrva jaiḥ dhṛtā śrraddhayā dhārayet yaḥ tām kṣemam gacchet akiñcanaḥ atra te varṇayiṣyāmi gāthām nārāyaṇa anvitām nāradasya ca saṃvādam ṛṣeḥ nārāyaṇasya ca sanātanam ṛṣim draṣṭum yayau nārāyaṇa āśramam yaḥ vai bhārata varṣe asmin kṣemāya svastaye nṛṇām dharma jñāna śama upetam ā kalpāt āsthitaḥ tapaḥ tatra upaviṣṭam ṛṣibhiḥ kalāpa grāma vāsibhiḥ tasmai hi avocat bhagavān ṛṣīṇām śṛṇvatām idam yaḥ brahma vādaḥ pūrveṣām jana loka nivāsinām śrī bhagavān uvāca tatra sthānām mānasānām munīnām ūrdhva retasām śvetadvīpam gatavati tvayi draṣṭum tad īśvaram brahma vādaḥ su saṃvṛttaḥ śrutayaḥ yatra śerate tatra ha ayam abhūt praśnaḥ tvam mām yam anupṛcchasi tulya śruta tapaḥ śīlāḥ tulya svīya ari madhyamāḥ api cakruḥ pravacanam ekam śuśrūṣavaḥ apare śrī sanandanaḥ uvāca sva sṛṣṭam idam āpīya śayānam saha śaktibhiḥ yathā śayānam saṃrājam vandinaḥ tad parākramaiḥ śrī śrutayaḥ ūcuḥ jaya jaya jahi ajām ajita doṣa gṛbhīta guṇām yatas udaya astam ayau vikṛteḥ mṛdi vā a vikṛtāt kṣapaṇa kathā amṛta abdhim avagāhya tapāṃsi jahuḥ kim uta punar sva dhāma vidhuta āśaya kāla guṇāḥ sat asataḥ param tvam atha yat eṣu avaśeṣam ṛtam udaram upāsate ye ṛṣi vartmasu kūrpa dṛśaḥ taratamataḥ cakāssi anala vat sva kṛta anukṛtiḥ atha vitathāsu amūṣu avitathām tava dhāma samam sva kṛta pureṣu amīṣu abahir antara saṃvaraṇam tava puruṣam vadanti akhila śakti dhṛtaḥ aṃśa kṛtam carita mahā mṛta abdhi parivarta pariśramaṇāḥ caraṇa saroja haṃsa kula saṅga visṛṣṭa gṛhāḥ vayam api te samāḥ sama dṛśaḥ aṅghri saroja sudhāḥ kim api na tatra śāstram avakṛṣya śayīta yadā vipaṇam ṛtam smaranti upadiśanti te ārupitaiḥ tri guṇa mayaḥ pumān iti bhidā yat abodha kṛtā sat abhimṛśanti aśeṣam idam ātma tayā ātma vidaḥ parivayase paśūn iva girā vibudhān api tān viyataḥ iva āpadasya tava śūnya tulām dadhataḥ samam anujānatām yat amatam mata duṣṭa tayā saritaḥ iva arṇave madhuni lilyuḥ aśeṣa rasāḥ nṛṣu tava bhramam amīṣu avagatya bhṛśam vijita hṛṣīka vāyubhiḥ adānta manaḥ tura gam vyasana śata anvitāḥ samavahāya guroḥ caraṇam tvayi sati kim nṛṇām śrayate ātmani sarva rase bhuvi puru puṇya tīrtha sadanāni ṛṣayaḥ vimadāḥ sa yat ajayā tu ajām anuśayīta guṇān ca juṣan duradhigamaḥ asatām hṛdi gataḥ asmṛta kaṇṭha maṇiḥ an apagata antakāt an adhirūḍha padāt bhavataḥ guṇa viguṇa anvayān tarhi dehabhṛtām ca giraḥ tvam api yad antara aṇḍa nicayāḥ nanu sa āvaraṇāḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca iti etat brahmaṇaḥ putrāḥ āśrutya ātma anuśāsanam iti aśeṣa samāmnāya purāṇa upaniṣad rasaḥ samuddhṛtaḥ pūrva jātaiḥ vyoma yānaiḥ mahātmabhiḥ tvam ca etat brahma dāyāda śraddhayā ātma anuśāsanam dhārayan cara gām kāmam kāmānām bharjanam nṛṇām śrī śukaḥ uvāca evam saḥ ṛṣiṇā ādiṣṭam gṛhītvā śraddhayā ātmavān pūrṇaḥ śruta dharaḥ rājan āha vīra vrataḥ muniḥ śrī nāradaḥ uvāca namaḥ tasmai bhagavate kṛṣṇāya amala kīrtaye yaḥ dhatte sarva bhūtānām abhavāya uśatīḥ kalāḥ iti ādyam ṛṣim ānamya tad śiṣyān ca mahātmanaḥ tatas agāt āśramam sākṣāt pituḥ dvaipāyanasya me tasmai tat varṇayām āsa nārāyaṇa mukhāt śrutam iti etat varṇitam rājan yat naḥ praśnaḥ kṛtaḥ tvayā yathā brahmaṇi anirdeśye nīḍa guṇe api manaḥ caret yaḥ sṛṣṭvā idam anupraviśya ṛṣiṇā cakre puras śāsti tāḥ yam sampadya jahāti ajām anuśayī suptaḥ kulāyam yathā śrī rājā uvāca viruddha śīlayoḥ prabhvoḥ viruddhā bhajatām gatiḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca śivaḥ śakti yutaḥ śaśvat tri liṅgaḥ guṇa saṃvṛtaḥ tatas vikārāḥ abhavan ṣoḍaśa amīṣu kañcana upadhāvan vibhūtīnām sarvāsām aśnute gatim hariḥ hi nirguṇaḥ sākṣāt puruṣaḥ prakṛtyāḥ paraḥ nivṛtteṣu aśva medheṣu rājā yuṣmad pitāmahaḥ saḥ āha bhagavān tasmai prītaḥ śuśrūṣave prabhuḥ nṛṇām niḥśreyasa arthāya yaḥ avatīrṇaḥ yadoḥ kule śrī bhagavān uvāca yasya aham anugṛhṇāmi hariṣye tad dhanam śanais sa yadā vitatha udyogaḥ nirviṇṇaḥ syāt dhana īhayā vijñāya ātma tayā dhīraḥ saṃsārāt parimucyate atas mām su durārādhyam hitvā anyān bhajate janaḥ tatas te āśu toṣebhyaḥ labdha rājya śriyā uddhatāḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca śāpa prasādayoḥ īśāḥ brahma viṣṇu śiva ādayaḥ sadyas śāpa prasādaḥ aṅga śivaḥ brahmā na ca acyutaḥ vṛka asurāya giriśaḥ varam dattvā āpa saṅkaṭam vṛkaḥ nāma asuraḥ putraḥ śakuneḥ pathi nāradam dṛṣṭvā āśu toṣam papraccha deveṣu triṣu durmatiḥ saḥ āha devam giriśam upādhau āśu siddhi asi yaḥ alpābhyām guṇa doṣābhyām āśu tuṣyati kupyati daśa āsya bāṇayoḥ tuṣṭaḥ stuvatoḥ vandinoḥ iva aiśvaryam atulam dattvā tatas āpa su saṅkaṭam iti ādiṣṭaḥ tam asuraḥ upādhāvat sva gātrataḥ tadā mahā kāruṇikaḥ sa dhūrjaṭiḥ yathā vayam ca agniḥ iva utthitaḥ analāt nigṛhya dorbhyām bhujayoḥ nyavārayat tad sparśanāt bhūyas upaskṛta ākṛtiḥ tam āha cāṅgālam alam vṛṇīṣva me yathā abhikāmam vitarāmi te varam prīyeya toyena nṛṇām prapadyatām aho tvayā ātmā bhṛśam ardyate vṛthak devam sa vavre pāpīyān varam bhūta bhaya āvaham yasya yasya karam śīrṣṇi dhāsye sa mriyatām iti sa tad vara parīkṣā artham śambhoḥ mūrdhni kila asuraḥ tena upasṛṣṭaḥ santrastaḥ parādhāvan sa vepathuḥ yāvat antam divaḥ bhūmeḥ kaṣṭhānām udagāt udak a jānantaḥ prati vidhim tūṣṇīm āsan sureśvarāḥ yatra nārāyaṇaḥ sākṣāt nyāsinām paramaḥ gatiḥ śāntānām nyasta daṇḍānām yatas na āvartate gataḥ tam tathā vyasanam dṛṣṭvā bhagavān vṛjina ardanaḥ dūrāt pratyudiyāt bhūtvā baṭukaḥ yoga māyayā mekhalā ajina daṇḍa akṣaiḥ tejasā agniḥ iva jvalan abhivādayām āsa ca tam kuśa pāṇiḥ vinīta vat śrī bhagavān uvāca śākuneya bhavān vyaktam śrāntaḥ kim dūram āgataḥ kṣaṇam viśramyatām puṃsaḥ ātmā ayam sarva kāma duh yadi naḥ śravaṇāya alam tvad vyavasitam vibho bhaṇyatām prāyaśas pumbhiḥ dhṛtaiḥ sva arthān samīhate śrī śukaḥ uvāca evam bhagavatā pṛṣṭaḥ vacasā amṛta varṣiṇā śrī bhagavān uvāca yaḥ dakṣa śāpāt paiśācyam prāptaḥ preta piśāca rāj tarhi aṅga āśu sva śirasi hastam nyasya pratīyatām yadi asatyam vacaḥ śambhoḥ kathaṃcid dānava ṛṣabha tadā enam jahi asat vācam na yat vaktā anṛtam punar bhinna dhīḥ vismṛtaḥ śīrṣṇi sva hastam kumatiḥ nyadhāt atha apatat bhinna śirāḥ vraja āhataḥ iva kṣaṇāt jaya śabdaḥ namaḥ śabdaḥ sādhu śabdaḥ abhavat divi mumucuḥ puṣpa varṣāṇi hate pāpe vṛka asure deva ṛṣi pitṛ gandharvāḥ mocitaḥ saṅkaṭāt śivaḥ muktam giriśam abhyāha bhagavant puruṣottamaḥ hataḥ kaḥ nu mahatsu īśa jantuḥ vai kṛta kilbiṣaḥ kṣemī syāt kim viśveśe kṛta āgaskaḥ jagat gurau yaḥ evam avyākṛta śakti udanvataḥ parasya sākṣāt paramātmanaḥ hareḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca sarasvatyāḥ taṭe rājan ṛṣayaḥ satram āsata vitarkaḥ samabhūt teṣām triṣu adhīśeṣu kaḥ mahān tasya jijñāsayā te vai bhṛgum brahma sutam nṛpa tad jñaptyai preṣayām āsuḥ saḥ abhjagāt brahmaṇaḥ sabhām aśīśamat yathā vahnim sva yonyā vāriṇā ātma bhūḥ parirabdhum samārebhe utthāya bhrātaram mudā patitvā pādayoḥ devī sāntvayām āsa tam girā atho jagāma vaikuṇṭham yatra devaḥ janārdanaḥ śayānam śriyaḥ utsaṅge padā vakṣasi atāḍayat tatas utthāya bhagavān saha lakṣmyā satām gatiḥ āha te svāgatam brahman niṣīda atra āsane kṣaṇam a jānatām āgatān vaḥ kṣantum arhatha naḥ prabho punīhi saha lokam mām loka pālān ca mad gatān pāda udakena bhavataḥ tīrthānām tīrtha kāriṇā adya aham bhagavan lakṣmyāḥ āsam ekānta bhājanam śrī śukaḥ uvāca evam bruvāṇe vaikuṇṭhe bhṛguḥ tat mandrayā girā nirvṛtaḥ tarpitaḥ tūṣṇīm bhakti utkaṇṭhaḥ aśru locanaḥ punar ca satram āvrajya munīnām brahma vādinām sva anubhūtam aśeṣeṇa rājan bhṛguḥ avarṇayat tat niśamya atha munayaḥ vismitāḥ mukta saṃśayāḥ bhūyasam śraddadhuḥ viṣṇum yatas śāntiḥ yatas abhayam dharmaḥ sākṣāt yatas jñānam vairāgyam ca tad anvitam aiśvaryam ca aṣṭadhā yasmāt yaśaḥ ca ātma mala apaham munīnām nyasta daṇḍānām śāntānām sama cetasām akiñcanānām sādhūnām yam āhuḥ paramām gatim sattvam yasya priyā mūrtiḥ brāhmaṇāḥ tu iṣṭa devatāḥ bhajanti an āśiṣaḥ śāntāḥ yam vā nipuṇa buddhayaḥ tri vidha ākṛtayaḥ tasya rākṣasāḥ asurāḥ surāḥ guṇinyā māyayā sṛṣṭāḥ sattvam tat tīrtha sādhanam śrī śukaḥ uvāca ittham sārasvatāḥ viprāḥ nṛṇām saṃśaya nuttaye puruṣasya pada ambhoja sevayā tad gatim gatāḥ śrī sūtaḥ uvāca pīyūṣam bhava bhaya bhid parasya puṃsaḥ su ślokam śravaṇa puṭaiḥ pibati abhīkṣṇam śrī śukaḥ uvāca ekadā dvāravatyām tu vipra patnyāḥ kumārakaḥ jāta mātraḥ bhuvam spṛṣṭvā mamāra kila bhārata vipraḥ gṛhītvā mṛtakam rāja dvāri upadhāya saḥ idam provāca vilapan āturaḥ dīna mānasaḥ brahma dviṣaḥ śaṭha dhiyaḥ lubdhasya viṣaya ātmanaḥ kṣatra bandhoḥ karma doṣāt pañcatvam me gataḥ arbhakaḥ hiṃsā vihāram nṛpatim duḥśīlam ajita indriyam prajāḥ bhajantyaḥ sīdanti daridrāḥ nitya duḥkhitāḥ evam dvitīyam viprarṣiḥ tṛtīyam tu evam eva ca visṛjya sa nṛpa dvāri tām gāthām samagāyata parete navame bāle brāhmaṇam samabhāṣata rājanya bandhuḥ ete vai brāhmaṇāḥ satram āsate dhana dāra ātmaja apṛktāḥ yatra śocanti brāhmaṇāḥ te vai rājanya veṣeṇa naṭāḥ jīvanti asum bharāḥ aham prajāḥ vām bhagavan rakṣiṣye dīnayoḥ iha anistīrṇa pratijñaḥ agnim pravekṣye hata kalmaṣaḥ śrī brāhmaṇaḥ uvāca saṅkarṣaṇaḥ vāsudevaḥ pradyumnaḥ dhanvinām varaḥ tat katham nu bhavān karma duṣkaram jagat īśvaraiḥ tvam cikīrṣasi bāliśyāt tat na śraddadhmahe vayam śrī arjunaḥ uvāca na aham saṅkarṣaṇaḥ brahman na kṛṣṇaḥ kārṣṇiḥ eva ca aham vai arjunaḥ nāma gāṇḍīvam yasya vai dhanuḥ mā avamaṃsthāḥ mama brahman vīryam tryambaka toṣaṇam jagāma sva gṛham prītaḥ pārtha vīryam niśāmayan prasūti kāle āsanne bhāryāyāḥ dvija sattamaḥ pāhi pāhi prajām mṛtyoḥ iti āha arjunam āturaḥ divyāni astrāṇi saṃsmṛtya sajyam gāṇḍīvam ādade nyaruṇat sūtikāgāram śaraiḥ nānā astra yojitaiḥ tiryak ūrdhvam adhas pārthaḥ cakāra śara pañjaram tatas kumāraḥ sañjātaḥ vipra patnyā rudan muhur sadyas adarśanam āpede sa śarīraḥ vihāyasā yasya śekuḥ paritrātum kaḥ anyaḥ tad avitā īśvaraḥ dhik arjunam mṛṣā vādam dhik ātma ślāghinaḥ dhanuḥ daiva upasṛṣṭam yaḥ mauḍhyāt āninīṣati durmatiḥ evam śapati viprarṣau vidyām āsthāya phālgunaḥ yayau saṃyamanīm āśu yatra āste bhagavān yamaḥ vipra apatyam acakṣāṇaḥ tatas aindrīm agāt purīm āgneyīm nairṛtīm saumyām vāyavyām vāruṇīm atha rasātalam nāka pṛṣṭham dhiṣṇyāni anyāni udāyudhaḥ agnim vivikṣuḥ kṛṣṇena pratyuktaḥ pratiṣedhatā darśaye dvija sūnūn te mā avajñā ātmānam ātmanā ye te naḥ kīrtim vimalām manuṣyāḥ sthāpayiṣyanti divyam sva ratham āsthāya pratīcīm diśam āviśat lokālokam tathā atītya viveśa su mahat tamaḥ tatra aśvāḥ śaibya sugrīva meghapuṣpa balāhakāḥ tān dṛṣṭvā bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ mahā yoga īśvara īśvaraḥ sahasra āditya saṅkāśam sva cakram prāhiṇot puras tamaḥ su ghoram gahanam kṛtam mahat vidārayat bhūri tareṇa rociṣā guṇa cyutaḥ rāma śaraḥ yathā camūḥ samaśnuvānam prasamīkṣya phālgunaḥ pratāḍita akṣaḥ pidadhe akṣiṇī ubhe tatas praviṣṭaḥ salilam nabhasvatā balīyasā ejat bṛhat ūrmi bhūṣaṇam sahasra mūrdhanya phaṇā maṇi dyubhiḥ vibhrājamānam dvi guṇa īkṣaṇa ulbaṇam sita acala ābham śiti kaṇṭha jihvam sāndra ambuda ābham su piśaṅga vāsasam mahā maṇi vrāta kirīṭa kuṇḍala śrīvatsa lakṣmam vana mālayā āvṛtam mahā maṇi vrāta kirīṭa kuṇḍala śrīvatsa lakṣmam vana mālayā āvṛtam vavande ātmānam anantam acyutaḥ jiṣṇuḥ ca tad darśana jāta sādhvasaḥ tau āha bhūmā parameṣṭhinām prabhuḥ beddhāñjalī sa smitam ūrjayā girā pūrṇa kāmau api yuvām nara nārāyaṇau ṛṣī iti ādiṣṭau bhagavatā tau kṛṣṇau parameṣṭhinā om iti ānamya bhūmānam ādāya dvija dārakān nyavartetām svakam dhāma samprahṛṣṭau yathā gatam viprāya dadatuḥ putrān yathā rūpam yathā vayaḥ niśāmya vaiṣṇavam dhāma pārthaḥ parama vismitaḥ yat kiñcid pauruṣam puṃsām mene kṛṣṇa anukampitam iti īdṛśāni anekāni vīryāṇi iha pradarśayan bubhuje viṣayān grāmyān īje ca ati urjitaiḥ makhaiḥ pravavarṣa akhilān kāmān prajāsu brāhmaṇa ādiṣu yathā kālam yathā eva indraḥ bhagavān śraiṣṭhyam āsthitaḥ hatvā nṛpān adharmiṣṭhān ghāṭayitvā arjuna ādibhiḥ añjasā vartayām āsa dharmam dharma suta ādibhiḥ śrī śukaḥ uvāca sukham sva puryām nivasan dvārakāyām śriyaḥ patiḥ sarva sampad samṛddhāyām juṣṭāyām vṛṣṇi puṃgavaiḥ kanduka ādibhiḥ harmyeṣu krīḍantībhiḥ taḍit dyubhiḥ nityam saṅkula mārgāyām mada cyudbhiḥ mataṃgajaiḥ udyāna upavana āḍhyāyām puṣpita druma rājiṣu nirviśat bhṛṅga vihagaiḥ nāditāyām samantataḥ reme ṣoḍaśa sāhasra patnīnām eka vallabhaḥ vijahāra vigāhya ambhaḥ hradinīṣu mahodayaḥ kuca kuṅkuma lipta aṅgaḥ parirabdhaḥ ca yoṣitām upagīyamānaḥ gandharvaiḥ mṛdaṅga paṇava ānakān vādayadbhiḥ mudā vīṇām sūta māgadha vandibhiḥ pratiṣiñcan vicikrīḍe yakṣībhiḥ yakṣa rāj iva tāḥ klinna vastra vivṛta ūru kuca pradeśāḥ siñcantyaḥ uddhṛta bṛhat kavara prasūnāḥ krīḍā abhiṣaṅga dhuta kuntala vṛnda bandhaḥ naṭānām nartakīnām ca gīta vādya upajīvinām krīḍā alaṅkāra vāsāṃsi kṛṣṇaḥ adāt tasya ca striyaḥ kṛṣṇasya evam viharataḥ gati ālāpa īkṣita smitaiḥ narma kṣveli pariṣvaṅgaiḥ strīṇām kila hṛtāḥ dhiyaḥ cintayantyaḥ aravinda akṣam tāni me gadataḥ śṛṇu mahiṣyaḥ ūcuḥ kurari vilapasi tvam vīta nidrā na śeṣe tvam roravīṣi karuṇam bata cakravāki dāsyam gata vayam iva acyuta pāda juṣṭām kim vā srajam spṛhayase kavareṇa voḍhum kim vā mukunda apahṛta ātma lāñchanaḥ prāptām daśām tvam ca gataḥ duratyayām tvam yakṣmaṇā balavatā asi gṛhītaḥ indo kṣīṇaḥ tamaḥ na nija dīdhitibhiḥ kṣiṇoṣi govinda apāṅga nirbhinne hṛdi īrayasi naḥ smaram śrīvatsa aṅkam vayam iva bhavān dhyāyati prema baddhaḥ ati utkaṇṭhaḥ śavala hṛdayaḥ asmadvidhaḥ bāṣpa dhārāḥ smṛtvā smṛtvā visṛjasi muhur duḥkha daḥ tad prasaṅgaḥ priya rāva padāni bhāṣase mṛta sañjīvikayā anayā girā śuṣyat hradāḥ karaśitāḥ bata sindhu patnyaḥ a prāpya muṣṭa hṛdayāḥ puru karśitāḥ sma haṃsa svāgatam āsyatām piba payaḥ brūhi aṅga śaureḥ kathām dūtam tvām nu vidāma kaccit ajitaḥ svasti āste uktam purā kim vā naḥ cala sauhṛdaḥ smarati tam kasmāt bhajāmaḥ vayam kṣaudra ālāpaya kāma dam śriyam ṛte sā eva eka niṣṭhā striyām śrī śukaḥ uvāca iti īdṛśena bhāvena kṛṣṇe yogeśvara īśvare śruta mātraḥ api yaḥ strīṇām prasahya ākarṣate manaḥ uru gāya uru gītaḥ vā paśyantīnām ca kim punar yāḥ samparyacaran premṇā pāda saṃvāhana ādibhiḥ jagat gurum bhartṛ buddhyā tāsām kim varṇyate tapaḥ evam veda uditam dharmam anutiṣṭhan satām gatiḥ gṛham dharma artha kāmānām muhur ca adarśayat padam āsthitasya param dharmam kṛṣṇasya gṛha medhinām āsan ṣoḍaśa sāhasram mahiṣyaḥ ca śata adhikam tāsām strī ratna bhūtānām aṣṭau yāḥ prāk udāhṛtāḥ rukmiṇī pramukhāḥ rājan tad putrāḥ ca anupūrvaśas ekaikasyām daśa daśa kṛṣṇaḥ ajījanat ātmajān yāvatyaḥ ātmanaḥ bhāryāḥ amogha gatiḥ īśvaraḥ teṣām uddāma vīryāṇām aṣṭādaśa mahā rathāḥ āsan udāra yaśasaḥ teṣām nāmāni me śṛṇu sāmbaḥ madhuḥ bṛhadbhānuḥ citrabhānuḥ vṛkaḥ aruṇaḥ puṣkaraḥ vedabāhuḥ ca śrutadevaḥ sunandanaḥ eteṣām api rāja indra tanu jānām madhu dviṣaḥ pradyumnaḥ āsīt prathamaḥ pitṛ vat rukmiṇī sutaḥ tasyām tatas aniruddhaḥ abhūt nāga āyata bala anvitaḥ sa ca api rukmiṇaḥ pautrīm dauhitraḥ jagṛhe tatas vajraḥ tasya abhavat yaḥ tu mauṣalāt avaśeṣitaḥ subāhoḥ śāntasenaḥ abhūt śatasenaḥ tu tad sutaḥ alpa āyuṣaḥ alpa vīryāḥ ca abrahmaṇyāḥ ca jajñire yadu vaṃśa prasūtānām puṃsām vikhyāta karmaṇām saṅkhyā na śakyate kartum api varṣa ayutaiḥ nṛpa tisraḥ koṭyaḥ sahasrāṇām aṣṭāśīti śatāni ca āsan yadu kula ācāryāḥ kumārāṇām iti śrutam saṅkhyānam yādavānām kaḥ kariṣyati mahātmanām yatra ayutānām ayuta lakṣeṇa āste saḥ āhukaḥ deva asura āhava hatāḥ daiteyāḥ ye su dāruṇāḥ te ca utpannāḥ manuṣyeṣu prajāḥ dṛptāḥ babādhire tad nigrahāya hariṇā proktāḥ devāḥ yadoḥ kule avatīrṇāḥ kula śatam teṣām eka adhikam nṛpa teṣām pramāṇam bhagavant prabhu tvena abhavat hariḥ ye ca anuvartinaḥ tasya vavṛdhuḥ sarva yādavāḥ śayyā āsana aṭana ālāpa krīḍā snāna ādi karmasu na viduḥ santam ātmānam vṛṣṇayaḥ kṛṣṇa cetasaḥ tīrtham cakre nṛpa ūnam yat ajani yaduṣu svaḥsarit pāda śaucam kṛṣṇasya etat na citram kṣiti bhara haraṇam kāla cakrāyudhasya līlā tanoḥ tad anurūpa viḍambanāni karmāṇi karma kaṣaṇāni yadu uttamasya śrīmat kathā śravaṇa kīrtana cintayā eti grāmāt vanam kṣiti bhujaḥ api yayuḥ yad arthāḥ
